[A:i-1]@/ /gleng brjod/! 'das pa'i lo shas sngon nas gong dkar chos sde'i bla ma rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal (1432-96) gyi gsung par bskrun bya rgyu'i 'char gzhi yod/
de rjes phyi lo 2001 lor khong gi rnam thar (ngo mtshar rin po che'i gter mdzod )par bskrun byas nas gom pa dang po de chags yod/ spyir btang bla ma rdo rje gdan pa rang
gi gsungs pa sa skya rdzong lugs kyi skor da lta yod pa'i yig cha dkon po yin dus de ni yid skyo dgos pa'i gnas tshul zhig los yin/ skabs 'di bla ma de'i gsung gi nang
las cha shas zhig yin na yang gsan yig 'dir bla ma de'i dmigs gsal mdzad 'phrin dang / bod nang gi rdo rje theg pa'i bstan pa brgyud pa'i lo rgyus gsal po byas nas bstan
yod dus deb 'dir dmigs gsal khyad chos ma 'dra ba zhig yod//rdzong lugs ni bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan (1312-75) gyi slob ma nas brgyud pa zhig red/ 'jam mgon a
mes zhabs kyis gsungs pa ltar na/ de la snga rabs dang / phyi rabs gnyis su dbye dgos par gsungs/ bla ma dam par gsung ngag 'dzin pa'i thugs sras brgyad yod pa'i nang rdzong
chung ba sngags 'chang gzungs gyi dpal ba dang / ngor lugs srol 'byed pa po bla ma dpal ldan tshul khrims 1333-99 gnyis yang yin/ rdzong chung ba bzhugs sa sa skya rdzong
chung bla brang yin dus mtshan yang 'di ltar chags/ khong nas brgyud pa'i lam 'bras skor de snga rabs pa yin la/ de nas chos rje bzang po rgyal mtshan dang / rgyal
mtshan dkon mchog brgyud nas mus srad pa byams pa rdo rje

[A:i-2]rgyal mtshan (1424-98) bar brgyud nas mus srad pas rdzong lugs snga rabs kyi skor gtsang phyogs la khyab spel gnang / phyi rabs ni/ bla ma dam pa sku tshe smad skabs
kyi slob ma theg chen chos rgyal kun dga' bkra shis (1349-1425) nas brgyud pa yin la theg chen lugs yang zer/ khong gi slob ma gtso bo rdzong pa kun dga' rgyal mtshan (1382-1436)
dang brag thog pa bsod nams bzang po gnyis yin/ rdzong pas bstan pa la stod byang du khyab spel gnang / brag thog pas dbus kyi gong dkar rdzong dang nye bar gnas
chu bo ri la gdan sa chags btab/ skabs de dus gong dkar gyi rdzong dpon mtshan rgyal ba shes rab ni thon gyi mi rabs nas brgyud pa red/ rdzong dpon rgyal ba shes rab kyi
sras rdo rje gdan pa yin la/ rdo rje gdan pa khong ni dgung lo bco lnga lon rjes yab kyi sku tshab tu rdzong dpon gnang rung / srid las chos la 'dun pa che bar yod stabs
dgung lo nyer bdun la bsnyen par rdzogs te mtshan kun dga' rnam rgyal zhes gsol/ rigs brgyud thon yin stabs thon btsun du yang gsol/ lo drug gi rjes la gong dkar chos sde
chags btab/ brag thog pa ni khong gi rtsa bla yin par theg chen chos rgyal nas brgyud pa'i rdzong lugs phyi rabs pa'i chos rnams gsan/ gzhan yang bu ston rin po che'i
rgyud kyi man ngag brgyud pa shar pa ye shes rgya mtsho (1404-73) dang / khong rang dang rus brgyud gcig pa paN chen byams pa gling pa bsod nams rnam rgyal (1401-75) las
dus 'khor sogs gsan pas de gnyis khyad par gyi bla mar gyur/ khong gi sku tshe'i nang spyir sa skya dang yang dgos ris med kyi rdo rje theg par mkhas pas phul du gyur//da
lam gsan yig 'dir gzhig na khong ni thos rgya chen po zhig yin par mngon thub la/ da

[A:i-3]dung khong rang gi rnam thar dang gzhig na gsan yig 'di cha lag tshang ba ma yin pa mngon gsal red/ gang lags zhu na rnam thar nang du khong rang nas brtsam pa'i gsan
yig nang bla ma rer mchod brjod snyan dngags tshig bcad re bkod yod tshul gsal kyang gsan yig 'dir de rnams mi gsal/ yang dgos paN chen nags kyi rin chen/(1384-1468) kun
mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel (1411-85) dang / shar pa ye shes rgya mtsho'i rtsa bla yin zer ba'i rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan gsum las gsan pa mngon rung gsan yig 'dir
ma tshang ngo //gsan yig de dang lhan du bkod rgyur/ sa skya gong ma la phul ba'i 'phrin yig rtsod bzlog dang / lam 'bras lag len mkho ba'i dri lan gnyis/ zhal gdams khag
gnyis bcas bkod yod/ spyir btang deb 'dir ma yig gzhir gzhag las bzo bcos byas med la skabs re yig nor phran bu 'dug pa de rnams bzo bcos byas yod pas der rtags rgyab yod/
gzhan yang rnam thar rtsom pa po rgya ston byang chub dbang rgyal gyis ngor chen dkon mchog lhun grub la lam 'bras kyi skor rtsod lan gcig kha skong gi tshul du bkod yod/
'di ni bla ma rdo rje gdan pa sku gshegs nas lo bzhi bcu zhe gsum song rjes brtsams pa'o/ /don gnyer pa rnams la phan rer dmigs nas rnam par thar pa ngo mtshar rin po
che'i gter mdzod nang 'khod pa'i gsung rtsom tho yig yang bkod yod/ /rgyal yongs sa chen zhes pa las spyi lo 2005 zla ba 7 tshes 21 mchod rten rin po che gtsos thugs rten
mang dag mkha' dbyings su dad ldan tshogs la zhal mjal ston pa'i dus khyad nyin dad 'dun rtse gcig gis par rtsa zhus pa'i dge bas 'brel tshad rten bzang thob pa'i rgyu
ru bsngo'o// //

snyan brgyud nyams khrid/ bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i spyod 'jug gi TIkka lung /328cha) sgrub thabs rgya mtsho thob yig/330ja) jo bo'i chos 'byung brgya rtsa'i thob yig/338nya)
mi tra brgya rtsa la sogs pa'i thob yig/344

bi la sa badzra/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ intra bho ti/ lcam lakShmi ka ra/ nag po spyod pa/ bram ze dpal 'dzin/ ga ya dha ra man chad lam 'bras dang
'dra ba ni/ mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i kye rdo rje'i sgrub thabs dang / de'i rdzogs rim gyi man ngag padma ba'i lam bsnyen bsgrub bzhi zab pa'i tshul dgus bskyed pa

mdzad pa/DoM bhi he ru ka'i lam lhan cig skyes grub kyi brgyud pa ni/ badzra dha ra sya/ DA ki Ni/ DoM bhi ba/ a la la badzra/ ba na si pa/ garbha ri pa/ shrI pendha pa/ surYa
tsaNDa/ bi ra badzra/ rje 'brog rje se/ rje zhang / rje sa skya pa man chad lam 'bras dang 'dra ba ni lhan cig skyes grub kyi rgyud pa'o/ /yang / de ltar rnal 'byor dbang
phyug gis kyai rdor rgyud gsum/ gdan bzhi/ mA yA sogs la rten nas/ rdo rje bdag med ma'i gsung bzhin lam 'bras bu dang bcas pa'i gdams ngag mdzad pa/ bla chen gyis shar
phyogs nags su dge slong dpa' bo rdo rje dang / bod du gA ya dha ra las padma ba'i lam/ mchod rten drung thob/ gtum mo lam rdzogs/ yon po srang ba/ bsam mi khyab dang
bcas pa gsan/ yi ge med pa'i gdams ngag a mo gha badzra la bod du dang / intra bhU ti'i lam dang / lhan cig skyes grub gnyis/ paNDi ta dang shes rab gsang ba las bod du
gsan nas mdzad pa po brgyad kyis mdzad pa'i chos tshan dgu la lam bskor dgur grags pa rnams thob bo//yang / snyigs dus kyi 'gro ba mtha' dag gi 'dren mchog rje btsun sa skya
pa yab sras lnga'i gsung 'bum yongs su rdzogs pa'i lung rnams ma tshang ba med par zhus pa ni/ yab sras lnga po las/ chos rje 'phags pas rin chen sgang bla brang du gsungs

nag po pa'i mngon rtogs/ nag po pa'i

dkyil chog nag po pa'i dbang gi sdoms/ nag po pa'i mchod 'phreng / lha mo bcu drug gi mchod pa gnyis/ bde mchog gi bstod pa'i rab byed ston shes bskul ba/ sgo 'tshams ma rnams
la bstod cing bskul ba/ nag po pa'i sbyin bsreg gi don rgyas par bshad pa/ nag po pa'i sbyin bsreg gi sdoms/ bde mchog lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs yan lag bcu bzhi pa/
bde mchog lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs bsdus pa/ kha che rin chen rdo rje'i bkra shis kyi kha bskong dang bcas pa'i bkra shis gnyis/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i sbyin bsreg nA ro

pa/ sgrol ma lha bcu bdun gyi sgrub thabs/ sgrol ma'i dbang chog sgrol ma'i lus dkyil bsgom pa'i rim pa/ rdo rje sgrol ma'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa/ 'jigs pa brgyad skyobs

thabs/ yang tshe dpag med kyi sgrub thabs/ tshe dpag med kyi bstod pa/ snang ba mtha' yas kyi nyal sgom dang / thugs rje chen po dang phyag rgya chen po zung 'jug tu nyams
su len pa'i tshul/ thugs rje chen po phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs/ seng ge sgra'i sgrub thabs/ a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs/ 'jam dbyangs dkar po'i sgrub thabs/ mi 'khrug
pa'i sbyin bsreg phyag na rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ rnam 'joms sgrub thabs/ mi g.yo ba sngon po'i sgrub thabs/ mi g.yo ba phyag bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs/ rta mgrin khyung gshog

tshul rnams so// ! //(Dha)pa la/ skyabs 'gro sems bskyed bsngo ba dang bcas pa/ sems bskyed cho ga sems bskyed skyabs 'gro dang bcas pa/ skyabs 'gro sems bskyed bsngo ba
dang bcas pa bsdus pa/ sems bskyed skyabs 'gro dang bcas pa/ skyabs 'gro bo lod ma/ skyabs 'gro a rog chen mo/ theg chen gsal ba zhes bya ba'i yi ge'i ma mo la spel ba/ theg

/ snying po'i sdoms/ thabs la mkhas pa'i sdoms/ ting nge 'dzin gyi sdoms/ sangs rgyas kyi sa'i sdoms/ byang chub sems dpa'i sdoms/ rgyud bla'i bsdus don/ theg pa'i rnam dbye/

pa/ bka' nyan pho mo gser gyi spu gri can zhes bya ba'i man ngag gnod sbyin pho mo dang / gshin rje pho mo'i tshul du bsgrub pa'i man ngag sa chen pas mdzad pa/ dam shing
la dbang bskur ba/ rbod rbad gsad gsum gcig tu sgril ba dang so sor spel ba/ sa chen pas mdzad pa/ bka' nyan spu gri can gyi sgrub thabs bsnyen sgrub gsad gsum lo rgyus
zhal gdams dang bcas pa'i gsal byed dam pas sbyar ba/ 'di'i rtsa ba tshigs bcad ma gter nas phyung ba/ yang / mon pa lcam sring gi sgrub thabs/ dkyil 'khor la ltos pa
dang ma ltos pa'i tshul/ dpal brtse ba chen po'i zhal gyi man ngag dam pas don tig gsal bar bkod pa/ 'di rnams kyi rgyud pa'i rim pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang / bram
ze mchog sred/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shrAddha ka ra warmma/ lo tsA ba chen po/ brag stengs pa/ mal lo tsA/ dpal brtse ba chen po'i zhabs/ yang / 'phags mchog klu sgrub/ padma
badzra/ dharmma pA la/ brag stengs pa/ 'brom jo sras/ dpal brtse ba chen po/ slob dpon bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa paN/ chos rgyal
'phags pa/ dam pa kun dga' grags/ bla ma kun bsod pa/ dpal ldan seng ge chos rje bla ma/ seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen rgyal mchog pa/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/
/yang / sa chen/ rta rtas so pa/ gan pa ston dar nas rim par rgyud pa'o/ /yang / nag po chen po'i man ngag snyan nas snyan du rgyud pa/ rtsa gsum la rten pa'i bsnyen bsgrub
las sbyor/ chos rje dpal ldan bla ma'i gsung bzhin bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan pas

sgrigs pa/ nag po chen po'i mdos bla ma shes rab 'byung gnas kyis mdzad pa/ yang / thugs dam mdos kyis bskang ba/ bla ma spyan chen pos mdzad pa rnams so/ /chos skyong gong
'og gi bstod 'bum ngag dbang grags pas sgrigs pa/ bla ma de nyid/ dpal ldan legs dbang / pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /nag po lha gsum dang / lha brgyad la rten pa'i
bsgrub skor pu tra lcam dral gyi dgos sgrub dang bcas par gda'o/ /yang nag po lha gsum ma'i bsnyen bsgrub las sbyor 'gro mgon 'phags pas mdzad pa'ang zhus so/ /yang / nag
po chen po zhal bzhi pa'i rtsegs zhal lo/ rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ gnyan lo tsA ba/ kha'u pa/ sa skya pa chen
po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa/ bla chen rong pa/ bla ma shes rab seng ge bla ma bsod nams lhun grub/ bla ma ngag gi dbang phyug
bla ma dpal ldan legs dbang / pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / gnyan gyi mgon po g.yas dkar g.yon dmar steng zhal dud kha lcam dral lnga'i rjes gnang gi brgyud
pa ni/ 'phags pa yan sngar dang 'dra ba la/ tshogs sgom pa/ nyan chen pa/ nam bza' pa bsod nams dpal/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ bzhi thog pa kun rin/ gcung grags pa blo
gros/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ pha chos kyi rje des bdag la'o/ /yang / zhal bzhi gtso 'khor drug pa dang / gdong gnyan bzhi pa dang / dkar po tshe sgrub/ ser po bsod nams
bsgrub pa/ dmar po dbang bsdud/ sngon po bgegs 'joms te drug gi rjes gnang so sor yod pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'phags pa yan sngar lta bu la/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/
bla ma dpal ldan seng ge chos rje dharmma

kirti/ chos rje blo bzangs/ nya dbon kun dga'/ lung rig rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o// //yang / par pu'i cho ga'i lung gi brgyud pa
ni/ gnam kha'u pa/ slob dpon/ go tsha/ dam pa de skyes/ gru rdor seng / bcom ral/ skyi ston/ kun mkhyen chen po/ nya dbon/ lung rig pa/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos
kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /de dag gi yig cha'i rim pa la/ rtsegs zhal gnyis ma'i las tshogs/ chos 'phrul 'gyed pa/ DA ki ma bzhi'i than 'gyed/ yum srin mo'i dgos sgrub/ nor
sgrub kyi cho ga byin brlabs kyi yi ge dang bcas pa/ dkar ser nag dmar bzhi'i mngon rtogs rdo nag yig dmar gyi man ngag yang / lingga bca' thabs/ nag po chen po'i dug gi
spu gri'i nang nas bsdus pa srog gi spu gri'i man ngag drag po 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs gsang ba srog gi spu gri/ rdo 'bigs srog gi dmar len/ gdong bzhi pa'i sgrub thabs
gsang ba srog gi man ngag dgra mkhar brtsad nas bshig pa/ bsgrub bya gnas nas phyung ba rnams kyi brgyud pa/ gnyan lo/ gshong ma'i sngags ban ge rad/ rtogs ldan mtsho
dkar/ 'dis dgung lo mang po thub pas sku tshe'i bstod la sngags ban dang mjal/ smad spyan mnga' 'di dang mjal te/ spyan mnga' bsod grags pa/ rin po che 'tshal min pa/ rin
po che seng ge dpal ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i gzhung tshigs bcad ma/ 'di nas bzlas pa/ bsnyen rtags/ 'brub khung du
gsad pa/ 'dze btang ba/ rabs bcad pa/ zhing spel bya ba/ rims gtang ba/ grong khyer dkrug pa/ gnad nas skrad pa/ dbang du bya ba/ smyo bar bya ba/ sbyin sreg bya ba/ 'dod

don spel ba rnams/ 'bum phrag gsum pa las rgyud de gnyan lo tsA bas bsgyur 'di'i bar dpe ma byung bas med thal/ ba/ spobs pa'i zhal shes sa chen gyi man ngag bla ma gnyan la
dbus phrug phur pa dar gyis zhus pa'i sgrub yig gtor ltas dang bcas pa/ gtor ma dang kha sbyar dbye ba'i dus kyi 'bod bskul/ bsnyen bsgrub gsad gsum gyi las sgrigs chen
mo/ lta ba'i gdeng 'dzugs/ ma nyams par bsrung rgyu'i dam tshig mthun pa'i rdzas brten tshul/ ma nor ba'i sngags bzla tshul/ 'khu ldog spang ba'i snying chu bsre ba/ las
ma nyan na gnad la 'bebs pa/ mgon po pha ltar skur ba'i gdams ngag gnyis pa bya zhes pa'i man ngag spos sbyor/ gtor ma dang / 'khor lo'i rtsibs la sngags bkod tshul/ paNDi
ta ta thA ga ta rakShi ta dang mjal tshul/ yang bsnyen bsgrub las sbyor snga ma dang mi gcig pa'i che ba gcig zhal bzhi pa'i dngos grub kyi dam tshig sgrub pa'i thabs
rakShi tas mdzad pa gnyan gyis bsgyur ba/ yang rten gsum 'dzugs thabs dus gtor dang bcas pa/ yang ba dan la rten nas spyan drangs thabs/ glo bur du las 'chol ba'i gtor ma
'bul thabs/ rten bshams nas 'bul ba'i tshul/ bying rgod bsal ba dang 'jam rtsub skabs dang sbyor tshul/ ma chun na bcun pa'i thabs/ bdag skyed ye shes mgon po bka' nyan
'jig rten pa'i mgon por bya ba/ lha mo nag mo'i zhal gdams/ 'bum phrag gsum pa las rgyud pa'i mgon po gdong gnyan can gyi sgrub tshul/ gnod pa bsrung zhing bar chad bzlog
pa'i 'khor lo ling tse nyi shu bri thabs/ mgon po'i gtor chen bya tshul/ las mthar sbyin bsreg bya ba/ gsang ba bya ba/ nyams chag che na gtor skyongs bya ba/ yang nyams
chag yig brgyas bkang tshul/ chos skyong la gtsug lag gtod pa'i tshul/ gnas

dang / mal cha/ nor rdzas bsrung ba/ mgon po rtag pa'i spos sbyor/ mchod pa'i spos sbyor/ khams gsum dbang bsdus kyi las/ mi nor dbang du bya ba yid bzhin nor bu'i man ngag
'khon nag zas su za ba/ ma hA ba las 'dre mnan pa/ sri'u gso ba/ mngal bsrung ba/ bu 'tshol ba/ sri'u gso thabs gnyis pa/ chung sri 'dul ba/ dur khrod du gsad pa'i las sbyor/
mdze btang ba/ rabs bcad pa/ zhing sel/ rims btang / grong khyer dkrug bskrad pa bya/ dbang du bsdu/ sgong zor gyi las/ gtum po'i sha bzlog khyung zor gyi las/ bskrad
las mthar thug rdzas la rten nas bsgrub bya dbang du bya ba/ gsang sngags ring thung spel tshig bya thabs/ dgra la ltas ngan btang ba/ bsreg pa yungs kar gyi las rnams
so// //yang / lo rgyus rjes gnang gi yi ge seng rgyal bas mdzad pa/ gtor chen dang dus gtor gyi yi ge lha mchog ma hA ka la zhes pa'i spyan 'dren/ bskang gso khyed mthun
ma/ mchod pa dur khrod gnas brgyad ma/ bstod pa rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ gnyan los mdzad pa'i pad nyid ro stengs ma/ mi rtog dbyings nas zhes pa'i bstod pa/ kha'u pas

rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ padma badzra/ shrI badzra ra hU la/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ dznyA na siddhi/ dpal dam tshig rdo rje/ 'chi med blo gros bzang po/ bai ro tsa na/ rgwa lo

/ 'khor mang po smin cing grol bar mdzad nas/ sprul pa'i rgyal po zla ba bzang pos bsdus te shambha lar shAkya'i rigs kyi rgyal po rnams dang / rigs ldan gyi rgyal po

pa rin chen rgyal mtshan pa/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / chos rje sa paN la/ rin po che skyob pa dpal/ rgyal tsha chos dbang / lo mchog lo chen/ bla ma ye
shes mgon/ bla ma dar ma bzang po/ grags chen pa/ spang khang pa/ slob dpon rin chen brtson/ chos rje byang seng pa/ bkras rin pa/ de gnyis ka la/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/
pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ dha byang chub sems dpa'/ a bhya ka ra/ ratna rakShi
ta/ dza ya se na/ sum lo dar ma yon tan/ mkhas pa sa mu tra/ seng ge rgyal mtshan/ lo tsA ba grags rgyal/ dpal mchog rgya thams cad mkhyen pa/ srin po ri pa/ sgrag ston rdo
rje dpal/ 'tshur phu ba tshul rin/ chos rje rang byung rdo rje/ yor pa ye shes dpal/ mkhan

chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / rang byung pa la/ snye mdo kun dga' don grub/ bla ma bsod nams 'od zer/ bla ma bag ston/ bla ma tshul rgyal/ bla
ma bde legs pa/ de la rin po che bsod bzang pa dang / gnas rnying mkhan chen rin chen rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis gsan/ de gnyis ka la mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ pha chos kyi
rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho'i brgyud srol gcig la/ sa paN/ nyan chen pa/ dpal ldan seng ge byang seng pa/ lung rigs rgya mtsho/ mkhan chen seng ge
dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i yig cha'i rim pa la/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rin po che dbang gi rgyal po'i mdzod/ sgrub thabs rgyas pa rin po che pad ma rwa
ga'i gter/ sbyin bsreg gi cho ga rin po che me shel/ gtor ma'i cho ga rin po che aShma garbha/ maNDal gyi cho ga rin po che margad rnams te/ rin po che rnam pa lnga/ paNDi
ta dza ya se nas mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan gsang mtshan ye shes rdo rjer grags pas bsgyur ba dang / rkang pa bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad pa/ lo tsA ba des bod skad
du bsgyur ba'i lung yang thob bo/ /yang / 'khor lo bde mchog gi rtsa ba'i rgyud/ le'u lnga bcu nga gcig pa/ pad ma ka ra dang / lo chen gyis bsgyur ba mar do dang / pradznya
kirtis bcos pa'i steng du bu ston pas zhus dag mdzad pa/ mkha' 'gro ma kun spyod kyi rgyud/ bde mchog gi chos 'byung / rtsa rgyud kyi 'grel tig rgyas pa/ kun spyod kyi
TI ka bde mchog don gsal/ bde mchog lU hi pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga de kho na nyid gsal ba/ mngon par rtogs pa rnal 'byor bzhi ldan/ sbyin sreg gi cho ga 'phrin las
kun 'grub/ mchod phreng rgyas pa/ nyer spyod lnga dang / rigs ma bcu drug gi gar yig bde mchog nag po pa'i

mngon rtogs kyi dka' 'grel rnams mkhyen rabs dbang phyug bu ston chos rjes mdzad pa/ yang / slob dpon bhu 'u ri pas mdzad pa'i rgyun bshags/ dpal chos kyi grags pas mdzad pa'i
bstod pa rgyun chags yi ge stong sum brgya bzhi cu rtsa bzhi pa chag lo'i 'gyur/ bram ze rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa'i bstod pa mar do'i 'gyur/ kha che rin chen rdo rjes
mdzad pa'i bkra shis lo chen gyi 'gyur/ chos rje bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i dril bu lus dkyil gyi mngon rtogs/ dril bu lha lnga'i mngon dkyil/ mkhan chen rin chen rnam
rgyal gyi mdzad pa/ yang / bde mchog sdom 'byung gi cho ga rgyas pa dri ma med pa'i chu rgyun ces bya ba dang / sgrub thabs dngos grub rin po che'i gter ces bya ba/ bu ston
chos rjes mdzad pa/ yang / bde mchog lU hi pa'i mngon rtogs chos rje bla ma dam pas mdzad pa/ de'i dkyil chog theg chen chos rjes mdzad pa/ yang / bshad rgyud/ mngon brjod
phyi ma las byung ba/ bde mchog khro bo reg tshig gi dbang dang / lung bu ston pas mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas zhus pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ slob
dpon arYA de ba/ ratna saM gi ti/ buddha saM gi ti/ pad ma saM gi ti/ ba ri lo tsA/ dge bshes dbus pa/ mnga' ris kyi ston/ jo bo stag bzang / nag tsho rig 'dzin/ bud sgang
pa/ nag tsho shes rab rgyal mtshan/ gnyos dharmma rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon 'brog ston pa/ bla ma dgon 'og pa/ slob dpon bsod dbang / lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan
seng ge thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / khro bo reg tshig gi yab bka'/ yum bka'/ sbags sgrub/ gsang
sgrub/ las mkhan khrag mig mon pa spun gsum dang bcas pa'i dbang / byin

rlabs/ rjes gnang rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ arYA de ba/ ratna saM gI ti/ padma saM gI ti/ buddha saM gI ti/ ba ri lo tstsha ba/ dge bshes dbus
pa/ rgya lcags ri ba/ mnga' ris kyi ston/ jo bo stag bzang / nag tsho rigs 'dzin grags/ bud sgang pa/ nag tsho sher rgyal/ dar ma rgyal mtshan/ gron gyi slob dpon/ 'brog
ston/ gcung bsod dbang / lha rje dpags shi/ chos rgyal/ bsod rgyal/ bsod nams 'od zer/ bag ston tshul rgyal/ bde legs dpal/ chos rje tshal min pa/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/
pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i yig cha arYa de bas mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs tshigs bcad ma/ rdo rje gdan pa dang / ba ri'i 'gyur/ reg 'bigs sgrub thabs tshigs
bcad rkang pa bcu gcig pa/ rkang 'jog dbang chog gi tshigs bcad ma/ yang dbang gi cho ga nag tsho shes rgyal gyis mdzad pa/ reg tshig dam tshig gsang ba'i sgrub thabs/ arYA
de bas mdzad pa/ rdo rje gdan pa dang / ba ri'i 'gyur/ sbyin bsreg byang chub seng ges bris pa/ gtor chog tshigs bcad zhe drug pa dang / lha chen gsum gyi sgrub thabs/
bsnyen pa rdzogs pa'i bla ma yis/ /bsrung ba'i 'khor lo legs bris la/ /zhes pa nas/ kho rang gshed mas bskor bar bya/ /zhes pa'i bar dang / sngags bzlog drag po'i man ngag
ces pa rnams arYa de bas mdzad pa/ dbang chog ma bu tshang ma bag ston gyis stag sde bkra shis sbug tu sbyar ba/ rta dbyangs brtul ba'i lo rgyus ba ri bas gang la bstan
pa dang spel ba'i lo rgyus/ bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs dang / reg tshig ma bstod pa gnyis byang seng gis mdzad pa/ bsrung ba don bdun pa la/ bsnyen pa/ gtor ma/ sbyin
bsreg mnan pa/ bzlog pa/ 'khrul 'khor gyi

bsrung ba rnams so/ /sngags kyi them yig dang sngags don/ yang chu'i bsrung ba/ bsrung 'khor/ phyir bzlog 'khor lo/ dgra gsad pa/ mnan pa ste gdams ngag lnga/ reg tshig gi
lung blang ba nag tsho sher rgyal gyis byas pa/ yang bsrung 'khor dpung pa g.yon la 'dogs pa/ mnan gtad sbags pa'i las brgyad/ 'jigs rnam dgu'i zhal shes/ rta dbyangs kyis
'phags pa lha la phul ba'i/ me reg tshig gi lo rgyus dang man ngag reg tshig sngags bdag gi sgrub thabs/ las mkhan dgos bsgrub kyi gtor ma/ las mkhan khrag mig gi man ngag
snyan nas snyan du brgyud pa/ mon pa spun gsum gyi sgrub thabs/ reg tshig las mkhan dgos sgrub la/ zhes sogs chig brgyud ma/ bdud nag po khrag mig can sgrub pa/ las mkhan
nag po ngan sngags kyi sgrub pa/ spyi'i mngon rtogs yid kyi mun sel 'brog ston gyis sbyar ba/ mngon rtogs dang dbang gi zin bris gnyis rnams kyi lung yang zhus so/ /yang
/ ma hA mA ya sgyu ma chen po lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba/ chos rgyal 'phags pa'i yig cha'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi
mkha' 'gro ma/ ku ku ri pa/ mtsho skyes rdo rje/ DoM bhi he ru ka ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ zhi ba bzang po/ mar pa lo tsA/ rngog chos rdor/ zhe sdang rdo rje/ rngog chos sku/
rngog tsha dkon mchog dpal/ klog kya dbang phyug grags/ bla ma ldong / 'gro mgon 'phags pa las brgyud de/ zhang ston/ lo mchog kyi ston grags rgyal/ pradznya kirti/ mkhan
chen byang chub seng ge theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o// ! //bde ral bskor/ yang / rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud/ bde chen ral pa gcig pa/ lha nyi
shu rtsa lnga'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba yongs su rdzogs pa thob

pa'i yig cha'i rim pa la/ dbang gi cho ga'i sngon du 'gro ba sogs/ cho ga bdun gsum nyi shu rtsa gcig de dag gi gnad rgyas par ston pa'i cho ga lnga gsum bco lnga dang bcas
pas/ thun mong du bum dbang bcu gcig rgyas par bskur ba'i tshul/ bcu gnyis pa thun mong ma yin pa'i bum dbang / rdo rje slob dpon bdag po'i dbang / dbang gong ma gzhan lus
shes ldan lam gyi dbang gsum/ de dag re re la'ang gsang dbang gi bum dbang sogs bzhi bzhir phye nas bskur ba'i tshul/ rnal 'byor dbang phyug shrI dza ga ta mi tra a nanta'i
zhal gdams mthar thug dbang bskur ba de dag 'brel ba'i bskyed pa'i rim pa dang / gtso bor rdzogs rim ston pa'i gzhung rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i zhal nas dngos su gsungs
pa rdo rje sbas pa'i gsang lam/ paNDi ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba snubs mi bskyod rdo rje'i 'gyur/ mngon rtogs yab yum lhan skyes dang / nyi shu rtsa lnga'i sgrub thabs rgyas
pa/ paNDi ta'i gsung bzhin lo tsA bas bkod pa/ lha bcu bdun gyi sgrub thabs slob dpon mi pham sbas pas bsdus pa/ shrI mi tra dang / snubs lo'i 'gyur/ ral gcig gi rnal
'byor gyi cho ga rnam gsum/ rdzogs rim gyi skor la/ gzhan lus shes ldan la/ rmongs pa spang ba'i don du snga khrid kyi rim pa ni/ byang sems kyi dkar khrid/ 'og sgo bde
chen gyi lam la/ tshan pa lnga'i nyams myong dga' ba bzhi'i khrid/ lcags kyu'i 'dul khrid/ ting nge 'dzin gyi rtsal khrid/ sgra gcan gyi gza' khrid rnams so/ /yang / ye
shes 'pho ba'i byin brlabs kyi cho ga rang lus thabs ldan gyi gdams pa de kho na nyid rdo rje sbas pa'i gsang lam/ sngon 'gro/ dngos gzhi/ rjes gsum gyi dngos gzhi la/ rtsa
rlung thig le man ngag gsum dang / sems la gtso bor rten pa'i man ngag rang dbang rang gis sgyur

ba/ 'khor los bsgyur ba'i rgyal po lta bu dang / lus la gtso bor rten pa'i man ngag rten 'brel thabs kyi yan lag gis lam du slongs pa shing rta'i 'khrul 'khor lta bu sogs rdo
rje sbas pa'i gsang lam gyi don 'grel/ de'i bsdus don dang bcas pa rlung yi ge ris kyi rang bzhin gyi rtsa sbyang pa/ 'thug 'phrad thog 'gel gyi man ngag gis byed dgu
chos su btang ba/ khams dwangs snyigs gnyis kyis dag ma dag shan 'byed pa/ 'da' kha 'chi brod kyi man ngag gis rlung rig gnad du bsnun pa/ bar do 'od gsal gyi man ngag gis/
rlung rig ya bral ba/ sku gsum rang chas kyi man ngag gis/ 'khor ba ma stongs kyi bar du 'gro don byed pa/ ral cig ma'i gdams skor don tshan du bsdus pa/ 'di'i bka' bsrungs
kA la dang / bi kA la zhes bya ba gnod sbyin dmar nag gi rjes gnang dang bsgrub skor tshang ma thob bo/ /de ltar chos tshan 'di'i dbang rgyud/ 'grel pa/ man ngag dang
bcas pa'i brgyud pa'i rim pa ni/ rje btsun spyan ras gzigs/ byang sems blo gros rin chen/ ti lo shes rab bzang po/ rgyal sras rol pa'i rdo rje/ paN chen mi tra dzo ki
sgra bsgyur byams pa lo tsA/ mkhan chen bsod dbang / mkhan chen bsod nams seng ge yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston chos rje/ rin po che grags pa tshul khrims/ mthu stobs

gsad/ gtong ba btsal/ gter 'don/ tshe brtag gsang ba lha min gyi sgrub thabs rnams so/ /ral gcig yum gyi bskor la/ yum gyi sgrub thabs/ phyag mtshan bzhi'i sgrub thabs/ las
tshogs/ 'thug 'phrad

thog 'gel/ 'khrul pa shan 'byed/ 'da' kha 'chi brod/ bar do 'od gsal/ sku gsum rang chas rnams te/ yum skor 'di rnams zhu rgyu'o// ! //gsang 'dus kyi bskor// yang / 'dod chags

mkhan chen rin rnam pa/ yang / rdo rje 'chang chen dpal ldan birWa pa/ DoM bhi pa dang ni ra Di ya dang / ma ti ba dang snyog med dpyal chos bzang / rje btsun rgwa lo shes

rje 'jam gsang / rje btsun rgwa lo/ bla ma shes rab seng ge bla ma dpal ldan pa/ chos rje bu ston pa/ mkhan chen rin chen rnam rgyal/ bzad pa rin rgyal ba/ pha chos kyi
rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / brgyud srol gcig la/ rdo rje 'chang / birWa pa/ nag po pa/ sa pa li/ shI la tsantra/ dA na shi la/ chos rje 'jam gsar/ rje btsun rgwa lo/ bla
ma shes rab seng ge man sngar bzhin no/ ! /yang / yig cha'i skor la dbang gi cho ga rgyas

pa/ mngon par rtogs pa sgom pa'i tshul/ mchod phreng rnams bu ston chos rjes mdzad pa/ gshin rje gshed dmar po'i rdzogs rim rnal 'byor bzhi'i rim pa dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa'i
rdo rje'i tshig rkang / de'i man ngag gi gnad dArpan A tsarYa'i gsung bzhin/ lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen gyis bkod pa'i steng nas nyams khrid kyi tshul du tshang bar
thob/ de'i cha lag sngon 'gro bsag sbyang gnyis dang / rnal 'byor bzhi'i byin brlabs zhal shes phyogs glang gsar mas mdzad pa/ rnam rtog 'od gsal gyi byin brlabs dang / 'khrul
'khor dang phyir bzlog drug gi byin brlabs shes rab dar gyis mdzad pa/ rdzas kyi bcud len/ khol bsgrub/ phyag mtshan gnyis kyi sgrub thabs/ khro bo bcu'i bsrung 'khor/
'pho ba'i rnal 'byor/ 'od gsal 'char ba'i byin rlabs/ rang byin gyis brlabs kyi rim pa/ lha mo 'od 'dzin ma'i byin brlabs/ de'i sgrub thabs/ sems gong du 'pho ba'i man
ngag gi byin brlabs/ bdud rtsi ril bu'i byin brlabs/ phyir bzlog dang bsrung 'khor gyi byin brlabs/ 'tsho ba'i de kho na nyid/ gshin rje gshed dmar nag thun mong ba'i mchod
chog dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ 'khrul 'khor gyi de nyid nges bshad byang chub snying pos mdzad pa/ las tshogs yid bzhin nor bu'i skor la/ las tshogs spyi'i sgrub thabs
dang / dga' bas tshim ma zhes bya ba nas/ sgrub thabs sum cu rtsa grangs pa/ paNDi ta dA na shi la'i rang 'gyur/ gshed dmar lha lnga'i mngon dkyil bu ston chos rjes mdzad
pa/ gshin rje gshed dmar po'i rdzogs rim/ rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug dpal ldan birWa pa'i rdo rje'i tshig rkang dang / de'i man ngag paNDi ta dArpan A tsarYa'i gsung
lo tsA ba rmongs pa'i gnyen po dgos 'dod 'byung bas bsgyur cing bkod pa'i shin tu spros pa med pa'i

man ngag gi khrid yongs su rdzogs pa thob cing / yig cha'i skor la lha lnga'i dkyil chog mngon rtogs/ las bzhi'i sbyin sreg zhi ba'i sbyin sreg mchod phreng / rang byin brlabs
kyi yig cha rnams bu ston chos rjes mdzad pa/ lha lnga'i sgrub thabs/ lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs/ gtor chog rnams bi ru pas mdzad pa rnams kyi lung kyang thob bo/ ! /yang
/ bcom ldan 'das gshin rje'i gshed dgra nag bcu gsum ma'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba yongs su rdzogs pa thob pa'i brgyud pa'i rim pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes
kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pradznya rakShi ta/ dze ta ri pa/ rwa lo tsA ba badzra kirti/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rong pa rgwa lo/ rong
pa shes rab seng ge bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston chos kyi rje/ mkhan chen rin rnam pa/ mkhan chen grags rgyal ba/ bzad pa rin rgyal ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag
la'o/ ! /yang / brgyud srol gcig la/ 'jam dbyangs/ ye shes zhabs/ dpal sde ba/ dri med sbas pa/ karNa pa/ sa manta bha tra/ dpal 'dzin/ ka yaShtha pa/ dznyA na mi tra/ ratna
kirtI/ pen dha ba/ so na shrI/ men dza gling pa/ thugs rje chen po'i bar sngar bzhin no/ /'di'i mngon par rtogs pa'i sgom tshul mkhan chen rin chen rnam rgyal gyis mdzad
pa'i lung yang thob bo/ /zhwa lu ba'i phyag len la/ dbang gi cho ga gshed dmar bcu gsum ma'i yig cha de'i steng nas mdzad par gda'o// ! //yang / bcom ldan 'das gshin
rje'i gshed zhal drug pa'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba yongs su rdzogs pa thob nas/ brgyud pa'i rim pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ ti lo pa/ nA ro pa/
pradznyA rakShi ta/ men dza gling pa/ bal po thugs rje chen po/ rwa lo tsA ba chen po rdo rje

grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rong pa rgwa lo/ rong pa shes rab seng ge rong pa rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ bu ston chos kyi rje/ mkhan chen rin chen rnam
rgyal/ mkhan chen grags rgyal ba/ bzad pa rin rgyal ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o// ! //yang / brgyud srol gcig la/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ nag po pa/ bha dha
pa/ dha ma pa/ de ba pa/ dze ta ri pa/ a na ka badzra/ a kA ra ma ti/ bal po thugs rje chen po/ rje btsun rwa lo nas sngar ltar ro/ /'di'i sgrub thabs mkhan chen rin rnam
pas mdzad pa'i lung yang thob/ /yang / bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed lha bzhi bcu zhe dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'jigs byed/
ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra che chung gnyis/ skyo 'od kyi 'byung gnas/ rtsangs yang dag 'bar/ rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rngog rdo rje rgyal
po/ gze ba don grub seng ge khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma 'phags pa/ zhang ston rin chen dpal/ bla ma bsod nams 'bum/ bla ma gzhon tshul
ba/ sa bzangs paN chen/ yang / skyo 'od 'byung la/ skyo 'jam dpal/ skyo pad ma/ skyo kham lung pa/ gnyan rin chen brtan/ gnyan 'od bsrungs/ gnyan chos rgyal/ bla ma 'phags
pa/ blo chen pa/ bla ma gzhon tshul ba/ sa bzangs paN chen/ sa bzangs 'phags pa/ 'dan ston puNye dznyA na/ bla ma dpal ldan legs dbang / pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/
! /yang / bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed rwa lo tsA ba'i lugs/ lha bcu gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba zhus pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed/
ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ slob dpon la li ta badzra/ a

mo gha badzra/ a nanta badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ padma badzra/ di paM ka ra/ rwa rdo rje grags/ rwa ye shes seng ge rwa chos rab/ rwa 'bum seng / rje btsun rgwa
lo/ bla ma byang chub dar/ 'dzam gling paNDi ta/ bla ma a mo gha pa/ bzad pa rin rgyal ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag go /yang / bla chen rong pa/ bla ma shes rab seng ge
bag ston gzhon tshul ba/ khyung ri pa/ rje btsun seng ge yang / rwa 'bum seng la/ dbus pa dbang phyug grags/ ldong ston shes rab dpal/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ shar pa rgyal
mtshan bzang po/ gu rum pa dkon mchog rgyal mtshan/ bla ma tshul rgyal ba/ bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang
/ bla ma shes rab seng ge la/ bag ston gzhon tshul/ bag ston tshul rgyal/ kun mkhyen bde legs dpal/ gnyag dbon chos rje/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos rje/ des bdag

dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / rwa ye shes seng ge rwa dharmma seng ge rwa dkon mchog seng ge rwa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/
rgya ston kun dga' brtson 'grus/ bla ma yon tan 'bum/ bla ma sangs rgyas skyabs pa/ bla ma rgyal mtshan tshul khrims/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / bcom ldan
'das rdo rje 'jigs byed mal lo tsA ba lugs kyi ro langs brgyad bskor du grags pa de'i sgrub dkyil chos rje 'phags pas mdzad pa'i steng nas bka' dang lung zhus pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs

ba chos dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / yig cha'i bskor la/ rtog pa bdun pa'i rgyud rwa lo'i 'gyur/ rtog pa gsum pa'i rgyud rong zom gyi 'gyur/
rtog pa gcig pa zhes bya ba gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa/ rtog bdun gyi dka' 'grel dang / rwa pa'i chos brgyad/ rtog bdun gyi tshig don rnam bshad/ man ngag gnad bdun bshad pa/
bsnyen sgrub las gshin sbrel ma/ rwa los mdzad pa'i 'khor lo'i cho ga gsal byed/ 'di rtag bsrung bzlog gsad gsum gyi man ngag shog dril gsum gyi man ngag sngags bzlas
dang / 'khor tshul gyi man ngag drag po'i sbyin sreg zhi ba'i sbyin

sreg mi mthun kun sel/ rgyas pa'i sbyin sreg 'dod pa kun 'phel/ dbang gi sbyin sreg gnad kyi lcags kyu/ rdzogs rim mtshan ma gyen sgreng / rwa rtse'i rnal 'byor/ mtshan mo
rgyu ba'i man ngag 'khrul 'khor bri thabs/ 'chi kha ma'i gdams ngag gtor ma'i man ngag lha bcu gsum gyi mngon rtogs yid bzhin gter mdzod/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rgyas pa
rnams rwa los mdzad pa/ nyi ma bzhi pa'i man ngag rwa 'bum seng gis mdzad pa/ las mkhan tstshun tstshun dha ra'i sgrub thabs/ de'i cho ga zhib mo bshad pa/ phyag mtshan sum
cu rtsa gnyis la rten nas 'phrin las sna tshogs bsgrub pa/ rgya ston pas mdzad pa'i rtog bdun dang rtog gsum gyi 'grel pa/ bu ston chos rjes mdzad pa'i rtog gsum gyi 'khrul
'khor gsal byed me long lag khrid zhal shes dang bcas pa/ 'khrul 'khor rnams kyi dpe chung dang / bri thabs/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi bskyed rim bsgom tshul bogs 'don
sngags kyi bzlas pas 'phrin las sgrub pa'i tshul 'bri khung dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ yang / yi ge bzhi pa'i man ngag shog dril gsum gyi gnad 'grol/ zhi ba 'jigs pa brgyad
las skyob pa sogs kyi zhal shes/ lo tsA ba phyi ma dang rgya ston gyis mdzad pa/ dmar po mda' gzhu 'gengs pa'i rjes gnang dang / man ngag zhal shes gsum dril/ yi ge bzhi
pa'i gsad bzlog las kyi sham bu dang bcas pa/ 'jigs byed sngo nag phyag gnyis pa la rten nas dug 'joms pa'i man ngag dug dbang rma bya rgyas pa'i dbang bskur dang / yig
cha'i rim pa/ lo rgyus/ brtag thabs/ gso ba/ bsrung ba/ 'dred bya ba/ bya rwa ba/ dbang bskur gyi yig sna che chung rnams so/ ! /yang / 'jigs byed phyag drug pa'i mngon
rtogs khams gsum za byed/ phyag bzhi pa'i mngon rtogs dri med chu rgyun/ phyag gnyis pa'i mngon rtogs rin chen don 'dus/ man ngag bcud kyi thigs pa rnams rwa los mdzad pa'i
lung yang zhus so/ ! /las gshin gyi brgyud pa ni/ gshin rje gshed/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ ku ma ra tsantra/ nA ga bo ti/ li la badzra/ dznyA na kIrti/ mi nyag ston
bsgom/ lo bsgom zhig po/ zhang bsod nams rin chen/ thang bstod pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rdo rje bzang po/ bla ma ArYa de ba/ chos rje kun blo ba/ mkhan chen seng
ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i yig cha la/ la li ta badzras mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ bal po thugs rje chen po dang rwa lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ de'i man ngag
bsnyen bsgrub gsad gsum gyi las sgrigs/ bla ma chen po'i gdams pa lcags bsgom ras pa la gtad pa/ rjes gnang gi yi ge bla ma ArYa bas mdzad pa rnams so// ! //yang phur sogs/
yang / dpal ldan bla ma bka' drin mnyam med de las/ gsang sngags snga 'gyur rnying ma'i skor thob pa la/ yang dag pa lugs lha lnga bcu rtsa brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor cho

rin chen dpal/ dznyA na sA ga ra/ ye bres rgya mtsho/ ra bi sing ha/ nyi ma seng ge smra ba'i ye shes/ ba dhi siM/ buddha gho Sha/ sangs rgyas dbyangs/ shAkya singga / shAkya
seng ge shrI ba na ratna/ dpal nags kyi rin chen/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / 'phags pa mi g.yo ba dkar po shes rab skyed pa'i rjes su gnang ba zhus
nas/ paNDi ta sbyin pa tshul khrims kyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs/ tshigs su bcad pa drug pa/ paNDi ta de nyid kyi rang 'gyur lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom

chen sher rdor ba/ rje btsun chos sgo ba chos dpal

shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o// ! //rme rtsegs kyi bskor// yang / khro bo rme ba rtsegs pa'i rjes su gnang ba/ gong 'og gnyis la rjes gnang gi yi ge so sor yod/
bla ma rgya ston a nantA birYas mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas zhus shing / des mdzad pa'i bstod pa dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan
pa che chung gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa chen/ rje btsun pa/ sa paN/ 'jam dbyangs rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma mus chen pa/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bla ma 'bri phyugs pa
rin chen dpal/ bla ma rme rtsegs pa bsod rdor/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / rme brtsegs pa la/ mkhan chen rin chen rgyal mtshan/
mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / rme brtsegs gter ma'i brgyud pa ni/ gu ru chos dbang / sras pad ma dbang chen/ de sras chos rdor/
bla ma ngag dbang pa/ mkhan chen byang seng pa/ bla ma rin chen dpal/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / khro mo rme rtsegs ni/ sangs
rgyas/ phyag rdor/ seng gdong can/ gru ratna/ gru spang rtsa ba rdo rje seng ge dmar shAkya grub/ chos rje 'od kyi mtshan can/ chos rje bsod nams seng ge bla ma rgya gar
rgyal mtshan/ bka' bzhi pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ //yang / rme brtsegs kyi gzungs chog rjes snang gi cho ga rme
brtsegs kyi sgrub thabs/ dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na dang / lo tsA ba 'brom gyi bsgyur zer ba gcig kyang thob bo/ /yang sgrub thabs/ las tshogs bcu gcig dang bcas pa'i yig
sna/ chos rje sa skya pas mdzad pa'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ chos rje sa

paN/ bla ma 'phags pa/ bla ma shes rab seng ge bla ma grags 'byor/ bla ma 'dzam gling pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des
bdag la'o/ /'phags pa stobs po che zhes bya ba'i lung yang zhus so/ ! /gzhan yang / rigs gsum ka dang 'brel ba/ bya spyod kyi dbang gi sgo 'byed/ rigs gsum spyi'i rig pa
gtad pa'i cho ga rje btsun pas mdzad pa'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ kha che ye shes rdo rje/ lo chung grags mchog shes rab/ sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun rtse mo/
rje btsun pa/ chos rje pa/ do pa ston tshul/ yar lung pa rgyal tsha lung mangs/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos
dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o// ! //tshe dpag med kyi bskor// gzhan yang / tshe dpag med bla med grub pa'i rgyal mo ras chung pa'i lugs/ gan pa rin rgyal
gyis mdzad pa'i sgrub thabs dang dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga la rten pa'i dbang bskur ba yongs su rdzogs pa dang / de'i las kyi lha rta mgrin dpa' bo gcig pa'i rjes gnang

chen dpal 'byor ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag

rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / tshe dpag med grub rgyal ma'i lha tshogs la bstod pa yon tan nor bu'i 'phreng ba/ chos sgo bas mdzad pa'i lung yang zhus
so/ ! /yang / dze ta ri dgra las rnam rgyal gyi lugs/ tshe dpag med lha dgu'i bsnyen pa dang dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga 'chi bslu dang bcas pa'i yig cha lo tsA ba rin rnam

rnam rgyal ba ri lo tsA ba'i lugs/ lha dgu'i rjes su gnang ba dang / sgrub thabs/ stong mchod la sogs pa'i yig cha 'gro mgon 'phags pas mdzad pa dang / slob dpon tsantra
go mis mdzad pa lha dgu'i bstod pa/ mdo sde las 'byung ba gso sbyong rang gis blang ba'i cho ga sogs yan lag tshang bar zhus so/ /'di'i brgyud pa'i rim pa ni/ yang dag par
rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa/ mgon po byams pa/ 'phags pa thogs med/ slob dpon dbyig gnyen/ bskal ldan grags pa/ shI la ka ra ma ti/ paNDi ta bai ro tsA na rakShi
ta/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen

grags/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa paN/ go lung pa/ dga' ldan pa/ khams pa rgan mo lhas pa/ slob dpon ston pa/ bla ma bsod nams
dbang phyug mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma bsod nams seng ge chos rje bsod rgyal ba/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi
rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / sangs rgyas/ badzra pA Ni/ dze ta ri pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba/ chung ba/ ba ri lo tsA ba nas gong bzhin no/ ! /yang / gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi
gzungs kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri ba/ sa chen pa/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ dus 'khor ba/ bla
ma 'jam dbyangs pa/ bag ston gzhon tshul ba/ ma ti paN chen/ snyag dbon/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /gtsug tor dri ma med pa'i rjes gnang
gi yi ge sgrub thabs rin chen rgyal mtshan gyis gnas snying gi gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba/ rgyal ba zla ba dri ma med pa'i sku zhes pa'i bstod pa rnams kyi lung dang rjes
gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ thub pa/ 'jam dpal/ boddhi sa twa/ boddhi sa twa chung ba/ rgyal po dga' ba'i dpal/ dge ba'i dpal/ a ti sha/ lha btsun byang chub 'od/ ti se ba

rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /gtsug tor 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs bsam yas pas mdzad pa/ gtsug tor 'bar ba'i las tshogs/ yang / khro bo gtsug tor 'bar ba'i sgrub thabs byang chub gzhon
nus mdzad pa'ang zhus so// //kun rig gi skor// yang / bcom ldan 'das kun rig gi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba zhus nas rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa kun rig gi cho ga gzhan

rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ slob dpon rab 'byor skyangs/ slob dpon kun dga' snying po/ slob dpon shes rab skyangs/ slob dpon zhi
ba snying po/ sha ku la mi tra/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ shrAddha ka ra warmA/ lo tsA ba chen po/ bla ma brag stengs pa/ mal lo tsA ba/ sa chen pa/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje

jo bo rje/ go mi sgom chen/ kyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal pa nyi

she/ gnur nyi ma shes rab/ rtsas skya ston grags/ shAkya 'bum/ 'dzims pa rin she/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo
ba chos dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / bu ston chos rjes mdzad pa'i kun rig gi cho ga rgyas pa'i steng nas dbang lung yongs su rdzogs par thob/

'dzin/ dpa' bo rdo rje pha la/ ye shes rdo rje/ pradznyA siddhi/ de bzhi ka la kun dga' snying po/ pradznyA wa li ta/ rab 'byor skyangs/ shraddha ka ra warmma/ sangs rgyas

ma dbang rnon pa/ bla ma kun dga' rin chen/ bzad pa rin rgyal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga

rgyas/ gsang ba'i

po/ bla chen rong pa/ 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston chos rje/ thugs sras lo tsA ba/ bla ma bsod nams dpal/ bzad pa rin rgyal ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/

pa/ gtor ma/ gzungs/ klu gtor/ bstod pa/ lo rgyus/ byin rlabs/ gzungs lung rnams yod do/ ! /yang / sman bla sprul pa sku'i rjes su gnang ba'ang zhus la/ bdag gi bla

ltar ro/ ! /yang / sman bla'i mdo chog gi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ thub pa/ 'jam dpal/ boddhi sa twa che chung / rgyal po dge ba'i dpal/ a ti sha/ lha btsun byang chub 'od/
ti se ba chen po/ byang sems zla rgyal/ ong po lo tsA/ dgra bcom rgyal

mtshan/ bla ma dbang mdzes/ bla ma dpal mdzes/ yon tan dbang phyug shangs pa 'dul 'dzin/ mkhan chen bsod grags/ rgyal sras thogs med/ lo chen byang rtse/ dpal ldan ye shes/
de gnyis ka la bka' bzhi pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / g.yul las rnam par rgyal ba'i sgrub thabs/ sha ri pu
tra dang rnal 'byor pa kun dga' blo gros rgyal mtshan dpal bzang pos sgyur ba zhus/ dri med kyi bsgom bzlas mdor bsdus pa yon tan dpal gyis sbyar ba/ rjes gnang gi yi ge
gtsug tor dri ma med pa'i sgrub thabs rin chen rgyal mtshan gyis gnas rnying gi gtsug lag khang du sbyar ba/ rgyal ba zla ba dri ma med pa'i sku zhes pa'i bstod pa rnams

bdag la'o// ! //gzhan yang / rdo rje 'phreng ba zhes grags pa'i dbang bskur ba rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khyab bdag rdo rje 'chang / rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor
ma/ mkhas pa a bha ya ka ra gupta/ na ya ka pa/ da sha ba la shrI/ bi khya ta de ba/ kha che shAkya shrI bha tra/ bhU mi shrI/ bi ma la shrI/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal
mtshan/ dharmA rA dza/ a mo gha shrI/ chos rje byang chub dpal/ pha chos kyi

rje/ des bdag la'o/ /'di 1la gsang ba 'dus pa 'jam pa'i rdo rje lha bcu dgu/ 2mi bskyod pa la lha so gnyis/ 3kha sbyor gyi rdo rje sems pa lha so bdun/ 4ye shes mkha' 'gro
lha bcu gsum/ 5kyai rdo rje mtshon cha can phyag gnyis pa/ 6phyag bzhi pa/ 7phyag drug pa/ 8phyag bcu drug pa ste/ lha bcu bdun re yod pa'i dkyil 'khor bzhi/ 10bdag med ma
lha nyi shu rtsa gsum/ yang bdag med ma lha mo bco lnga dang / 11ku ru kulle lha bco lnga/ 12rdo rje bdud rtsi lha nyi shu rtsa gcig bdud rtsi lhag ma gsum rgyud las 'byung
bar bstan/ rtsa rgyud las bshad pa'i/ 13kyai rdo rje thod pa can zhal gcig phyag gnyis pa/ 14phyag bzhi pa/ 15zhal gsum phyag drug pa/ 16zhal brgyad phyag bcu drug pa
ste lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor bzhi/ 17ma hA ma ya lha lnga/ 18sangs rgyas thod pa lha dgu/ 19kha sbyor las mngon brjod las/ bshad pa'i hU~M mdzad lha bcu gcig gzhan rnams 'dir
'jam rdor/ mi bskyod pa/ rdor sems kyi khro bcus bskor ba'i hU~M mdzad lha bcu gcig ma gsum yang snang / 20lU hi pa'i rjes 'brang gi bde mchog lha drug cu rtsa gnyis
dang / 21bde mchog gtso 'khor thams cad zhal gcig phyag gnyis 22par byas pa'i lugs gnyis te bde mchog gi dkyil 'khor gsum/ 23yang 'di 24la phag 25mos gtso byas pa'i dpa'
mo rnams kho na bsgom pa'i dkyil 'khor gsum/ 26yang sangs rgyas thod pa lha nyi shu rtsa lnga'i dkyil 'khor gcig 27rdo rje gdan bzhi'i rnal 'byor nam mkha' lha lnga bcu nga
bdun gyi dkyil 'khor/ 28gshin rje'i gshed nag po lha bcu gsum gyi dkyil 'khor/ 29gur gyi sgrol ma lha bcu gcig phyag mtshan brgyad dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor/ 30'od zer
can lha nyi shu rtsa lnga/ 31so sor 'brang ma ser mo lha dgu/ 32rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor sgo gnyis sbrag la rtsa ba'i lha lnga bcu nga gsum/ skal bzang dgu brgya
dang

go drug kha bskong rgyu/ 33rgyu 'phrul drwa ba'i 'jam rdor sgo gnyis sbrag gi dkyil 'khor lha bzhi cu rtsa gsum/ 34chos dbyings gsung dbang sgo bzhi sbrag gi dkyil 'khor lha
nyi brgya dang nyi shu rtsa gcig 35gtsug dgu'i dkyil 'khor lha sum cu so bdun/ 36phyag na rdo rje 'byung po 'dul byed lha sum cu so gsum/ 37bshad rgyud rdo rje gur gyi
mkha' 'gro lnga bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor bsdus pa'i rgyas pa lha lnga bcu nga gsum/ 39bde mchog 'khor lo sgyur ba drug gis bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor lha bdun bcu don gnyis/ dpal
dus kyi 'khor lo yongs rdzogs lha drug brgya sum cu rtsa drug gi dkyil 'khor sgo sum sbrag dang bcas pa/ 'di yan la dngos su dkyil 'khor sum cu so dgu/ 'di rnams kyi bka'
a bha ya nyid kyi bzhed pa bla med phyogs gcig yin pa 'dra yang / bu ston sogs kyi bzhed pa ltar/ rgyud sde bzhi so sor phye ba'i lugs dang / dkyil chog rdo rje phreng
ba/ mngon rtogs rnal 'byor rdzogs 'phreng / sbyin sreg 'od kyi snye ma ste phreng ba skor gsum la/ man ngag snye ma nas kha skong dgos pa/ snye ma bco brgyad pa'i dkyil
'khor gyi dag pa'i lung dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs par zhus shing / bdud rtsi gsum gyi mngon rtogs bu ston pas mdzad pa'ang zhus so// //yang / sa skya pa'i gser chos dmar
po bskor gsum du grags pa'i dang po/ lha mo ku ru kulle'i rjes gnang zhus nas/ brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ nag po pa/ DA ma ru pa/ a ba dhu
ti/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ se mkhar chung pa/ zhang dgon pa ba/ sa chen pa/ slob dpon pa/ rje btsun pa/ sa paN/ 'u yug pa rig pa'i seng ge nyi thog pa kun
smon/ bla ma yon tan dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ bla ma gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo

rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na/ rdo rje 'chang / ku ru kulle/ rgyal po lhan cig skyes pa'i rol pa/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung
gnyis/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje sa chen man gong bzhin no/ /'di'i rjes gnang rgya ston pas mdzad pa/ sgrub thabs dang las tshogs/ 'khor lo la rten nas bsgrub bya ba dang / maNDal
la rten nas bya ba dang / rdzas la rten nas bya ba rnams/ rje btsun chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i steng nas zhus so/ ! /yang / khro bo 'dod pa'i rgyal
po'am/ bkag chol mar grags pa'i rjes su gnang ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ de'i rtsa ba ni dus kyi 'khor lo/ he ru ka pad ma dbang chen/ bde mchog 'khor lo/ dgyes pa rdo
rje/ rdo rje gur/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro la sogs pa'i man ngag gi don bsdus nas/ rdo rje 'chang chen pos/ yum bde ba rgyas byed ma la gnang / des dze ta ri dgra las rnam rgyal/
des la li ta badzra/ paNDi ta ta thA ga ta rakShi ta/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po/ rdo rje gdan pa chung ba/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa chen pa/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun
pa/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ yang / sa chen pas khams pa don grub/ phag mo grub pa/ bshen rdor seng / dza dza ne/ rong pa dge rings/ slob dpon jo btsun/ bla ma 'phags pa dang /

chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / rdo rje gdan pa che chung gnyis/ tha ba ri pa chen po/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ rje btsun lcags thang pa/ jo btsun se chung / sa chen pa/ rje
btsun rtse mo/ rje btsun grags rgyal/ sa paN/ slob dpon khams pa/ slob dpon

dbon/ yang rong pa dge rings/ rgya do pa/ slob dpon jo btsun no/ /yang / khams pa la/ grub thob stag te'u/ bla chen dran/ sras shes rab seng ge mkhas pa dkon rin/ lha rin chen
grags/ bsod nams byang chub/ 'dzam gling pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos sgo ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /de'i yig cha'i rim pa ni/ dbang bsdus las
kyi 'khor lo'i byung tshul/ brgyud pa'i lo rgyus manydzu gho Sha na thas sbyar ba/ dbang bsdus las kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag 'gro ba'i srog snying 'gugs pa'i lcags kyu/ mkha'
'gro ma'i sgrub thabs dbang bsdus las kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag dbang du bsdus pa'i cho ga phrin las myur du sgrub pa las kha rlung la gzhol ba/ rjes gnang man ngag 'jam
dbyangs mgon pos bsdus pa/ yang rjes gnang gi man ngag yig chung / dbang gi tsakra'i zhal gdams/ las sbyor gyi gnad/ 'khor lo bri thabs zhal gdams zin bris ma/ tha mo
che bri thabs/ yang / 'khor lo'i bri thabs yig chung / zhal gdams khrigs chags su sgrigs pa nyams su blang bde ba snying nang gi khrag lta bu gzhung dang mi 'gal bar sdebs
pa/ mkha' 'gro ma'i gsang sgrub rnams 'dzam gling paNDi tas sgrigs pa/ ra dzA sogs dbang du byed na zhes pa sbyin sreg dang 'khor lo la rten pa'i las sbyor/ sngags kyi
rgyal po'i dam tshig gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa ba ri ba'i 'gyur/ sa skya pa'i phreng ba dmar po'i gdams pa/ dbang gi 'phrin las lag len dge
slong shI la kirtis sbyar ba/ gsang sgrub tha chen gyi 'khor lo bri thabs/ 'khor lo'i bri thabs nyin mtshan gyi bsrung ba dang bcas pa/ rjes gnang gi 'di zlos/ yig chung
'jam dbyangs mgon pos sbyar ba/ 'dod rgyal yab yum gyi sbags sgrub

rgyal po dpal gyis mdzad pa/ las bzhi ka bsgrub na zhes pa dang / rin chen bsgrub pa'i man ngag zhes pa dang / tha chen gyi 'khor lo bri thabs/ gsal byed nyi ma'i 'khor los
snod bcud dbang du bya ba/ rdo rje gdan pas mdzad pa/ sa chen gyis mdzad pa'i 'grel pa rdo rje rin po che'i myu gu/ snod bcud dbang du bya ba sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ sku gsung
thugs kyi rab gnas/ zhal gdams kyi zin bris zhes pa dang / gzhan dbang du bya thabs ba ri bas sa skya pa la gnang ba/ rtags kyi yig chung / sbyin sreg bya thabs rnams
so/ /'di rnams cung zad bzlos pa srid kyang tshig zur la khyad par yod do/ /yang / de'i yig cha'i rim pa la/ ba ri ba'i zhal gdams bka' rgya ma/ rjes gnang dang / sngags
rings gnyis dang bcas pa'i bri bzlas sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ sbas pa'i mig 'byed sa chen gyis sgrol ma lha khang du bkod pa/ yang rab gnas sogs dbang gi nang sgrub zab mo
sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ gnad 'bebs nyi zla'i 'khor lo rje btsun rin po ches mdzad pa/ mkha' 'gro ma'i spobs chog sa paN gyis mdzad pa/ dbang gi nang sgrub sa paN gyis mdzad
pa rnams so// //yang / tshogs bdag dmar po'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje phag mo/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ ri khrod mgon po/ ha ngu dkar po/ mal gyo
blo gros grags/ sa skya pa chen po/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun chen po/ chos rje sa paN/ rin po che skyob pa dpal/ gzhon nu bkra shis/ rdo rje dpal/ gzhon nu dpal/
gu ru shes rin/ 'dzam gling pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos sgo ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /de'i yig cha'i rim pa la/ rjes gnang gi yi ge gcig bsnyen
sgrub las sbyor man ngag phran tshegs dang bcas pa chos rgyal 'phags pas

mdzad pa/ rjes gnang gi phyag len zin bris yar lung pa seng ge rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa/ tshogs kyi bdag po la mchod cing gsol ba gdab pa'i tshul shlau ka sum cu rtsa bdun
pa dang / tshogs bdag gi bstod pa mdor bsdus pa dpal ldan bla ma dam pas mdzad pa/ 'phags pa tshogs kyi bdag po'i gzungs gnyis/ tshogs bdag dmar po phyag bcu gnyis pa'i/
phyag mtshan bcu gnyis kyi las tshogs/ yang las tshogs kyi yig chung gcig tshogs kyi bdag po'i 'khor lo'i gsal byed DoM bhi he ru kas mdzad pa/ 'khor lo'i de kho na nyid
gsal bar byed pa rin chen ljon shing tshul blos mdzad pa rnams so// ! //yang / tshogs bdag dkar po phyag bzhi pa'i rjes gnang lung dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ a mo gha
badzra/ nA ro pa/ dI paM ka ra/ 'brom ston pa/ po to ba/ sha ra ba/ 'chad kha ba/ khro phu ba/ khyi lo/ yo ba/ shI la pra bha wa/ dos ku ma ra/ lcan bandhe/ gsal ba sgang
pa/ slob dpon dpal mgon/ slob 'od ma/ 'tshal min chos rje rin po che seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / a mo gha badzra/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri ba/
sa chen/ rtse mo/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ bla ma khang ston pa/ bla ma byang chen pa/ chos rje bka' bcu pa/ gung pa bkra shis bzang po/ 'tshal min chos rje/ mkhan chen seng ge
dpal ba/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /de'i yig cha'i rim pa ni/ brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i gsang ba'i sgrub thabs/ a mo gha badzras mdzad pa nag tsho'i
'gyur/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i sgrub pa'i man ngag rab gnas bya thabs/ gtor ma 'bul ba/ bstod pa a mo gha badzras mdzad pa/ la du zhes pa'i zhal zas 'chos thabs dang / gcun
sngags/ tshogs bdag sgrub

pa'i rten gyi gang zag gi zhes pa dang / zan nam chan la gtor ma bre gang yan chad bzang bar bya ste zhes pa dang / de la 'di sgrub par 'dod pas/ zhes pa'i sgrub thabs gsum/
tshogs kyi bdag po'i snying po gzungs la phyag 'tshal lo zhes pa'i bstod pa/ rnal 'byor longs spyod rtag dka' bas/ zhes pa'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa/ bgegs kyi rgyal po'i
sgrub thabs ni/ zhes pa'i sgrub thabs/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i gzungs mig mthong gi gdams pa rnams so/ /yig cha 'di rnams tshogs bdag dmar po phyag bzhi pa dang thun mong du
snang ngo / ! /tshogs bdag dkar po zhal gsum phyag drug pa'am/ chags pa rdo rjer grags pa'i rjes gnang / lung dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ intra bhu ti/ rgyal po grags pa/
byang chub 'byung gnas/ rin chen 'od zer/ yang dag sbyin pa/ rin chen 'byung gnas zhi ba/ jo bo rje/ rgya brtson seng / grub thob shol so ba/ sangs rgyas dbon ston/ sangs
rgyas ston tshul/ khyung tshang pa slob dpon tshul rgyal/ snar thang pa mkhan po nyi ma/ dbu ma pa grub brtson/ chos rje bka' bcu pa/ gung chen pa/ 'tshal min chos rje/
rin po che seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /de'i yig cha'i rim pa ni/ tshogs bdag gi lo rgyus/ tshogs bdag khro bo sgrub thabs gser gling pas mdzad pa/
tshogs kyi bdag po'i gsang sgrub/ gtor ma/ mi 'gyur bkod pa pho brang rdo rje'i gdan/ zhes pa'i gsol gdab spyan 'dren/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i bgegs sel ba'i sgrub thabs/
chags pa rdo rje dam tshig gi bstod pa jo bos mdzad pa/ rab gnas bya thabs/ rtags ma byung na yi dam lha gnad la dbab pa/ gnad la 'bor ba/ bzlas pa'i zhal gdams/ chags pa
rdo rje'i zhal

gdams tshig gnyis/ chags pa rdo rje'i las mtha' la sbyin sreg dang / gsad pa/ spobs pa'i yig chung / sngags 'bum gyi gdams pa/ 'jur bgegs sel ba'i sgrub thabs/ rjes gnang gi
yi ge ga na pa ti'i spre'u'i sgrub thabs/ tshogs bdag gi gsang sgrub/ ga lnga pa bla ma'i zhal las rnyed pa'i gdams ngag rnams so// ! //yang / gnyan lo nas brgyud pa'i
dmar chung skor gsum la/ ku ru kulle/ nor rgyun ma/ lha mo te nu rnams la dpal mo gser gyi snying thag can du grags pa'i rjes gnang sgrub thabs/ las tshogs dang bcas pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma/ gnyan lo/ gnam kha'u pa/ sa chen pa/ slob dpon rtse mo/ rje btsun pa/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ khams pa rdo rje dpal/
bla ma grags pa dpal/ bla ma 'phags pa/ bla ma dkon rgyal ba/ bla ma rin chen dpal/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / rje btsun chen po/
bla chen yar bsgom/ rgyal tsha lung mangs po/ mkhas pa yon tan khri/ mkhan chen seng ge bzang po/ yang / sa paN/ tshogs sgom/ nyan chen/ na bza' brag phug pa/ bka' bcu
pa/ gung pa/ lung mangs po/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /de'i yig cha'i rim pa ni/ lo rgyus dang / ku ru kulle'i nyams su blang tshul sogs
gnyan lo'i u pa de sha/ ku ru kulle'i bstod pa DoM bhi bas mdzad pa/ ku ru kulle'i rjes gnang / nor rgyun ma'i sgrub thabs zhal shes dang bcas pa/ lha mo te nu'i sgrub thabs
rjes gnang dang bcas pa rnams so// ! //yang / rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyi skor thob pa la/ gar mkhan mchog gi rgyud nas gsungs pa'i rnam sras ser chen rta

bdag brgyad kyis bskor ba/ ljang khu klu brgyad kyis skor ba/ mthing kha zhal gsum phyag drug lha mo brgyad kyis bskor ba/ shu rangga warmma lugs kyi rnam sras a pa ra tsi
ta dang bcas pa'i sgrub thabs/ 'gro bzangs snying po'i lugs kyi sgrub thabs sham bu bdun gyi man ngag dang bcas pa/ bu ston chos rjes mdzad pa'i ser chen gyi phyi sgrub/
bsnyen sgrub gtor chog dang bcas pa/ ljang khu gsang sgrub gong khug sro ma can gyi bskor bsnyen bsgrub las sbyor dang bcas pa/ rta bdag brgyad kyi khol bsgrub/ ser chen
dang / mdung dmar 'di bu ston gyis mdzad pa yin/ can gnyis kyi rjes gnang gi yi ge bu ston pas mdzad pa/ DoM bhi he ru ka nas brgyud pa'i mdung dmar can gyi sgrub thabs nA
ro pa'i zhal gdams dang bcas pa/ gsang sgrub yid bzhin nor bu tshe sgrub dang bcas pa/ gces yig bsdus pa/ dam tshig bsrung thabs/ bzlas pa'i man ngag gsang ba'i man ngag
rten gsum gyi 'chad thabs/ ku be ra la rta phyugs gnyer du gtad pa/ gces yig bco brgyad pa/ dgra la 'chad pa bcad pa/ mdung dmar can bo dong bya rgod gshongs kyi gter ma/
las tshogs zhal shes dgos 'dod 'byung ba lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal gyis zin bris su sgrigs pa rnams thob bo/ /chos tshan de dag gi lung ser chen gyi rjes gnang dang
bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ gsang ba'i bdag po/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro bzangs snying po/ paNDi
ta rin chen rdo rje/ kha che dgon pa ba/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ g.yor po jo ston/ bsod nams rin chen/ 'jid chu ba/ lha rje jo bzangs/ byams pa lo tsA ba/ bsod nams dbang phyug
bsod nams seng ge rin chen seng ge bu ston chos rje/ bla ma thabs kyi blo gros/ bzad pa rin rgyal ba/ pha chos

kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /mdung dmar can gyi brgyud pa ni/ phyag na rdo rje/ slob dpon dga' rab rdo rje/ rgyal po g.yu sgra snying po/ khri srong lde'u btsan/ skyes bu lha
bzangs skyid dpal/ des bya rgod gshongs kyi gtsug lag khang du sgrub thabs dang sku 'bag gnyis gter du sbas/ de snyal pa nyi ma shes rab kyis snyed/ de nas rim bzhin snur
nyi ma 'od zer/ dbus pa dmar ston/ bcur ston/ 'od zer bla ma/ ye shes rgya mtsho/ slob dpon thabs blo/ bzad pa rin rgyal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang / mi pham
skra'i zla ba can/ a bhya ka ra/ zangs dkar lo tsA/ thugs kyi mang ston/ rin po che pa/ sogs pa byang yon/ dpal rgwa lo nas so/ ! /yang / slob dpon pad ma saM bha ba'i
lugs kyi rnam sras gter ma'i skor thob pa la/ sprin gseb ma rta bdag brgyad dang / klu mo gnyis kyi sgrub thabs/ mdzod pa'i sgrub thabs/ rdo rje srid rgyal gyi sgrub thabs/
'joms byed rtsal khyi can mtshon bsrungs kyi man ngag g.ya' spang rtsal sre mong can chang nyes kyi sbyor ba/ drag po rtsal bya rgod mgo can gyis gsad pa/ mche phyug
dred mgo can gyis mnan pa/ 'phrog byed spre'u'i mgo can gyis 'byed pa/ gar dbang khyung mgo can gyis dbye zhing skrad pa/ thog chen dred mgos ser ba dbab pa/ dpa' bo rgyal
'ug pa'i mgos gdug pa can gnas nas dbyung ba ste mgo gnyan can brgyad kyi sgrub thabs/ las sbyor/ lo rgyus dang bcas pa'ang thos shing rtogs so// ! //dzam bha la nag po'i
srog gi 'khor lo'i brgyud pa ni/ gsang ba'i bdag po/ mkha' 'gro ma ganggA siddhi/ dA na siddhi/ u rgyan pad ma/ bal po hung / snubs phag mo lung pa/ 'gar ston 'bum dar/
slul kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ rin po che bsod nams byang

chub/ 'dzam gling paNDi ta/ bla ma rin chen rgyal po/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i yig cha la/ lo rgyus/ bzlas pa/ chu sbyin/ gtor ma/ 'khor
lo/ thab khung / rgyab yol/ dam tshig rtags/ spogs chog chud mi za ba rnams dge slong chos kyi bla mas bkod pa/ chu sbyin gyi lag len mngon rtogs gru rdo rje seng ges
bkod pa/ phyag mtshan ne'u le'i sgrub thabs bka' rgya ma/ yang gsang srog gi 'khor lo'i lo rgyus dang bca' thabs/ mgon po nor bdag bsgrub pa'i thabs zhes pa/ srog 'khor
dmar khrid yig chung / srog 'khor gyi zhal gdams/ yang / zhal gdams bal po a hU~M gis gter nas gton pa/ srog 'khor bca' gzhi'i gnad/ dngos grub myur du bskul ba zhes pa/
srog 'khor gyi bri yig yang / srog 'khor gyi gnad kyi yig chung rnams so/ /'di rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ thabs kyi blo gros/ bzad pa rin rgyal ba/ de la bdag gi bla
mas gsan pa lags so// ! //yang / dzambha la sbas pa bum 'khyil gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ paNDi ta sarbA dznyA kriShNa/ shar phyogs rgyal po/ bhangga la'i rgyal po/

pa/ sprul pa'i

'phrin las kyi rnam par thar pa bstan pa/ rin chen sna bdun gyi ming tshan pa gsum/ grong khyer shing rtags can gyi lo rgyus/ gter bum dang thod pa la rten nas nor sgrub pa/
dga' bzhi'i ye shes bskyed pa/ rna ba mnan pa/ mdangs 'phrog pa/ byis pa'i gzugs 'jigs pas zhes pa'i las tshogs gsum/ char dbab pa/ nor bdag gzir bas nor rnams 'phrog ces
pa'i las tshogs/ chu dbang snying rje can zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa snod 'dzin gyi gzungs/ chu sbyin pa'i man ngag chu sbyin pa'i gleng gzhi rnams so// ! //dmar
po'i skor grwa pa mngon shes nas brgyud pa la/ sgrub thabs thun mong ma yin pa/ thod pa la rten nas sgrub pa/ dbang du bya ba'i 'phrin las/ sbyin sreg la rten te sgrub pa/

pa/ grwa pa mngon shes kyis bton pa'i brgyud pa ni/ slob dpon pad ma/ grwa pa mngon shes/ grwa pa thugs rje 'bum/ shu la tsantra/ slob dpon tshul rgyal/ mkhan po nyi ma/
slob dpon don bzangs/ dbu ma pa grub brtson/ bka' bcu pa bkra shis bzang po/ blo gros bzang po/ rin po che seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / paN chen

ma 'bul ba/ tshogs 'bul ba ste thun mong gi dngos grub sgrub pa/ byin brlabs kyi cho ga rnams te/ bla ma brgyud pa gsan yig na mi bzhugs pas 'dir yang de ltar ro// ! //yang
/ jo

bo rje lha gcig gi dzambha la la rten pa'i mthun rkyen bsgrub pa'i man ngag ces bya ba/ ri khrod pa'i gces nor khyad par can cig kyang zhus so/ /'di'i yang bla ma brgyud pa
gsan yig na mi bzhugs pas 'dir yang de ltar ro/ /gong 'og 'di gnyis bdag gi bla mas bzad pa rin rgyal ba la zhus par gda'o/ ! /yang / dbyug gu ma spun gsum gyi brgyud pa
ni/ thub pa'i dbang po/ rje btsun 'jam dpal/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa chen/ slob dpon pa/ rje btsun/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ rin po che tshogs sgom/ bsod
nams brtan pa/ na za pa/ ye shes dpal/ blo gros bzang po/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal/ 'di la ba ri lo tsA ba'i thugs dam mkha' 'gro ma'i lag bcangs ma zhes bya ba dang /
de'i lag len chos dpal bzang pos sbyar ba'i lung yang thob bo/ /gzhan yang rim pa gnyis kyi man ngag mang du thob pa la/ ba ri ba'i 'bum nag gam/ rig pa'i 'bum chen mo zhes
bya ba'i mdo/ rig pa lnga bcu yod pa dang / rig pa thor bu ba bsdus pa 'bum zhes pa'am/ sna tshogs rigs pa'i 'bum chung rig pa gya lnga yod pa/ byad ma 'bum bzlog tu grags
pa la/ lo rgyus/ bsrung ba/ ngag mnan/ mtshon bsrungs/ jag chings/ nor sgrub/ tshe bsgrub/ rmi lam ngan pa bzlog pa/ bzlog pa byed lugs rnams kyang zhus so/ /'di rnams

pa'i thabs dang shes rab gtan la dbab pa grub

pa/ shanti bha tra dang / mgos 'gyur/ de gnyis la brten nas rgyal po intra bhu tis ye shes grub pa mdzad/ de la rten nas lakShis gnyis med grub pa mdzad/ DoM bhi he ru kas
lhan cig skyes grub mdzad/ des dA ri ka pa dang / tsi ro gnyis la bshad/ dA ri ka pas gsang ba de kho na'i man ngag mdzad/ tsi ros/ dngos po gsal ba'i rjes su 'gro ba'i de
kho na nyid grub pa mdzad/ snga ma snga mas/ phyi ma phyi ma'i don du mdzad/ phyi ma phyi mas/ snga ma snga ma'i gzhung dang / nyams myong la rten nas mdzad ces grag go
! /yang / snying po'i skor la/ sa ra has mdzad pa'i do ha mdzod/ klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i phyag rgya bzhi gtan la 'bebs pa/ rma can 'gyur/ de ba tsantras mdzad pa'i shes
rab ye shes gsal ba/ dharmma kirti'i 'gyur/ lhan cig skyes pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa'i gnas pa bsdus pa/ rma ban 'gyur la/ 'tshur gyis bcos pa 'di dA ri ka pas mdzad zer ba'ang
'dug ste don cig tog rtse pas mdzad pa'i bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i man ngag 'di la 'gyur byang mi 'dug ! /de ltar phyag rgya chen po grub snying gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo

'o brgyad ston chung / rtag tshal gyi zhal snga ring mo/ ba reg thos pa dga'/ bra'o 'bum la 'bar/ dge bshes gangs pa she'u/ rong pa shes 'dri mi rnams te/ phyag na la zhabs
rtog che tshad bsod nams che bar byung ste/ ba reg gis gser phul gyis gcal nas phul te/ snga ma la mkhar gzhong gang phul/ phyi ma la zangs gzhong gang phul/ ba reg sems
phyogs la mkhas pas/ snying po skor mkhas/ zhal snga ma brgyud pa yin pas/ grub bskor mkhas/ brang ti mngon pa

dang / dbu tshad pa yin pas/ aM nas la mkhas/ 'o brgyad yo ga ba yin pas/ dam rgya mkhas/ she'u ris tshogs la mkhas/ de ltar na/ brang ti las/ rtsangs yang dag 'bar/ phyug
zungs skyabs/ rtsang pa 'byung seng / lce ston mdo seng / bla ma ston shAka lce blo ldan seng ge bla ma 'phags pa yon tan rgya mtsho/ bu ston kha che/ mkhan chen byang seng
pa/ rin po che bkras rin pa/ rin po che seng ge dpal/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ ! /grub snying la rten pa'i a ma na se'i skor la/ lta ba ngan sel gnyis med rdo
rjes mdzad pa/ 'tshur ye 'byung gi 'gyur/ sngags kyi lta ba ston pa dbu ma drug pa/ mai tri pas mdzad pa nag tsho'i 'gyur/ lta ba ngan pa sel ba'i dran pa'i dka' 'grel/ gnyis
med rdo rjes mdzad pa 'tshur gyi 'gyur/ sngags kyi spyod pa ston pa lhan cig skyes grub/ 'tshur gyi 'gyur/ rmi lam nges bstan gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa nag tsho'i
'gyur/ sgyu ma nges bstan/ rab tu mi gnas pa gsal bar ston pa/ gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa nag tsho'i 'gyur/ de kho na nyid bcu pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ nag tsho 'gyur/
'dir 'tshur la 'gyur gdan byas pa/ zung 'jug rab tu gsal bar mdzad pa a wa dhU tis mdzad pa/ nag tsho 'gyur/ dga' bcugs lnga pa/ mi phyed pa lnga pa/ bde ba chen po
gsal ba rnams mai tri pas mdzad pa/ rma ban 'gyur/ thun mong gi lta ba ston pa de kho na nyid rin po che'i 'phreng ba/ gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa nag tsho 'gyur/ de kho
na nyid rab tu brtan pa/ gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa 'gyur byang med/ de bzhin gshegs pa lnga'i phyag rgya rnam par bshad pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ rma ban 'gyur/
dbang gi dgos pa mdor bsdus pa/ 'tshur gyi 'gyur/ dbang gi cho ga bsdus pa/ gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad

pa/ rang bzhin lnga pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ a mr-i de bas zhus te gsol ba btab nas brtsams zer ba'ang 'dug thabs shes rab rtse ba lnga pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa
'tshur dznyA na a ka ra'i 'gyur/ dAo ha zhes pa de kho na nyid kyi man ngag a wa dhU tis mdzad pa/ dhI ri shrI dznyA na'i 'gyur/ theg pa chen po nyi shu pa gnyis med rdo
rjes mdzad pa/ shAkya brtson 'grus kyi 'gyur/ yid la mi byed pa gnyis med rdo rjes mdzad pa/ gnyan chung gis bcos pa/ de kho na nyid theg pa chen po nyi shu pa gnyis med
rdo rjes mdzad pa/ seng dkar shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ gsang ba dam pa zhes pa'i chos tshan gcig dbang bskur nges bstan mai tri pas mdzad pa/ nag tsho'i 'gyur/ de'i dka' 'grel
slob dpon dga' ba skyong gis mdzad pa/ sa manta bha tra dang / nag tsho'i 'gyur/ de kho na nyid bcu pa'i 'grel pa lhan cig skyes pa'i rdo rjes mdzad pa/ 'tshur dznyA
na a ka ra'i 'gyur/ rdo rje'i tshig ces bya ba/ badzra pa Nis mdzad pa 'tshur gyi 'gyur/ 'di la chos sna nyi shu rtsa drug bzhugs pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / sa ra

pa/ sa paN/ 'phags pa/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ chos rje bla ma/ sa skya bu ston/ bar pug pa bzang po dpal/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /yang
/ dbu ma lugs kyi byang chub du sems bskyed pa/ chos rje sa skya pas mdzad pa'i cho ga dang / lung sbyor gyi steng nas zhus pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i
sangs rgyas/ rje btsun 'jam dpal/ byang chub sems dpa' nor bzangs/ 'phags pa klu grub/ zhi ba lha/ dze ta ri/ puNye shrI mi tra/ sa skya pa chen po/ rje btsun sku mched/
chos rje sa paN/ 'gro mgon 'phags pa/ bla chen kun blo/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o/ /gzhan yang / shes
rab snying po/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa bsdud pa/ ltung bshags/ shes spring / byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa la 'jug pa/ paN chen ma tis mdzad pa'i chos spyod
rab gsal snang ba/ chos kyi 'byung gnas gsung rab rin po che'i bang mdzod chos 'byung chen mor grags pa/ bu ston gyis mdzad pa rnams kyang zhus shing / yang / rgyal sras
rin po che'i bka' 'bum thor bu ba thob pa'i rim pa ni/ thog mar bla ma'i rnal 'byor/ bla ma la bstod pa dwang ba'i chu rgyun/ bla ma la bstod pa dad pa bskyed byed/ spang
lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pa la bstod pa/ mkhan chen bu ston pa la bstod pa/ chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa la bstod pa/ dmar khrid brgyud pa'i bla ma rnams la bstod
pa/ sum pa lo tsA'i snyan brgyud kyi bla ma rnams la bstod pa/ snying po don gsum gyi bla ma brgyud pa la bstod pa/ smon 'jug sems bskyed kyi bla ma brgyud pa la bstod pa/
dbu ma lugs kyi sems bskyed brgyud pa'i bla ma rnams la bstod pa/ byang sems

sdom brgyud kyi bla ma rnams la bstod pa/ yang byang sems sdom brgyud kyi bla ma rnams la bstod pa/ blo sbyong gi bla ma brgyud pa rnams la bstod pa/ rten 'brel snying po'i
bla ma brgyud pa rnams la bstod pa/ skyid sdug lam khyer gyi bla ma brgyud pa la bstod pa/ bcu gcig zhal gyi snyung gnas kyi bla ma brgyud pa rnams la bstod pa/ bsnyen rdzogs
kyi mkhan brgyud rnams la bstod pa/ 'jam dbyangs 'khon ston thugs rje rin chen la bstod pa/ chos la bskul ba'i gtam rin po che'i 'phreng ba/ chos la bskul ba'i gtam
rin po che'i rgyan/ dam bca' rnam gsum/ rang gi slob ma la gdams pa gnyis/ rgyal sras lag len/ rang nyid la bskul ba/ rang la gdams pa/ rang la gros 'debs ang drug yang
rang la gros 'debs/ jo bo rin po che la bstod pa/ spyan ras gzigs la bstod pa tshig rgyan me tog 'phreng ba/ thugs rje chen po la phyag 'tshal ba phan bde'i 'byung gnas/
'jam dbyangs la phyag 'tshal ba/ mgon po byams pa la bstod pa/ sgrol ma la phyag 'tshal ba/ phyag rgya chen po'i bla ma brgyud pa la bstod pa/ slob dpon zhi ba lha'i lugs
kyi smon 'jug gi sems bskyed kyi cho ga sems tsam lugs kyi smon 'jug sems bskyed kyi cho ga jo bo rje'i lugs kyi sems bskyed kyi cho ga chos spyod rab gsal/ gser gling pa
nas brgyud pa'i blo sbyong don bdun ma'i khrid yig rten 'brel snying po'i khrid yig skyid sdug lam khyer gyi khrid yig bcu gcig zhal gyi snyung gnas/ sgo yig dang po/ gnyis
pa/ gsum pa/ don zhags lha lnga'i bstod pa/ thugs rje chen po'i bsgom bzlas/ thugs rje chen po'i gtor ma/ kun rig gi sgrib sbyongs/ dzambha la/ nor rgyun ma dang bcas
pa'i mngon rtogs/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas la bstod pa/ sman bla'i

rjes gnang / byang sems bcu drug gi bstod pa/ g.yu drung dpal gyi don du mdzad pa'i yan lag bdun pa/ rtse thang pa'i gdan sa pa slob dpon chen po grags rin pa la gdams pa/
rang gi slob ma rnams la gdams pa/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa'i drung du phul ba'i zhu yig lo tsA ba byang chub rtse mo'i dris lan/ skal ldan bsod nams 'od zer la gdams pa/
slob dpon ldong ston la gdams pa/ chos blo dbon po la gdams pa gnyis/ chos kyi blo gros la gdams pa/ nad la sogs pa lam du khyer ba'i tshul/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen shAkya bsod
nams la gdams pa/ slob dpon chos mchog la phul ba gnyis/ bya bral ba nam mkha' bzang po'i dris lan/ rin po che skyob pa dpal gyi drin lan/ blo ldan blo gros dpal la gdams
pa/ rtse thang gi sngags pa seng ge rgyal mtshan la gdams pa/ mi nyag rgyal mchog 'bum la gdams pa/ snar thang phu'i bla ma po tog pa la gdams pa/ sbud skra'i rtogs
ldan bsod nams rin chen la gdams pa/ bla ma rab ston 'jam dbyangs rin chen grags la gdams pa/ rtsib ri ba slob dpon gzhon nu byang chub la gdams pa/ bsgom chen bsod rgyal
la gdams pa/ chen po bsod nams bzang po la gdams pa/ 'od zer bzang po la gdams pa/ byams chen pa'i drung du phul ba/ bla ma ri pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan la gdams pa/ shAkya
bzang po la gdams pa gnyis/ bon po khyi thul can la gdams pa/ mkhan chen gro sa pa la gdams pa/ nam mkha' rin chen dpal bzang po la gdams pa gnyis/ slob dpon nam mkha'
dpal la gdams pa gnyis/ gnas rnying pa rgyal dbang la gdams pa/ rdzogs chen pa chos nyid rgyal mtshan gyi dris lan/ dpon shAkya bzang po la gdams pa/ dge slong chos dbang
rin chen grogs

mched gnyis la gdams pa/ chos blo dbon po kun dga' rgyal mtshan la gdams pa/ shes rab grub dang / ka drug pa la gdams pa re re/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen shAkya bzang po la gdams
pa gnyis/ stag lung pa sangs rgyas dpal/ bshes gnyen nam mkha' 'grub/ dpon chen byang pa si tu bsod nams dpal/ ras rkyang pa rgyal mtshan dpal rnams la gdams pa re re/
dge ba'i bshes gnyen dpal ldan ye shes kyis bskul ba'i dam bca' dang smon lam/ dam chos sgrub pa la gces pa'i man ngag bshes gnyen rab rtse la gdams pa/ pha jo g.yu drung
dpal la gdams pa/ rten gyi dkar chag lo rgyus rgyas bsdus gnyis/ nang gi lo rgyus/ mdo sde rgyan gyi TI ka'i dbu zhabs kyi tshigs bcad/ rgyud bla ma'i TI ka'i dbu zhabs
kyi tshigs bcad/ spyod 'jug gi TI ka'i dbu zhabs kyi tshigs bcad/ zla bzangs kyi don du mdzad pa'i drang po'i gtam/ bya bral ba dpal rin gyi don du mdzad pa'i bsngo ba smon
lam/ dpon rin chen bzang po'i don du mdzad pa'i smon lam/ khams pa ma Ni ba la gdams pa/ g.yu 'di gong du ma song / drung dpal gyi don du mdzad pa'i yan lag bdun pa/ rang
la gdams pa shlau ka gcig yang gcig bkra shis kyi tshigs su bcad pa sdig pa zhi byed/ rgyal sras rin po che'i rnam par thar pa lo chen byang rtses mdzad pa/ bla ma nai
sing pas mdzad pa'i thog mtha' bar gsum du dge ba/ nyan po ba dpal rin gyis mdzad pa'i gzhan phan 'od zer/ bla ma rgya ma bas mdzad pa'i mya ngan 'das chung / thugs rje
chen po'i dmar khrid rnams kyi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos rje rgyal sras pa/ lo chen byang chub rtse mo/ rdo rje 'dzin pa shrI ma ti/ pha chos kyi rje/ des bdag la'o//

/ des bdag la'o/ ! /bla ma de las rdo rje 'jig byed kyi gtso bo'i sgrub thabs dri med snang ba rwa los mdzad pa/ rwa lo'i nyams mgur chos brgyad du grags pa/ rgya ston
gyis mdzad pa'i bsrung bzlog bsad gsum gyi man ngag rtsa zhal gsum gyi las tshogs rwa phyi mas yi ger bkod pa/ dgra nag gi TI ka rwa los mdzad pa rnams nam lhun brgyud/!
yang / 'jigs byed kyi rgyud rtog pa bzhi pa'i lung thob te/ grags don pa yan rgyud 'bum dang 'dra la/ de la rngog byang chub dpal/ des bla ma dpal ldan rgya mtsho/ brag
