lo pa/ nA ro pa/ dznya na rakShi ta/ bal po thugs rje chen po/ rwa rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ de'i sras gcen ye shes seng ge gcung dharma seng ge gcen gyi sras rwa 'bum
seng / gcung gi sras dkon mchog seng ge de'i sras shes rab rgyal mtshan/ de nas rgya ston dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ rgya ston kun dga'
brtson 'grus/ bla ma mgon po rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ 'od zer seng ge ldan ma tshul rgyal/ rgyal ba phyag na/ des brag nag pa rin rgyal/ yang na rgya ston kun
dga' brtson 'grus la mkhan dwang ma ba brtson 'grus byang chub/ bdag po bsod yon pa/ mkhan chen chos dpal bzang po/ chos rje blo gros brtan pa/ brag nag pa rin chen rgyal
mtshan/ chos rje dpal 'dzin bzang po/ des bdag

la'o////yang / shin tu gces pa'i man ngag lam 'bras glegs bam du grags pa rje btsun chen po'i dkar chag gi lugs bzhin tshang mar thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/theg chen chos kyi rgyal
po/ chos rje kun dga' rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen nam mkha' lhun bzang / brag thog pa chos rje dpal 'dzin pa'i drung / des bdag la'o/ /yang / gshed dmar lha lnga'i rdzogs
rim dpal birWa pa'i lugs kyi nyams khrid yongs su rdzogs pa dang / bdag byin gyis brlabs pa'i rim pa 'od gsal 'char ba'i byin brlabs/ rten 'brel rdzas kyi rnal 'byor gyi
byin brlabs rnams theg chen chos kyi rgyal pos mdzad pa'i yig cha'i stengs nas thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dbyangs/ gshin rje gshed/ birWa pa/ DoM bhi ba/ bram ze dpal
'dzin/ ma ti pa/ darpan A tsarYa/ glo bo lo tsA ba shes rab rin chen/ sras mchog sa pa/ mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen
pa/ chos rje bla ma/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ ta'i gu shrI yon tan rgya mtsho/ brag thog pa chos rje dpal 'dzin pa'i drung / des bdag la'o//! //theg chen chos kyi rgyal
po'i bka' 'bum gyi lung thob ste/ brtag pa gnyis pa'i TI ka dag ldan snye ma/ de'i zur 'debs dka' 'grel snye ma/ brtag gnyis le'u gsum pa nas gsungs pa'i he ru ka gsum
gyi sgrub thabs/ mtsho skyes rdo rje'i rjes su 'brangs pa'i kye rdo rje'i mngon rtogs zung 'jug rnam rol/ kye rdo rje rgyud lugs kyi mngon rtog yan lag drug pa/ DoM bhi
ba'i rjes su 'brangs pa'i kye rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga kye rdo rje rnam par rol pa bum chog rdo rje gur gyi bum pa lhag par gnas pa'i cho ga rdo rje gur gyi sbyin
bsreg gi cho ga ye shes me dpung rnam par rol pa/ lam dus kyi dbang rgyas 'bring bsdus pa len pa'i lag len bdud rtsi

snying po/ kye rdo rje mngon rtogs tshul bcu bzhi/ kye rdo rje la rten nas bshin po rjes su bzung ba'i cho ga kye rdo rje'i lag len zin bris/ birWa pa'i bsrung ba/ dus 'khor
yongs rdzogs kyi mngon rtogs/ lam mchog rab gsal sogs rgyas bsdus gsum/ dkyil mchog rab gsal snying po/ mchod phreng / sa chog gi zur 'debs zin bris mdor bsdus pa/ dus
'khor nas gsung ba'i 'khor lo sdom chen gyi sgrub thabs/ rdo rje gsum gyi sgrub pa gsal bar byed pa sgron ma'i snying po yid bzhin nor bu rin po che/ 'khor lo bde mchog lU
hi pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bde mchog rnam par rol pa/ 'khor lo bde mchog lha lnga'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga snying po bde blag tu 'jug pa/ bde mchog lha lnga'i dbang
gi tho yig dril bu lus dkyil gyi dbang gi zur 'debs/ 'khor lo bde mchog lU hi pa'i lugs kyi sbyin bsreg gi cho ga phrin las rnam par rol pa/ bde mchog lU hi pa'i dri lan
nyi 'od snang ba/ shin tu spros med kyi de kho na nyid snang bar byed pa'i rnam bshad yid bzhin gyi nor bu zin bris/ bdag byin gyis brlob pa'i cho ga ye shes rnam rol/ 'od
gsal 'char ba'i byin brlab bde gsal snying po/ rten 'brel rdzas kyi rnal 'byor gsal bar byed pa'i sgron ma/ rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rnal 'byor gyi zin bris sogs/ gshin
rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i mngon rtogs snying po gsal ba/ gshin rje gshed dmar po zhal gsum pa'i sgrub thabs khro bo rnam par rol pa/ gshin rje gshed lha bcu gsum pa'i
sgrub thabs snying po mthong bas don rab tu gsal ba/ gshin rje gshed kyi mngon rtogs/ gshin rje gshed kyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bdud rtsi'i rol mtsho/ gshed dmar gnyis pa
dgra nag gdong drug gi sbyin bsreg gi cho ga ye shes rnam rol/ dgra nag gi sgrub thabs khro bo rnam rol la nye bar

mkho ba'i zin bris nyer mkho rnam rol/ gshin rje gshed kyi bstod bskul/ gsang 'dus mi bskyod rdo rje'i mngon rtogs mthong bas don rab tu gsal ba/ gsang 'dus 'jam pa'i rdo rje'i
dkyil mchog 'jam dbyangs rnam rol/ dpal rdo rje nag po chen po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga mgon po rnam par rol pa/ mchod gtor bstod pa phyag na rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi
cho ga bde blag tu 'jug pa/ phyag na rdo rje'i 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i sgrub thabs bsdus pa/ 'chi bdag 'joms pa'i tshe'i rig pa sgrub pa'i man ngag kun rig gi cho ga gzhan
phan snye ma/ kun rig rgyun gshags kyi 'grel pa/ kun rig khor yug gi yig sna/ kun rig dang kye rdor blo blongs kyi yig sna/ dbang gi rim pa gsal bar byed pa'i sgron ma/
rdo rje dril bu'i mtshan nyid zung 'jug rab gsal snang ba/ 'jam dbyangs a ra pa tsA na'i sgrub thabs/ dpa' bo gcig sgrub kyi rgyud du 'byung ba'i lha lnga'i sgrub thabs/
'jam dbyangs kyi bstod pa dag ldan snang ba/ 'jam dbyangs kyi po bstod/ yang 'jam dbyangs kyi bstod pa/ 'jam dbyangs smra seng gi yig lan/ sgrol ma sen mo'i sgrub thabs
'chi med rgya mtsho/ so so phreng ma lha mo lnga'i sgrub thabs/ lha mo 'od zer gyi sgrub thabs/ bsam mi khyab kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i lo rgyus/ rgyud kyi bla ma brgyud pa'i
lo rgyus/ lam 'bras brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ spros med brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ dmar khrid brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs rgyas bsdus gnyis/ ne gu chos drug gi gsol 'debs/ phyag
rgya chen po'i bla ma brgyud pa'i gsol 'debs/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor/lha dang bla ma la smre sngags gsol ba/ne gu chos drug gi sngon 'gro'i khrid yig thugs rje chen po'i dmar
khrid/ mkha' 'gro ma grub pa'i rgyal mo nas brgyud pa'i tshe dpag med byang chub kyi mchog tu

sems bskyed pa'i cho ga sangs rgyas stong gi smon lam las bsdus pa/ dge bsnyen du sgrub pa'i cho ga nang gi mol ba/ phyi'i mol ba/ yang nang gi mol ba bsngo ba/ dris lan nor
bu'i phreng ba/ dge bshes kun bzang dpal la gdams pa/ dge bshes tshul khrims 'phel gyi rtogs brjod dri lan/ sgrub pa po seng ge bzang po'i dri lan snying gi nor bu rtogs
ldan chos kyi rgyal mtshan la gdams pa/ bla ma thang shing pa bsod nams rin chen gyi dri lan yid bzhin nor bu/ rtogs ldan bsod nams dpal la spring yig A tsArYa shrI badzra
la gdams pa/ stag lung pa gzhon blo la gdams pa/ dpon chen nam mkha' 'od zer la gdams pa/ bod 'bangs spyi la sprin yig gdan sa pa rnams la spring yig rgyal po la phul
ba/ tham phud/ A li kA li'i bsrung ba rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po/ ta'i gu shrI yon tan rgya mtsho/ brag thog pa chos rje dpal 'dzin pa'i drung /
des bdag la'o/! /gsang ba 'dus pa'i rdzogs rim gyi yig cha thob pa la/ bskyed rdzogs gnyis gdan thog gcig tu sgom pa la lam rtags dang 'brel ba'i gdams ngag don lnga ma/
don bzhi ma dang rim lnga stan gcig gi steng du bsgom pa'i man ngag 'khor lo can dang / 'khor lo med pa dang / srog rtsol la brten nas/ gtum mo bsgom pa lam rim pa lnga
dang sbyar ba dang / rim lnga sems dpa' sum rtseg gi gdams pa dang / 'khor ba 'jug zlog la brten nas ma rig pa rtsad nas bcad pa dang / skye 'chi la brten nas grong 'jug
gis le lo can 'chi kar sangs rgya ba'i man ngag dang / mnyam gzhag sgyu ma'i man ngag rmi lam sgyu ma'i man ngag bar do sgyu ma'i man ngag sku gsum gyi 'pho ba'i man ngag
btsan thabs su 'pho ba'i man ngag chags can 'og sgo la brten nas bde ba lam du

blang ba'i man ngag sre ba drug gi man ngag rdo rje sems dpa'i bsegs lam/ sdig po che btsan thabs su sangs rgya ba'i man ngag mgrin par rmi lam la brten nas sgyu ma btsan thabs
su bzung ba'i man ngag snying khar mi shigs pa'i thig le la brten nas ma rig pa rtsad nas bcad pa'i man ngag rim lnga cig char ba'i man ngag gsang ba thugs brgyud kyi
rim lnga'i man ngag da lta nyid nas 'bras bu sangs rgyas kyi bzhugs tshul gtan la dbab pa/ pha rgyud yang snying / ma rgyud yang snying rnams gser sdings pa gzhon nu 'od
kyis mdzad pa dang / gsang 'dus rig lnga'i khrid yig grags chen pas mdzad pa/ dbang gong ma'i cho ga dang / ngo sprod yu mo khugs gnyis kun mkhyen 'phags 'od kyis mdzad
pa rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/gser sdings pa gzhon nu 'od/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin po che/ lo chen byang rtse/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/
red mda' ba gzhon nu blo gros/ bla ma don dpal ba/ byang sems shAkya dhwa dza/ brag thog pa chos rje dpal 'dzin pa'i drung / des bdag la'o/! /yang / bu ston rin po
che'i bka' 'bum gyi steng nas/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud 'grel gyi bshad thabs kyi yan lag gsang ba'i sgo 'byed/ mdor byas kyi rgya cher bshad pa skyed rim gsal byed/ sgron
ma rab tu gsal bar byed pa'i bshad sbyar mtha' drug rab gsal/ de'i bsdus don nyung gsal rim lnga'i dmar khrid kyi man ngag yid bzhin nor bu rin po che'i za ma tog rnams

drung / des bdag la'o/ /yang sgrol ma dmar mos 'gro ba dbang du bya ba'i man

yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ 'jam pa'i nga ro/ dpe med rdo rje/ seng ge rdo rje/ pad ma rdo rje'i myu gu zhabs/ intra bhu ti phyi ma/ rgyal po la gri mo/ snang ba'i rdo
rje/ yul dbus kyi bu mo gsang ba'i rdo rje/ o Te sha'i rgyal po bi su kalpa/ yul dbus kyi rgyal rigs sa ra ha pa/ dri med snying po/ grub pa'i ye shes/ sangs rgyas ye shes
zhabs/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ de la u rgyan gyi slob dpon yon tan 'byung gnas kyis gsol ba btab pa'i ngor/ ko sa la'i rgyan mdzad/ de nas/ shrAddha ka ra/ bu ston gsan yig
na/ shraddha/ man dpyad par bya gsung / 'di la kun snying bzhag nas shAkya bshes gnyen 'jug pa yin zhes rtsa skya pa gsung ngo // buddha shrI shInti/ lo chen/ lo chung
/ gnyal nyi/ gnur nyi/ sras badzra singha / glan chos 'byung / rtsa skya ston 'bum/ khri brtan/ gnur ye rgyal/ chos rgyal/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu
bsod nams/ ratna shrI/ tsaNDa shrI/ ye shes rgya mtsho/ thams cad mkhyen pa byams pa gling pa/ des bdag la'o// ! //yang na/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rab gsal zla ba/
rab 'byor skyangs/ 'di la kun snying bzhag nas/ shAkya bshes gnyen 'jug pa yin zhes rtsa skya pa gsung ngo /kun snying / pra dznyA wa li ta/ pra dznyA

boddhi/ mu ti ko Sha/ shraddha ka ra man sngar bzhin no// ! //de nyid 'dus pa'i 'grel pa a wa ta ra'i brgyud pa ni/ sa chen/ bshen rdor seng / dbus pa dbang phyug grags/ ldong
ston shes rab dpal/ dpal 'byor bzang po/ rtsa skya khri brtan/ gnur ye rgyal/ gnur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin po che/ khyung po lha
pa/ ratna shrI dang gcigdpal mi bskyod rdo rje/ tsandra shrI sogs sngar bzhin no/ /khams gsum rnam rgyal gyi dkyil chog slob dpon kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa'i lung gi brgyud
pa ni/ gnur chos rgyal yan rdo rje 'byung ba dang 'dra ba las/ de nas rgyal sras thogs med/ bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston/ dbang
rnon pa/ tsandra shrI/ slob dpon rin po che ye shes rgya mtsho/ dpal byams pa gling pa/ des bdag la'o// 'di'i brgyud pa ni gnur pa'i brgyud yig 'ga' re la tshul gcig par
snang bas brtag gsung ngo // ! //kun dga' snying pos mdzad pa'i spyan dbye'i cho ga dang / yang rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga sbyin bsreg kun bzangs/ pra dznyA wa li tas mdzad
pa'i spyan dbye'i cho ga ye shes rdo rjes mdzad pa'i thugs rje 'byung ba'i sgom bzlas/ rab 'byor skyangs kyi mdzad pa'i sbyin bsreg rnams kyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ kun dga'
snying po/ pra dznyA wa li ta/ pra dznyA boddhi/ mukti ko Sha/ shrAddha ka ra/ lo chen/ skyang po chos blo/ sum ston ye 'bar/ lce zhar ba/ spru ston 'bar thog rtsangs
yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs smra seng / lce jo mdo/ bla ma chos 'od/ lce blo ldan seng ge 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ ratna shrI/ tsantra pa/ ye shes rgya mtsho/ dpal byams pa gling
pa/ des bdag la'o// ngan song yongs su sbyong ba gtsug tor dgu pa'i dkyil chog kun snying gi mdzad pa thos pa'i smad lugs

kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ rab gsal ba/ de'i slob ma chos mchog bzhi ni/ sad dkar ye shes/ ye shes rdo rje/ rgyal po sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po/ nyi ma'i shing
rta ste/ de bzhis rgyal rigs sa ra ha pa/ kun snying / tha ga na pa/ ngag dbang grags pa/ ba lendra pa/ shAnti pa/ mi bskyod rdo rje/ shraddha ka ra/ lo chen/ lo chung
/ sum ston ye 'bar/ gnyan tshul 'bar/ thod pa dben tsha grags/ dge bshes jo phur/ thod pa 'od zer/ rong pa chos mgon/ lce blo ldan seng ge 'phags 'od/ bu ston/ slob dpon
dpal mchog tsandra pa sogs so/ /stod lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ kun snying / pra dznyA wa li ta/ go mi dge bsnyen/ shAkya dznyA na/ jo bo rje go mi sgom chen/ kyi nor dznyA na/
gnyal nyi/ gnur nyi/ gtum ston grags/ rtsa skya mnyam khad pa chen po/ khri brtan/ sras bsod bzangs/ de gnyis ka la gsal ba blo gros dpal/ bla ma grags chen pa/ 'phags
'od sogs so// //yang na/ gnur nyi nas/ stag tshal gdong sngon gyi spru ston 'bar thog rong smad lha stengs kyi rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ de'i sras smra seng / lce mdo seng
/ chos 'od/ blo ldan seng ge 'phags 'od sogs so// ! //'jam dpal mtshan brjod rnal 'byor rgyud du 'grel ba la/ lugs che ba gsum las/ dang po/ rje btsun 'jam dpal bshes
gnyen gyi lugs/ nam mkha' dri med chung bar grags pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang rdzogs pa dang / 'grel pa/ dbugs dbyung lnga la sogs pa'i gzhung tshang ma/ chos
kyi rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ nA ro pa/ rkan dbang phyug
blo gros/ mgar ston rdo rje snying

po/ nyang stod lce 'bar/ la chog pa/ khri ston kun dga' 'od zer/ mkhan po chos rin/ bla ma chos 'od/ 'phags 'od/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ khyung po lhas pa gzhon nu bsod
nams/ bla ma bkra shis rin chen/ ngor pa kun dga' bzang po/ dmar ston rgyal mtshan 'od zer/ dpal byams pa gling pa/ des bdag la'o// ! //'grel pa bar pa sgeg pa rdo rjes
mdzad pa'i lugs la/ dkyil chog yon tan 'byung gnas dang / gsang ldan gyi lugs gnyis las/ dang po'i lugs ltar/ rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba dang / gzhung
rnams dang / chos kyi rje nyid kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog shi ba la phan gdags pa'i cho ga rnams kyi lung dang bcas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ 'jam dpal
bshes gnyen/ sgeg pa'i rdo rje/ nyi ma'i snying po/ surYa singha / chos kyi rdo rje/ mu dra siddhi/ de we shwa ra/ smri ti dznyA na kIrti/ tshong sde ngag gi dbang phyug
khams pa shes rab rdo rje/ rngog chos rdor/ sba sba ba can/ rngog mdo sde/ tsangs smra seng / lce mdo seng / bla ma chos 'od/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin po che/
khyung po lhas pa/ phar chen pho so la/ 'di bla 'dags rin mtshan dngos bkra shis rin chen/ ngor pa kun dga' bzang po/ dmar ston sogs so// //yang na/ rngog chos rdor/ rgya
ma can/ bla ma shAkya seng ge khri ston/ kun dga' 'od/ mkhan po chos rin/ chos 'od/ 'phags 'od sogs so/ ! /yang na/ rngog chos rdor/ ram rtsan can/ dmar jo bo/ mkhas pa
bsod rgyal/ gye re lha zur ba/ g.yar nam mkha' bzang po/ bla ma gzhon nu seng ge bla ma chos kyi mgon po/ khyung po lhas pa sogs so// //lugs gnyis pa gsang ldan gyi lugs

kyi/ 'grel pa che ba rje btsun 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa'i lugs/ dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga chos kyi dbyings gsung gi dbang phyug nam mkha' dri med che bar grags pa'i lugs kyi
'grel gzhung gi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ bla ma rnam rgyal ba/ slob dpon tsantra ba/ slob dpon rin po che ye shes rgya mtsho/ rje thams
cad mkhyen pa byams pa gling pa/ des bdag la'o// ! //'di'i bu ston yan/ dbang brgyud ltar yin nam brtag 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa'i snying po rgyan gyi brgyud pa'ang
'di nyid do/ /rwa lugs kyi mgon po mngon byung lha drug gi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bo dong thams cad mkhyen pa 'jigs med pa/ dpal byams pa gling pa/ des bdag
la stsal to/ /bo dong pa yan stsal to// ! //gu ru drag po'i dbang gi brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku thugs rje chen po/ sprul sku pad ma 'byung gnas/
mnga' bdag myang ral pa can/ sras mchog 'gro mgon/ rta so 'gro mgon/ gnyan chen ras pa/ kun mkhyen dri med 'od zer/ 'khrul zhig sangs rgyas dbon/ thams cad mkhyen pa byams
pa gling pa/ des bdag la'o// //bya rgyud kyi skor la/ tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dze tA ri'i lugs kyi dbang gi brgyud pa ni// 'di btsal bar bya'o/ //gtsug tor rnam rgyal
lha mangs sum grags pa'i dbang gi brgyud pa ni/ sngar gyi gdan bzhi lha mangs kyi brgyud pa dang 'dra ba/ 'di'i sgrub dkyil/ gzungs 'grel/ bya rgyud spyi'i bum chog rnams/
rje thams cad mkhyen pa'i zhal snga nas mdzad pa'i lung yang thob bo// //gtsug tor rnam rgyal gyi gzungs kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ byams pa/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/

rakShi ta/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ sa chen/ rje btsun sa paN/ spyi lung pa/ rgan mo lhas pa/ ston pa dar shAka cung pa bsod dbang / lo mchog bag ston/ tshul rgyal/ gnyal pa bde legs/
rin po che bsod nams bzang po/ rin po che seng ge dpal/ dpal byams pa gling pa/ des bdag la'o// ! //bsrung ba lnga'i dbang gi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo
rje/ dze tA ri/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung / ba ri lo tsA ba/ gnyan ston grags/ gnyan rin chen grags/ gnas brtan dkon seng / rtogs ldan bya'u rgyal/ bla ma rgyal tsha/ blo

na/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ gnyag dbon bsod nams bzang po/ dpal byams pa gling pa sogs so// ! //rje dus zhabs pa la gsan pa'i skor bzhugs/ yang gro lung pa blo gros/
'byung gnas kyi bstan rim chen mo thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dpal ldan A ti sha/ rngog legs pa'i shes rab/ rngog blo ldan shes rab/ 'di yan ma bris kyang chog dge bshes gro

btsun kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po la'o// //mdo ting nge 'dzin rgyal po'i 'grel pa grags pa'i phreng ba zhes bya ba/ 'jam dpal grags pas mdzad pa thob pa'i brgyud
pa

ni/ bha ga wAn shrI shAkya mu ni/ shrI manydzu gho Sha/ ArYa nA gardzu na/ zla ba grags pa/ ArYa bha bya kIrti/ ArYa manydzu kIrti/ rje btsun bA gi shwa ra kIrti/ rje btsun
gser gling pa shrI dharmA kIrti/ rje btsun tai lo pa pradznyA bha dra/ dpal nA ro pa chen po/ ma hA stha bi ra shrI shAnti mi dra/ ma hA paNDi ta a bhyA ka ra gupta/ pUrNa
paNDi ta shu bha a ka ra gupta/ mu nendra shrI bha dra/ sgra gcan 'dzin dpal bzang po/ chag chos rje dpal/ bla brang pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ bla brang pa blo gros dpal/
bla brang pa bzang po dpal/ bla ma nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ rin po che bsod nams dpal 'byor/ dus 'khor ba don grub kun dga'/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang na/ A bhyA ka ra nas/
ngag gi dbang phyug sbas pa/ buddha shrI dznyA na/ nyi ma'i dbang po/ chag lo man chad 'dra/ ! /bde mchog sdom 'byung gi 'grel pa pad ma can gyi brgyud pa ni/ ratna rakShi
ta/ ma na ka shrIH chag chos rje dpal/ bla brang pa gzhon nu dpal/ bla brang pa blo gros dpal/ bla brang pa bzang po dpal/ bla brang pa nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ bla brang pa

chos rjes/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ ratna shrI/ ka lya na shanti/ ma ti/ ba ni ta bha dra/ bhU mi shrI/ bi ma la shrIH shongs blo brtan/ bde ba can pa seng
rgyal/ g.yung ston pa/ shes rdor ba/ de gnyis ka la grags tshul ba/ byang seng pa/ sa bzangs pa/ kun bzangs/ dmar ston/ rje thams cad mkhyen pa byams pa gling pa/ don
grub kun dga'/ des bdag go ! /dus 'khor gyi dbang thob pa'i brgyud yig dus go dang bcas pa gtor bas/ 'bri rgyu// ! //paN

po/ bzang po/ rnam rgyal/ dus zhabs pa che ba/ dus zhabs chung ba/ shAkya seng ge rgyal mtshan/ nyi ma'i 'od/ go tam dpal/ rin chen bkra shis/ rgyal ba'i rgyan/ blo ldan
rje/ shAkya bsrung ba/ rje chen po legs skyes/ dpal sangs rgyas dbyangs/ dpal nags kyi rin chen zhabs/ des so// ! //dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du

rdo rje/ chos kyi dbang phyug mA

ra kaNDa de wa/ sa 'dzin/ dpal gyi bshes gnyen/ chos kyi grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rin chen grags/ dpal nags kyi rin chen/ des so/ ! /'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi don dam pa'i mtshan
yang dag par brjod pa'i rgyud phan yon dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das shAkya thub pa/ dbang po'i gtsug rgyan/ pad ma'i rje/ mkhas pa'i rje/ sangs rgyas ye
shes/ legs skyes/ bkra shis blo ldan/ phyogs grol/ chos kyi mtsho/ ye shes rgya mtsho/ chos kyi rgyan/ srid pa'i dpung gcig grags pa'i rdo rje/ chos grags/ sangs rgyas dbyangs/
dpal nags kyi rin chen/ des so/ /bzang spyod dang / sgrol ma gnyis la/ de dang de'i lung yang thos gsung ba tsam las/ brgyud rings bgrangs pa mi snang / byang chub
sems bskyed kyi brgyud pa ni/ btsal bar bya'o/ ! dzi nA pA ri rgyal ba tshe dpag med/ mi tA yuH garbha pA daH snying po zhabs/ dze tA ri paH dgra las rgyal ba/ pu dznyA
naH ye shes bzang po/ dhya na pra dznyAH bsam gtan shes rab/ padma shaH mchog gi bsam pa/ rA ga badzraH chags pa'i rdo rje/ ga dza gho ShaH glang po'i dbyangs/ A nanda pA

chos dpal/ dznyA na sA ka raH ye shes rgya mtsho/ shrI dharmA rA dzaH chos dpal rgyal mtshan/ shrI ba na ratnaH dpal nags kyi rin po che/ tatma ma neH de bdag la/ 'di ni

@/ /mtshungs med chos kyi rje/ rdo rje slob dpon rin po che ye shes rgya mtsho'i drung du bka' lung thob yigdpal ldan mchog gi dang po'i rdo rje sems/ /'gro ba 'di yi rdo rje
slob dpon phyir/ /ngur smrig 'dzin pa'i tshul bzung chos kyi rje/ /rgya mtsho'i mtha' can bla ma'i zhabs la 'dud/ /gang gi thugs ni snying rje'i stobs ldan rnam dag mkhyen
pas chos kun gzigs/ /rgyal ba'i chos gter gsang ba'i mdzod 'dzin gzhan gyi don la dga' mgur spyod/ /srid bzhi'i dpal gyur phrin las lhun grub ma rungs bdud kyi yul las
'das/ /rgyal ba'i ye shes rgya mtshor myur 'jug mtshungs med bla ma la phyag 'tshal/ /thugs brtse gser gyi sa gzhi rab brtan zhing / /ye shes zab mo'i gting mtha' dpag
dka' bar/ /yon tan nor bu'i gter gyi rab gang ba/ /bla ma rgya mtsho'i dpal gyi bdag skyongs shig /ces bsngags par 'os pa dag la mchod par brjod de/ dus gsum sangs rgyas
thams cad kyi ngo bo/ snyigs dus kyi thub pa rdo rje 'chang gnyis pa/ don gyi lnga bcu pa las/ de nas mtshan smos brjod nas ni ming mthar zhal snga ldan par bya ces so//
slad du mtshan nas smos te/ chos kyi rje mtshungs med ye shes rgya mtsho'i zhal snga nas/ bdag cag la thugs brtse bas nye bar dgongs te/ smin grol gyi lam rgya chen po bkod
pa'i rim pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das dpal 'khor lo sdom pa lha drug cu rtsa bzhi/ grub chen lU hi pa'i lugs/ chos rje bu ston gyi mdzad pa'i mngon dkyil gyis stengs nas dbang
bzhi yongs su rdzogs par bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha ba ri pa/ lU hi pa/ dA ri ka pa/ rdo rje

dril bu pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ dzA landha ra pa/ nag po spyod pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam rgyal zhabs/ te lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa sku mched/ klog kya shes rab rtsegs/ mal lo tsA
ba/ bla ma sa skya pa chen po snying po'i zhabs/ slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo/ rje btsun chen po grags pa'i mtshan can/ rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'u yug bsod seng
/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin po che/ chos rje lo tsA ba/ rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags
pa rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med ye shes rgya mtsho/ de'i thugs rjes bdag mthu btsun kun dga' rnam par rgyal ba la'o/ /de dag ni sa skya pa nas brgyud pa yin la/ brgyud
pa chu bo drug lus la sogs pa rgyas par bu ston gsan yig las rtogs par nus so// ! //gsang ba 'dus pa 'jig rten dbang phyug gi gtso bo byas pa lha bcu dgu'i sgrub thabs/ jo
bo rjes lha btsun byang chub 'od kyi don du mdzad pa dang / dkyil chog 'jam rdor gyi dkyil chog bu ston rin po ches mdzad pa'i stengs nas/ de nyid kyi dbang bzhi yongs

gzi ba don grub mgon/ bar thang pa yab sras/ dar ma shAkya/ bsod nams dbang phyug lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ ku mA ra pra bha/ kirti shrI bha dra/ kun mkhyen 'phags pa/ bu ston
rin po che/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon rin po che/ des bdag la'o// //bcom ldan 'das rdo rje 'jigs byed dpa' bo gcig pa
mtshan ma bzhi bcus bskor ba'i sgrub thabs drag po bdud 'joms lo

rin pas mdzad pa dang / dkyil chog snying po mdor bsdus bu rin po ches mdzad pa'i steng nas dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / ye shes
kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ A tsarYa la li ta badzra/ a mo gha badzra/ ye shes 'byung gnas sbas pa/ pad ma badzra/ dI paM kA ra/ rwa lo tsA ba rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa ye
shes seng ge rwa 'bum seng / rje btsun rgwa lo/ bla ma shes rab seng ge bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston thams cad mkhyen pa/ lo tsA ba rin rnam pa/ rin po che grags rgyal
ba/ slob dpon rin po che'i zhal snga nas/ des bdag la'o/ /bsgrub dkyil gyi lung yang thob bo/ /yang na/ rje btsun rgwa lo nas/ 'gro ba'i mgon po 'phags pa rin po che/ bla
ma zhang dkon mchog dpal/ dga' ldan pa kun bsod/ gu ru dpal ldan seng ge man gong bzhin no/ /gang la mkhyen brtse'i snying po dang ldan gzhan phan ze'u 'bru'i phreng bas
gtams/ /blo gros yon tan 'dab ma rab rgyas tshul khrims dag pa'i dog pas 'khyud/ /mi zad chos kyi sbrang rtsi'i ro yis bskal bzang bung ba'i tshogs bsdud pa/ /dpal ldan
bla ma chu skyes de ni bdag yid dang mtshor 'bral med mdzod/ /lhag par yang / rnal 'byor rgyud kyi chos tshul la bka' drin mtshungs pa ma mchis pa chos kyi rje rin po che
de las/ dpal de kho na nyid bsdus pa rnal 'byor chen po rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi dum bu dang po las gsungs pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs/ rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen
po rtsa ba'i lha sum cu rtsa bdun/ bskal bzangs kyi sems dpa' dgu brgya dgu bcu rtsa drug dang bcas pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du slob dpon chen po kun dga' snying
po'i dkyil chog lugs su dbang thob pa'i smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ rab gsal zla ba/ sgra

gcan 'dzin/ dpa' bo rta pha la/ ye shes rdo rje/ pra dznyA siddhi dang bzhis kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA bA li ta/ pra dznyA boddhi/ mukti ko Sha/ shrAddha ka ra/ lo chen
rin bzang / skyang po chos blo/ sum ston ye 'bar/ lce zhar ba/ spru ston 'bar thog rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs smra seng / lce jo mdo/ bla ma chos 'od/ bla ma 'phags
'od/ bu ston rin po che/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med ye shes rgya mtsho/ des bdag mthu btsun kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal
bzang po la'o/ ! /stod lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad/ badzra satwa/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ pra kA ra tsantra/ rab gsal zla ba/ rA hU la/ sgra gcan
'dzin/ dpa' bo rta pha la/ dznyA na badzra/ ye shes rdo rje/ pra dznyA siddhiH de bzhi ka la A nanda garbha/ kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA ba li ta/ su bhU ti pa li ta/
rab 'byor skyangs/ dharmA pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ gur shing brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ mnur nyi ma 'od zer/ rtsa skya/ ston grags/
slob dpon shAkya 'bum/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston chos rje/ yang / ! su bhu ti pa li ta nas/ rab 'byor skyangs/ pra
dznyA boddhi/ mukti ko Sha/ grol ba'i mdzod/ dharma pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ gur shing brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ mnur nyi ma 'od zer/
rtsa skya ston grags/ mnyam gad pa rgya gar 'phan/ slob dpon shAkya 'bum/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu
ston rin po che/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med ye shes rgya mtsho/ de'i thugs rjes bdag mthu btsun

kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po la'o// ! //yang / rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bskur ba'i cho ga shin tu rgyas pa/ 'grel chen de nyid snang ba'i dgongs
pa/ 'grel pa lugs su grags pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du chog dbang rgyas par thob pa'i smad lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad/ badzra satwa/
rdo rje sems dpa'/ badzra pA Ni/ phyag na rdo rje/ rA dza pra kA sha tsantra/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ rA hU la/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ dpa' bo rta pha la/ dzA na badzra/ ye
shes rdo rje/ pra dznyA siddhi/ tata tsa tu rA nanda garbha/ de bzhis sa kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA ba li ta/ pra dznyA boddhi/ mukti ko Sha grol ba'i mdzod/ sangs rgyas
zhi ba/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ de gnyis ga la/ skyang po chos kyi blo gros/ sum ston ye 'bar/ lce zhar ba/ stag tshal gdong sngon gyi
spru ston 'bar thog rong lha stengs kyi rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs ston smra ba'i seng ge lce ston rdo rje seng ge mag dge stings pa kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/
kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ yang / rdo rje 'chang / badzra pA Ni/ phyag rdor/ ma hA indra boddhi/ indra boddhi che ba/ indra boddhi bar pa/ alpendra boddhi/ indra boddhi chung
ba/ nA gardzu na/ klu sgrub/ nA ga boddhi/ klu byang / dznyA na badzra/ ye shes rdo rje/ o Ta ya na bA dI tsu Da ma Ni A nanda garbha/ o Ta ya na gtsug gi nor bu'i kun dga'
snying po/ pra dhA tu mi dra/ rab dbyings bshes gnyen/ pad ma kA ra warmA/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes
rab/ klog kya ba/ spyang tshang ston tshe dang / jo she/ gnyis kyis gsan/ rtsangs/ gnyis la/ yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs ston smra ba'i seng ge lce mdo sde seng ge kun mkhyen
chos sku 'od zer/ lce blo ldan seng ge kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ yang / stod lugs kyi brgyud

pa ni/ bha ga wan bai ro tsA na/ bcom ldan 'das rnam par snang mdzad/ badzra satwa/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ rA dza pra kA sha tsandra/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ ra hU la bha dra/
sgra gcan 'dzin/ A nanda garbha/ kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA bA li ta/ shes rab skyangs/ dharmA pA la/ lo chen/ gur shing brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes
rab/ mnur nyi ma 'od zer/ rdo rje seng ge glan chos 'byung / rtsa skya ston 'bum/ rtsa skya khri brtan/ mnur ye shes rgyal mtshan/ mnur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ kun
mkhyen 'phags 'od/ de ltar tha dad nas brgyud de/ chos rje bu ston/ lo tsA ba rin rnam pa/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ yongs su 'dzin pa chen po ye shes rgya mtsho'i
zhabs/ des bdag yo ga ba kun dga' rnam par rgyal ba la'o// ! //dpal de kho na nyid 'dus pa'i dum bu gnyis pa las gsungs pa rdo rje'i rigs khams gsum las rnam par rgyal
ba/ rtsa ba'i lha sum cu so bdun/ mchod pa'i lha mo so gnyis/ bskal bzang khro bo dgu brgya dang dgu cu rtsa drug phyi rol rdo rje'i rigs lha bzhi bcu rtsa bzhi dang bcas
pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sambho ga kA ya bai ro tsA na/ longs sku rnam par snang mdzad/ nirmA Na kA
ya badzra satwa/ sprul sku rdo rje sems dpa'/ badzra pA Ni/ phyag na rdo rje/ rA dza pra kA sha tsandra/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ rA hU la/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ A nanda garbha/
kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA ba li ta/ dharmA pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ mang nang pa gur shing brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ mnur nyi
ma 'od zer/ sras badzra singha / glan chos 'byung / rtsa skya ston 'bum/ bla ma khri brtan/ mnur ye shes rgyal mtshan/ mnur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ rgyal sras thogs med
bzang po dpal/ chos rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pa thams

cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ bu ston chos kyi rje/ thugs sras rin rnam pa/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje'i slob dpon chen po ye shes rgya mtsho'i zhabs/
des bdag cag la'o// ! //bshad rgyud rdo rje rtse mo nas gsungs pa'i/ rtse mo'i rigs thams cad bsdus pa gsang ba mchod chen gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor/ gzhi dkyil sgo
nyis sbag dbus dkyil la rnam snang lha sum cu rtsa gsum/ shar du sangs rgyas gzugs can lha so gsum/ lhor sangs rgyas nyi ma lha so gsum/ nub du sangs rgyas sna tshogs gzugs
can lha so gsum/ byang du sangs rgyas chos 'dzin rgyal po lha so gsum/ shar lhor zla ba'i dkyil 'khor la rdo rje sems dpa' lha lnga/ lho nub du pad ma'i dkyil 'khor
la pad ma'i sems dpa' lha lnga/ nub byang du nam mkha'i dkyil 'khor la rin chen sems dpa' lha lnga/ byang shar du utpa la'i dkyil 'khor la rdo rje las lha lnga/ gzhi dkyil
nang ma'i grwa bzhir 'byung bzhi'i lha bzhi/ gzhi dkyil phyi ma'i grwa bzhir mchod lha nyi shu/ sgo bzhir sgo ba nyi shu/ 'jig rten pa bzhi bcu zhe drug bskal bzang dgu
brgya dgu cu go drug dang bcas pa'i dkyil 'khor du/ dkyil 'khor so sor 'jug pa'i dbang bskur ba rgyas par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad/ badzra
pA Ni/ phyag na rdo rje/ badzra dharma/ rdo rje chos/ ma hA indra bo dhi/ indra bo dhi che ba/ ha ya ba ra bi na shrI/ mi gsal/ ma dhya indra bhU ti/ indra bhU ti bar ma/
a llendra boddhi/ indra boddhi chung ba/ bha gi hi lakShmi ka ra/ bcom ldan ma lakShmi ka ra/ rA dza pu drA ra hU/ rgyal po'i sras sgra gcan/ la bha dra/ bzang po/ pA
dhU ddI pa/ legs pa'i sgron ma/ nA gardzu na/ klu sgrub/ ArYa de wa/ 'phags pa lha/ nA ga bo dhi/ klu'i byang chub/ dharmA badzra/ chos kyi rdo rje/ padma badzra/ pad ma
rdo rje/ dznyA na badzra/ ye shes rdo rje/ A nanda garbha/ kun

dga' snying po/ de la slob ma rgya gar shar phyogs/ lho phyogs dbus 'gyur 'chang dang srol gsum byung ba'i shar phyogs pa ni/ bhikShu a mo gha pA sha/ dge slong a mo gha pA
sha/ yo gi ni ka pA la ba ti/ rnal 'byor ma thod pa can/ ma Ni dI pa su kho badzra/ nor bu gling pa bde ba'i rdo rje/ bhi ka ma la wa ti/ brahma ratna badzra/ bram ze rin
chen rdo rje/ kasmi ra dznyA na shrIH kha che dznyA na shrI/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba 'phags pa shes rab/ lho phyogs pa ni pra dznyA siddhiH pra dznyA wa mi ta/ pu bhu ri pa
li ta/ rab 'byor skyangs/ shrAddha ka ra/ pad ma kA ra/ dznyA na shrIH zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ dbus 'gyur 'chang ba ni/ tha ga na/ bA gI shwa ra/ brahma ratna badzra/ bram
ze rin chen rdo rje/ kasmi ra dznyA nA shrI/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ de ltar zangs dkar ba la brgyud nas/ gnyan ston tshul 'bar/ thod pa dben tsha
grags/ thod pa 'od zer/ gtsang rong ri lung phug pa chos mgon bzang po/ sri'u chung pa lce blo ldan seng ge kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ chos rje bu ston/ bu ston gsan yig bzhir
bzhag na 'di phan gyi brgyud pa ni/ gdong ston mdo'i bshad rgyud yan gyi dbang rgyud min no/ /des na dus phyis kyi bla ma mang po'i gsan yig la 'di dbang brgyud la bris
pa 'di 'thad snyam/ yang / shAkya thub pa/ ganggA dha ra/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ mnur nyi ma 'od zer/ bla ma shAkya 'bum/ khri brtan/ bsod nams
bzang po/ bla ma grags chen pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ mkhan chen bu rin po che/ yang / yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ badzra garbha/ rdo rje snying po/ pra ka sha
tsandra/ rab gsal zla ba/ rA hU la bha dra/ sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po/ A nanda garbha/ kun dga' snying po/ bA gi shwa ra kIrti/ ngag dbang grags pa/ a kSho bhya badzra/
mi bskyod rdo rje/ ba menta pa/ ratnA kI ra shanti/ bhi ka ma la wa ti/ bram ze kA ra wa ti zer/ shrAddha kA ra warmA/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes
rab/ shangs kyi sum

ston yes 'bar/ gnyan tshul khrims 'bar/ thod pa dben tsha grags/ jo phur gnyis la mkhas pa 'od zer grags/ rong pa chos mgon/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma
dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin po che/ de ltar brgyud pa tha dad pa rnams bu ston chos rjes gsan nas/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rje
ye shes rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang na/ sangs rgyas/ rdo rje snying po/ indra boddhi che ba/ bi na shrI/ indra boddhi bar pa/ lcam lakShmi kA ra/ padma badzra/ klu
sgrub/ ArYa de wa/ nA ga boddhi/ dge slong a mo gha pA shA/ rnal 'byor ma kA ma la ba ti/ nor bu gling pa/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ briM ka ra wa ti/ rin chen rdo rje/ kha che
dznyA na shrI/ zangs dkar sum ston ye 'bar ba man sngar bzhin/ yang na/ bde ba'i rdo rje nas/ dpa' bo rdo rje/ lo chen man sngar bzhin no/ /dpal mchog shes rab kyi pha rol
tu phyin pa'i rgyud kyi dum bu dang po las gsungs pa/ dpal mchog rigs bsdus pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po gzhi dkyil sgo nyis sbag la sgo bsrungs 'khor los bsgyur ba brgyad/
nang dkyil dbus mar rdo rje sems dpa' lha so gsum/ 'jig rten pa zhe bzhi/ shar mar hU~M mdzad lha dgu/ 'jig rten pa zhe gnyis/ mtshams ma bzhi/ lho mar nam snying lha dgu/
mtshan ma brgyad/ nub mar spyan ras gzigs lha bcu bdun/ shar lhor 'jam dpal lha dgu mtshan ma brgyad/ lho nub tu nam mkha' mdzod lha bcu gsum/ mtshan ma bzhi/ nub byang
du rdo rje 'khor lo lha bcu gsum/ de'i grwa bzhir yang shar lhor zhi ba mdung / lho nub tu ming po gsum/ nub byang du sring mo bzhi/ byang shar du nag po chen po rnams
kyi dkyil 'khor ro/ /lha grangs gzhi dkyil gyi 'jig rten pa bzhi'i lta bu/ byang shar

du gnod sbyin lha dgu mtshan ma bcu gnyis/ phyi ma'i shar lhor zhi ba mdung gi dkyil 'khor du/ dbang phyug gtso 'khor sum cu tham pa yi ge dang bcas pa/ lho nub tu ma mo'i
dkyil 'khor du nag po chen po gtso 'khor lha bcu gsum/ nub byang du/ ming po gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du rgyal bar byed pa gtso 'khor bcu gcig byang shar du sring mo bzhi'i dkyil
'khor du sring mo bzhi mtshan ma bzhi dang bcas pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ ! /dbang yang dag par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ buddha bai ro tsA na/ sangs rgyas rnam
par snang mdzad/ badzra pA Ni/ phyag rdor/ ra bI shrIH nyi ma'i dpal/ badzra warmA/ rdo rje go cha/ A nanda garbha/ kun snying / manydzu shrI bi ma la kIrti/ 'jam dpal
dri med grags pa/ su bhu ti pa li ta/ rab 'byor skyangs/ shrAddha kA ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ skyang po chos kyi blo gros/ sum
ston yes 'bar/ lce zhar ba/ spru ston pa/ 'bar thog rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ rtsangs smra seng / lce jo mdo/ bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston rin
po che/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon rin po che/ des bdag la'o// ! //yang na/ rdo rje 'chang chen/ badzra pA Ni/ phyag rdor/
pra kA sha tsandra/ rab gsal zla ba/ rA hU la bha dra/ sgra gcan 'dzin bzang po/ kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA wa li ta/ pra dznyA boddhi/ dharmA pA la/ lo chen rin chen
bzang po/ rgya ye shes tshul khrims/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ mnur nyi ma 'od zer/ rtsa skya dkon mchog grags/ bla ma shAkya 'bum/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma chos
sku 'od zer/ bla ma 'phags pa man sngar bzhin no/ ! /dpal mchog rigs so so ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs rdo rje sems dpa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang rdzogs par
thob pa'i brgyud

pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ badzra pA Ni/ pra kA sha tsandra/ de la rA hU la bha dra/ swasti pha la/ dznyA na badzra/ pra dznyA siddhi dang bzhis gsan/ de bzhi ka la kun dga' snying
po/ de nas pra dznyA wa li ta/ pra dznyA boddhi/ mukti ko Sha/ dharmA pA la/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ rgya ye shes tshul khrims/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ mnur nyi ma
'od zer/ rtsa skya ston grags/ mnyam gad pa chen po/ rtsa skya ston 'bum/ rtsa skya khri brtan/ mnur ye shes rgyal mtshan/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma
dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin po che/ lo tsA ba rin rnam pa/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon rin po che'i zhal snga nas/ des bdag la'o/ ! /ngan song sbyong
ba'i rgyud las gsungs pa bcom ldan 'das kun rig rtsa ba'i dkyil 'khor sgo nyis sbag rtsa ba'i lha sum cu so bdun/ mgron thabs kyi lha drug cu/ dpal mgon bdun cu don lnga
dang bcas pa mnur lugs kyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba yongs su rdzogs pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das kun rig badzra pA Ni/ pra kA sha tsandra/ rA hU la bha
dra/ A nanda garbha/ pra dznyA ba li ta/ pra dznyA boddhi/ mukti kAo Sha/ dharma pA la/ di paM kA ra shrI dznyA na/ do pa sgom chen/ kyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes
rab/ mnur chen po/ gshen rdo rje seng ge glan chos kyi 'byung gnas/ gtum ston shAkya 'bum/ 'dzims pa rin chen shes rab/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge chos rje bu ston/
rin rnam pa/ rin po che grags rgyal ba/ mkhas grub ye shes rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / mnur chen po nas/ rtsa skya ston grags/ ltum ston shAkya 'bum/ kun mkhyen
'dzims pa/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu ston rin po che man sngar ltar ro/ ! /sbyong

rgyud las gsungs pa'i phyag na rdo rje 'chi bdag 'joms pa lha bcu gsum gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du mnur lugs kyi dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag par rdzogs
pa'i sangs rgyas/ badzra pA Ni/ pra kA sha tsandra/ ra hU la bha dra/ A nanda garbha/ pra dznyA ba li ta/ pra dznyA boddhi/ mukti ko Sha/ dharma pA la/ di paM kA ra
shrI dznyA na/ go bi sgom chen/ kyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ gnur nyi ma 'od zer/ sras rdo rje seng ge gnur byang chub 'od zer/ gnur nyi ma rgyal mtshan/
gnur ye shes rgyal mtshan/ gnur chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu ston chos kyi rje/ thugs sras rin rnam pa/ grags pa rgyal mtshan pa/ mkhyen brtse'i dbang
phyug ye shes rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ ! /ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i rgyud brtag pa phyogs gcig pa las gsungs pa'i/ shAkya seng ge'i dkyil 'khor rtsa
ba'i lha sum cu so bdun rdo rje rigs dbang yongs su rdzogs pa thob pa'i jo bo lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ badzra pA Ni/ pra kA sha tsandra/ dznyA na badzra/ A nanda
garbha/ pra dznyA ba li ta/ go mi u pa si ka shAkya dznyA na/ dge bsnyen/ jo bo rje/ go mi sgom chen/ kyi nor dznyA na/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ gnur nyi ma 'od zer/
gtum ston grags pa/ rtsa skya/ gnyam gad pa chen po/ mkhas pa khri brtan/ sras bsod bzangs/ de gnyis ka la gsal ba pa blo gros dpal/ bla ma grags chen pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags
'od/ bu ston chos rje/ lo tsA ba rin rnam pa/ grags pa rgyal mtshan pa/ rje btsun ye shes rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang na/ gnur nyi ma 'od zer nas/ stag tshal gdong
sngon gyi spru ston 'bar thog gtsang rong smad kyi rtsangs yang dag rdo rje/ de'i sras smra

seng / lce mdo sde seng ge bla ma chos sku 'od zer/ lce blo ldan seng ge kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu rin po che man sngar bzhin no/ ! /gtsug dgu lo chen lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/
yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ badzra pA Ni/ pra kA sha tsandra/ de'i slob ma'i mchog bzhi ni/ dznyA na puNDa ri ka pad dkar ye shes/ dznyA na badzra/ rA dza rA
hU la bha dra/ sUrYa garbha/ de bzhi la rgyal rigs sa ra pa/ A nanda garba/ tha ka na pa/ bA gI shwa ra kIrti/ ba lendra shanti/ a kSho bhye badzra/ mi bskyod rdo rje/ shrAddha
kA ra warma/ lo chen rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ sum ston yes 'bar/ gnyan ston tshul khrims 'bar/ thod pa en tsha grags/ jo phur thod pa 'od zer/
rong pa chos mgon/ lce blo ldan seng ge kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ bu rin po che man sngar bzhin no/ ! /yang / gtsug dgu paN chen nas brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ badzra pA
Ni/ dznyA na shrI mi dra/ bA gI shwa ra kIrti/ a bha yA ka ra gupta/ badzra A pa na/ rdo rje gdan pa/ bi Sha ta de ba/ paN chen shAkya shrIH dA na shI la/ g.yag sde lo tsA
ba bsod nams seng ge mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bu rin po che man sngar bzhin no/ ! /sbyong rgyud las gsungs pa/ rdo rje mi 'khrug pa lha bcu
gsum gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gser gling pa/ jo bo rje nas brgyud de/ mkhan po dbang phyug rin chen/ bla ma shAkya rdo
rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bong chung pa gzhon nu 'od zer/ bla ma grags chen pa/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/ chos rje bu ston/ thugs
sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ mtshungs med ye shes rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ ! /'jam dpal ye shes

sems dpa'i don dam pa'i mtshan yang dag par brjod pa rnal 'byor rgyud du bkral ba/ slob dpon 'jam dpal grags pa'i 'grel chen gyi lugs/ nam mkha' ltar yangs shing dri ma med
pa chos kyi dbyings/ gsung gi dbang phyug ye shes kyi snying po gsal ba'i dkyil 'khor/ rtsa gzungs chos gsum gyi dkyil 'khor sgo gsum sbag lha brgya nyi shu rtsa lnga/ de'i
phyi nas rdo rje rigs kyi dkyil 'khor zlum po la/ 'jig rten pa brgya dang bzhi yod pa'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor chen por dbang bskur ba rgyas pa thob pa'i brgyud pa
ni/ 'jam dbyangs/ dznyA na pa/ manydzu shrI rkIrti/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ shrI su gupta/ dpal sbas bzang po/ brahma dznyA na badzra/ bram ze ye shes rdo rje/ shes rab 'byung
gnas sbas pa/ pra dznyA kA ra gupta/ bram ze gzhad pa'i rdo rjebrahma a la la badzra/ de'i slob ma pad ma kA ra dang / shrAddha kA ra warmA gnyis ka la/ lo chen rin chen
bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ rngog dge ser ba/ rkyang po dar ma grags/ khri ston kun dga' 'od zer/ mkhan po chos rin/ chos sku 'od zer/ kun mkhyen 'phags 'od/
chos rje bu ston/ lo tsA ba rin rnam pa/ bla ma grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rtsa ba'i bla ma ye shes rgya mtsho/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i rtsa dkyil lha nyer dgu/ 'di gong du
'jug rgyu/ gzungs dkyil la nga drug chos dkyil la so gnyis/ las dkyil lam rdo rje rigs kyi dkyil 'khor la dngos su 'jig rten pa go gcig bran dang chung ma grangs med/ 'das
pa'i sgo ba brgyad do/ ! /spyod pa'i rgyud/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud las gsungs pa/ snying rje chen po 'byung ba'i dkyil 'khor sgo sum sbag
yod lha grangs 'bri rgyu/ par dbang bskur ba yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ manydzu gho Sha/ 'jam dbyangs/ dzAe tA ri/ dgra las rgyal
ba/ a sho ka

shrIH mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ la li ta badzra/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ a mo gha badzra/ don yod rdo rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba rin chen grags pa/ mchims brtson 'grus seng ge mchims don
ne/ mchims chos seng / mchims blo gros brtan pa/ mchims nam mkha' grags/ slob dpon dar ma rgyal mtshan/ byang chen pa bsod nams 'phel/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo
gros/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ mkhan chen grags pa gzhon nu/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rje btsun dam pa ye shes rgya mtsho/
des bdag la dgyes bzhin du gnang ba'o/ /de ltar de dag rnams kyi bka' ma tshang ba med par thob nas/ rdor dbyings nas 'di'i bar gyi dkyil chog bu ston rin po ches mdzad
pa rnams kyi lung yang tshang bar thob bo/ ! /yang / dam pa de'i drung du/ yo ga'i chos 'byung gru rdzings kyi lung dang / yog trika yid bzhin nor bu'i lung bshad rgyas
par thob cing / chos rje nyid kyi mdzad pa'i de kho na nyid bcu'i snying po gsal bar byed pa legs par bshad pa'i sgron me zhes bya ba'i steng nas bshad pa spyis phyin par
gnang zhing / mdor na rnal 'byor rgyud 'di skor gyi phyag khrid/ gar dbyangs/ thig la sogs pa ma tshang ba med par gnang bas/ chos 'di pa la mkhas pa bdag cag gyur pa nyid
do/ ! /rgyal po chen po rnam thos sras kyi rjes gnang / bu ston rin po ches mdzad pa'i yi ge'i steng nas/ zhi drag gnyis phyag len ji lta ba bzhin du thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ sangs rgyas rdo rje 'chang chen po/ phyag na rdo rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ dpal ldan kun tu bzang po/ slob dpon 'gro bzangs snying po/ paNDi ta rin chen
rdo rje/ kha che dgon pa ba/ bla ma zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ g.yor po jo ston/ spur ston bsod nams seng ge 'byid bu ba padma bkra

shis/ rtag pa jo bzangs/ lo tsA ba byams pa'i dpal/ bla chen bsod nams dbang phyug rin po che khro phu ba bsod nams seng ge bla ma yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge chos rje bu
rin po che/ lo tsA ba rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chen po ye shes rgya mtsho/ de'i thugs rjes bdag sngags 'chang kun dga' rnam
rgyal dpal bzang po la gnang ba'o/ ! /rje 'di nyid kyi rtsa ba'i bla ma rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan pa las/ byis pa'i dus su tshe dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ tshe
dpag med/ garbha pA dang / dze ta rI/ boddhi bha dra/ sa mA dhi bha dra/ badzra A pa na/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson seng / rgya gzhung phug pa/ mdzad pa shes rab rin
chen/ e pa 'khon ston/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs chen po/ bla ma rgyal ba ye shes/ grags pa dpal bzangs/ chos 'phags rgyal mtshan/ yang rtse ba rin chen seng ge bu ston rin po
che/ thugs sras rin chen rnam rgyal/ rin po che grags pa rgyal mtshan pa/ des bdag la gnang ba'o/ /dze tA ri'i lugs lha dgu ma'i dbang yin no// //@/ /chos kyi rje rgyal
ba'i gsung gi mdzod 'dzin sems dpa' chen po/ shAkya rgyal mtshan zhabs las/ rgyud 'bum skor gyi thob yigna mo badzra dha rA yA/ gang gis sangs rgyas sar 'gro ba/ /de yi
lam mkhan mchog gyur pa/ /bla ma'i zhabs la phyag 'tshal nas/ /de yi drin gyis brnyed pa'i nor/ /dus gsum rgyal ba'i bsgrod pa gcig pa'i lam/ /nye lam zab mo rdo rje theg
pa yi/ /rgyud sde rgya mtsho

thob pa'i rim pa dang / /bla ma brgyud pa'i phreng mdzes bkod par bya/ /de ltar na mchog gi go 'phangs/ sangs rgyas kyi sar snyegs pa'i blo gros dang / bskal ba can rnams kyi
'jug ngogs/ bstan pa rin po che'i snying po/ zab mo rdo rje theg pa'i bka' dri ma med pa/ chos kyi rje sems dpa' chen po shAkya'i mtshan can las nod pa rnams kyi rim pa
ni/ re zhig bu ston rin po ches bsgrigs pa'i go rim gzhir bzhag pa la/ 'dir gsang sngags kyi rgyud sde/ bya ba dang / spyod pa dang / rnal 'byor dang / rnal 'byor chen
po bla na med pa dang bzhi'o/ /bzhi pa la gnyis su med pa'i rgyud/ shes rab rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud/ thabs rnal 'byor pha'i rgyud dang gsum gyi dang po ni/ ka pa la/ dpal dus
kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud stong phrag bcu gnyis pa las phyung ba/ rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi dum bu mdor bstan pa zhes bya ba/ kha che'i paNDi ta so ma nA thA dang / 'bro shes rab
grags kyis bsgyur ba las/ sgra tshad pa rin rgyal gyis 'grel pa dang bstun nas dag par bcos pa dang / dus kyi 'khor lo bsdus pa'i rgyud le'ur lnga pa/ paNDi ta so ma nA
thA dang / lo tsA ba 'bro shes rab grags kyis bsgyur ba las/ dus phyis shongs lo tsA ba rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis dag par bcos pa dang / dus kyi 'khor lo'i rgyud kyi snying
po phyi ma gnyan lo tsA ba dar ma grags kyi bsgyur ba/ bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi brgol ba dum bu'i rgyud kyi snying po zhes bya ba/ 'dir dkar chag tu ma byung / lo tsA ba gyi
jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba/ dus 'khor bsdus rgyud las dA ri kA pas phyung ba dbang gi rab tu byed pa lo tsA ba rwa chos rab kyis bsgyur ba rnams kyi brgyud pa
ni/ 'di dkar chag du ma byung / byang chub sems dpa'i sprul pa gcig la/ dge slong bsod snyoms pa chen pos gsan/ de la lho phyogs kyi bram ze dA ri kA pa/ tsi lu paNDi ta/
dus

zhabs pa che chung gnyis/ boddhi bha dra/ sA dhU pu tra/ a bha ya kA ra gupta/ rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags/ a bhi dzu ka pa/ dharmA sA dhu pu tra/ dharma A kA ra/ bhaskA ra la/
se lo tsA ba tshul khrims gzhon nus a bha yA ka ra la tshar gcig rtsa mi la tshar gnyis/ a bhi dzu ka la stod cig bhas kA ra la tshar gcig de la gnyos 'od mas tshar gsum
gsan/ se lo tsA ba bkra shis rin chen/ sangs rgyas rdo rje/ grub chen u rgyan pa/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal
shes rab/ mkhan chen grags rdor ba/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje shAkya dhwa tsha/ des bdag la'o/ ! /gnyis pa shes rab gtso bor ston pa rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud la/ rigs
drug ka mnyam par ston pa'i rgyud/ he ru ka'i gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud dang / rnam snang gi rigs gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud/ rdo rje nyi ma'i rigs gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud/
pad ma gar dbang gi rigs gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud/ rta mchog gi rigs gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud/ rigs drug pa rdo rje 'chang gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud dang bdun gyi dang
po ni/ sangs rgyas thams cad dang mnyam par sbyor ba/ mkha' 'gro ma sgyu ma bde ba'i mchog ces bya ba'i rgyud bla ma/ rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa bcu pa/ 'di la dkyil 'khor
nyi shu rtsa gcig tu 'grel bar bshad/ de'i rgyud phyi ma rtog pa bdun pa'i dpe ma rnyed do/ /de'i rgyud phyi ma rtog pa lnga pa/ paNDi ta smr-i ti dznyA na kIrti'i rang
'gyur/ de gsum rdzogs pa la gzhung tshad khri brgyad stong du bshad do/ /de'i rgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas phyag rdor/ rdo rje gdan pa che chung gsum/ pUNya shrIH steng pa lo
tsA ba/ so thams cad mkhyen pa/ so 'dzam gling rgyan/ lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ glan bang so ba/ rgya pho ba lung pa/ gnyal pa chos

grags/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can pa/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ mkhan chen grags pa rdo rje/
chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o/ ! /gnyis pa la/ bde mchog dang / kyai rdo rje dang / sangs rgyas thod pa dang / sgyu 'phrul chen mo dang / a ra li gnyis
dang lnga'i dang po la/ rtsa ba'i rgyud 'bum pa chen po las bsdus pa'i rgyud rtsa ba'i rgyud/ phyi ma'i phyi ma le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa/ shlau ka shlo ka ces pa bod
skad du tshigs bcad dang grags pa la'ang bsgyur/ stong bdun brgya pa/ paNDi ta padma kA ra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba las/ dus phyis lo tsA ba/ grags
'byor shes rab dang / mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis/ bla ma nA ro pa'i phyag dpe las gtugs nas dag par bcos shing gtan la phab pa 'di la/ dngos su dkyil 'khor gnyis ston
cing / grol dgongs bkod nas bcu gsum du ston no/ /'gyur 'di la phreng sngags btu ba yod gzhan la med do/ /rgyud 'di ni pha chos kyi rje nyid la thob zin pas/ slad nas
ma nyan zhing brgyud yig kyang gzhan na gdog brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ bram ze sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha ba ra pa/ dA ri ka pa/ gandhaM pa/ rus sbal
zhabs/ dza landha ra pa/ karNaN pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam par rgyal ba'i zhabs/ bar ma'i slob dpon/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham thing pa sku mched/ klog kya shes rab rtsegs/ mal
gyo lo tsA ba/ rje sa chen pa/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta/ 'phags pa rin po che/ slob dpon chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ gar thig pa/
mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o/ ! /de'i

bshad rgyud thun mong ma yin pa dang / thun mong ba gnyis las/ thun mong ma yin pa la/ dang po nges par brjod pa'i rgyud bla ma'i bla ma zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u
drug cu rtsa dgu pa/ paNDi ta ku mA ra dang / lo tsA ba mang 'or byang chub shes rab kyis bsgyur ba bzhugs so/ /'di la dngos su dkyil 'khor sum cu so brgyad/ 'grel pa'ang
lnga bcu nga drug tu bkral zhing / gtso bo 'pho ba'i dbye bas dkyil 'khor drug brgya brgyad cu rtsa gcig tu ston no/ /brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang nas/ sa skya paNDi
ta'i bar rtsa rgyud dang 'dra la/ de nas/ 'u yug pa/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ dharmma sras/ dharmma dhwa dza/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor nas gong dang 'dra// ! /kha pa la/
rdo rje mkha' 'gro zhes bya ba'i rgyud chen po le'u lnga bcu pa/ paNDi ta shrI ga ya dha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba bzhugs so// dpal rdo
rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud phyi ma snying po btus pa/ 'di la dkyil 'khor drug yod/ brgyud pa ni/ ratna shrIH ka lyA Na/ dge ba'i dge legs/ shAnti ma ti/ pa ti de wa tra/ bhU
mi shrIH bi ma la shrIH shongs blo brtan/ lo mchog bde ba can pa ye shes mgon/ seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ gnyis ka la mkhan chen shes rdor man 'dra'o/ /mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho
rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po le'u lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa/ paNDi ta rgyal ba'i sde dang / lo tsA ba dharmma yon tan gyis bsgyur ba las/ phyis sum pa dpal mchog
dang po'i rdo rjes bka' dang bstun nas dag par bcos pa/ 'di la dkyil 'khor brgya dang bcu bzhi'am/ brgya bzhi cu rtsa gnyis yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag
rdor/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ rdo rje gdan pa/ dha byang sems/ a bha yA ka ra/ ratna shrIH dza ya se na/ lo tsA ba dharmma yon tan/ rje btsun pa/ chos rje pa/ skyob pa

dpal/ rgyal tsha sna po che/ mchog ldan/ sangs rgyas sras/ bla ma ye mgon pa/ bla ma dar ma bzang po/ shrI ri ba gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/
des bdag go/ ! /dpal sdom pa 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u sum cu rtsa gsum pa/ paNDi ta/ pa ra hi ti bha dra dang / lo tsA ba rgyus bandhe smon lam grags
kyis bsgyur ba las/ shongs lo tsA ba blo brtan gyi dag par bcos pa 'dis dkyil 'khor cig bstan no/ /brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / lU hi pa/ dA ri kA pa/ rdo rje dril bu
pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ dza landha ra pa/ dpe med dpal/ ratna rakShi ta/ chag lo tsA ba/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal/ shongs blo brtan/ lo mchog bla ma dpal ldan seng ge gar thig
pa la'ang zhus/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba man 'dra/ dpal khrag 'thung mngon par 'byung ba zhes bya ba/ rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bzhi cu rtsa lnga pa/ paNDi
ta a dwa ya badzra dang / 'di 'od zer rdo rje/ lo tsA ba chings yon tan 'bar gyi bsgyur ba 'di la dkyil 'khor gsum yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ nges brjod bla ma dang 'dra'o/
/rnal 'byor ma kun tu spyod pa'i rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /brgyud pa nges brjod bla ma dang 'dra'o/ /rnal 'byor ma bzhi kha sbyor ba'i rgyud
brtag pa bdun pa la chings yon tan 'bar gyi rgyud/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ sa ra ha/ klu sgrub/ sha ba ra pa/
lU hi pa/ dA ri ka pa/ gandha pa/ rus sbal zhabs/ dzA landha ra pa/ kahna pa/ gu hya pa/ rnam par rgyal ba'i zhabs can/ bar ma'i slob dpon/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham thing
pa sku mched/ klog kya shes rab rtsegs/ mal gyo lo tsA ba/ sa chen pa/ slob dpon pa/ rje btsun pa/ sa paN/ bsod

nams seng ge sangs rgyas 'bum/ sangs rgyas sras/ blo chen/ bde ba can pa ye mgon/ grags 'bum/ seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor man 'dra'o/ ! /phag mo mngon par
byang chub pa zhes bya ba'i bshad pa'i rgyud/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dznyA nA ka rI zhal snga nas dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba khu ston dngos grub kyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la
dkyil 'khor gsum yod/ brgyud pa/ rnal 'byor ma bzhi kha sbyor dang 'dra'o/ /ral pa gyen brdzes kyi rgyud las phyung ba'i rig pa 'dzin ma rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs
zhes bya ba/ paNDi ta dza ya se na dang / lo tsA ba dar ma yon tan gyi 'gyur/ 'di mai tri mkha' spyod kyi rgyud yin// ! /gnyis pa ni/ rgyud thams cad kyi gleng gzhi dpal
yang dag par sbyor ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po rtsa ba'i rgyud brtag pa bcu/ brtag pa re re la rab byed bzhi bzhi yod pa/ 'di la dngos su dkyil 'khor
bcu drug yod cing gtso bo 'pho ba'i dbye bas mang por 'gyur ro/ /de'i rgyud phyi ma dang bcas pa/ ga ya dha ra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ 'di rgyud sde mang po'i bshad rgyud
yin cing / khyad par bde mchog gi bshad rgyud do/ /'di'ang / pha chos kyi rje las thob pas/ brgyud pa'ang brtag gnyis dang mthun no// ! /ga pa la/ bde mchog gi bshad rgyud
du 'dod pa'i rtsod pa can rwa li'i skor la/ thugs kyi rgyud brgyad/ gsung gi rgyud brgyad/ sku'i rgyud brgyad/ kha 'thor gyi rgyud brgyad de dum bu so gnyis su bzhed
pa las/ dang po la/ gsang ba rdo rje'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bzhi pa/ paNDi ta ratna badzra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ gsang ba spyod pa'i rgyud/ dpal 'khor lo sdom pa gsang
ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ dpal nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud kyi

rgyal po/ dpal nam mkha' chen po'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ dpal sku gsung thugs kyi rgyud kyi rgyal po/ rin chen phreng ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ dam tshig chen po'i rgyud kyi rgyal
po rnams so/ /gnyis pa gsung gi rgyud la/ dpal stobs po che'i rgyud le'u lnga pa/ paNDi ta ga ya dha ra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ ye shes gsang ba'i rgyud/ ye shes phreng
ba'i rgyud/ ye shes 'bar ba'i rgyud/ zla ba'i phreng ba'i rgyud/ rin chen 'bar ba'i rgyud/ de rnal 'byor ma zla ba'i phreng ba dang / shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ nyi ma'i
'khor lo'i rgyud/ ye shes rgyal po'i rgyud rnams so/ /sku'i rgyud brgyad ni/ mkha' 'gro ma gsang ba'i rgyud/ gsang ba me 'bar gyi rgyud/ gsang ba bdud rtsi'i rgyud/ dur
khrod brgyan gyis rgyud rnams/ ga ya dha ra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ rdo rje rgyal po'i rgyud/ tsandra mA le dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ ye shes gsang ba'i rgyud/ ga ya dha
ra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ chags pa'i rgyal po'i rgyud/ rnal 'byor ma ratna mA le dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ mkha' 'gro ma sdom pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ bzhi pa 'phros
pa'i rgyud brgyad ni/ me'i phreng ba/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro ma gsang ba'i rgyud/ rdo rje 'jigs byed rnam par 'joms pa'i rgyud/ stobs po che ye shes rgyal po'i rgyud/ ga ya dha
ra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ rdo rje grub pa drwa ba sdom pa'i rgyud/ ga ya dha ra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ sku gsung thugs kyi snying po don gyi rgyud/ rje btsun cha ru
ba dang / seng dkar shAkya 'od kyi 'gyur/ dur khrod kyi rgyan smad du byung ba'i rgyud/ gA ya dha ra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ de rnams kyi steng du snyog pa med pa'i rgyud
bsnan pas 'phros rgyud du 'dod/ de ltar rwa li so gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ lU hi pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ dha ra shrIH ga ya dha

ra/ 'brog mi/ tshur dbang nge / spug thams cad mkhyen pa/ spug dharmma ke tu/ bya rin chen 'od/ bla ma sangs rgyas sras/ slob dpon dkon mchog shes rab/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen
shes rdor ba man 'dra/ snyog pa med pa'i rgyud/ ga ya dha ra dang / 'brog mi'i 'gyur/ brgyud pa gong dang 'dra/ yang bde mchog nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud le'u gsum
pa/ paNDi ta dznyA na badzras rang 'gyur du mdzad pa/ mkha' 'gro ma thams cad kyi sku gsung thugs gnyis su med pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i ye shes rdo rje phag mo mngon
par 'byung ba'i rgyud ces bya ba/ rtsa rgyud le'u bcu gsum/ rgyud phyi ma le'u gnyis dang bcas pa gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba'i brgyud pa ni/ gong gi phag mo
mngon par byang chub dang 'dra'o/ /dpal rdo rje nag po chen po khros pa'i mgon po gsang ba dngos grub 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud le'u nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ lo tsA ba khe
gad pa 'khor lo grags kyi bsgyur ba'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje dril bu pa/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ dga' ba'i rdo rje/ rdo rje gdan pa/ a bhya ka ra/ rtsa
mi sangs rgyas grags/ dpal rgwa lo/ khams pa dge slong shes rgyal/ gze ba don grub/ khams pa g.yag sde ba/ phyug po chos grags/ khams pa byang chub dpal/ bla ma gzhon
nu dar/ bla ma rgyal mtshan/ rdo rje mgon/ shrI ri pa gzhon nu rgyal mtshan/ rin po che grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o/ ! /gnyis pa/ kyai rdo rje'i skor la/ rtsa
ba'i rgyud/ bsdus pa'i rgyud/ rgyud phyi ma/ phyi ma'i phyi ma/ bshad pa'i rgyud/ snying po'i rgyud/ 'bras bu'i rgyud bdun gyi dang po/ rtsa ba'i rgyud kyai rdo rje 'bum
phrag lnga pa las bsdus pa'i kyai rdo rje zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ brtag pa dang po la le'u bcu gcig pa/ brtag pa gnyis pa le'u bcu gnyis pa/ paNDi ta ga ya dha
ra

dang / lo tsA ba 'brog mi shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la dkyil 'khor drug yod do/ /gnyis pa/ de'i thun mong ma yin pa'i bshad rgyud/ mkha' 'gro ma rdo rje gur zhes bya
ba le'u bco lnga pa 'gyur byang snga ma dang 'dra'o/ /'di la dngos su dkyil 'khor bcu gtso bo 'pho ba'i dbye bas drug cu rtsa gnyis su 'gyur ro/ /rtsa bshad 'di gnyis/
pha chos kyi rje las thob pa'o/ /de gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bdag med ma/ birWa pa/ DoM bhi ba/ a la la badzra/ nags khrod pa/ garbha ri pa/ bsod snyoms
pa rgyal ba dpal gyi ye shes/ mi thub zla ba/ dge slong dpa' bo rdo rje/ 'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ sa chen kun snying / slob dpon bsod nams rtse
mo/ rje btsun grags pa rgyal mtshan/ chos rje sa paN/ 'phags pa rin po che/ zhang mdo dpal/ 'jam skya/ bla ma dpal ldan seng ge bla ma bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba
nas gong bzhin no/ /gsum pa/ rgyud phyi ma phyag rgya chen po thig le zhes bya ba/ rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po le'u nyi shu rtsa brgyad pa/ paNDi ta shes
rab gsang ba dang / lo tsA ba skam chos kyi ye shes dang / phyugs 'tshams dgra bcom gyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig ston no/ /bzhi pa de'i rgyud phyi ma'i phyi ma
ye shes snying po rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po le'u bzhi pa/ dpal shes rab gsang ba'i rang 'gyur ro/ /'dis dkyil 'khor gcig ston no/ /lnga pa bshad pa'i rgyud
dpal ye shes thig le'i rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u sum cu pa/ dpal shes rab gsang ba'i rang 'gyur ro/ /'dis dkyil 'khor lnga ston no/ /drug pa snying po'i
rgyud grub pa nges bstan ni ma rnyed do/ /bdun pa 'bras bu'i rgyud/ dpal de kho na nyid kyi sgron ma/ dpal shes rab gsang ba'i rang

'gyur/ de rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang nas/ chos rje sa skya paNDi ta'i bar brtag gnyis dang mthun/ de nas kha ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ blo chen sangs rgyas/ bde
ba can pa seng rgyal/ bla ma dkon mchog seng ge gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba nas gong dang 'dra/ ! gsum pa/ gsal po mi 'dug sangs rgyas thod pa zhes bya ba/ rnal
'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bcu bzhi pa/ paNDi ta ga ya dha ra dang / lo tsA ba gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la dkyil 'khor bzhi yod/ brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje 'chang / DA ki ma/ lU hi pa/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ ga ya dha ra/ 'brog mi/ mtshur ston dbang nge / spug thams cad mkhyen pa/ spug dharmma ke ru/ jo gdan gnyal pa/
blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can pa/ bla ma gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor nas 'dra'o/ ! /bzhi pa/ sgyu 'phrul chen mo zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u gsum
pa/ lo tsA ba mgos lhas btsas kyi bsgyur ba 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje snying po/ ye shes kyi mkha' 'gro ma/ ku ku ri pa/ mtsho
skyes rdo rje/ DoM bhi ba/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ bal po shAnta bha dra/ mar pa lo tsA ba/ rngog chos rdor/ rngog mdo sde/ rngog tsha chos sku/ rngog tsha dkon mchog klog
kya dbang phyug grags/ lho pa shes rab dpal/ bla ma 'phags pa/ bla chen sangs rgyas sras man gong dang 'dra'o/ /lnga pa ri gi a ra li'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po le'u
bcu bzhi paNDi ta ga ya dha ra dang / lo tsA ba shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba/ rdo rje a ra li'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bcu pa 'gyur snga ma bzhin/ 'di gnyis la dkyil
'khor re re yod do/ /brgyud pa gong gi ra li so gnyis dang 'dra'o/ /gsum pa la/ gsal po mi 'dug rdo rje gdan bzhi'i rgyud/ gdan bzhi

re re la rab byed bzhi bzhi ste bcu drug paNDi ta smr-i ti'i rang 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /de'i bshad rgyud sngags kyi cha'i rgyud rgyal po smr-i ti'i 'gyur/
'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /de gnyis las/ rtsa rgyud 'di/ pha chos kyi rje las thob cing / bshad rgyud kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa/
rngog chos rdor/ rngog mdo sde/ tsad dharmma rA dza/ rgya gsar ba rin chen 'bum/ rgya bsod nams 'bum/ bya rin chen 'od/ blo chen/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes
rdor man 'dra'o// ! /nga pa la/ rnal 'byor thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po ni/ le'u brgya lhag pa 'gyur dang / brgyud pa gong bzhin no/ /'di la dkyil 'khor dgu
yod do/ /'di ni rgyud las/ ji ltar rnal 'byor nam mkha' nyid/ /de ltar rnam par snang mdzad bdag /ces bshad cing / slob dpon ArYa de bas kyang / rnal 'byor nam mkha' rnam
snang du gsungs shing / 'di ni rnam snang gi rigs so/ /dpal gtum po khro bo chen po rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ paNDi ta ratna shrI dang / lo tsA ba grags
pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la dkyil 'khor lnga yab yum yod med kyis phye bas bcu'o/ /brgyud pa ni/ shrI ri pa/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag
go /'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i rtog pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bdun pa/ paNDi ta a tu la badzra dang / lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur ba'o/ /khro bo'i rgyal
po thams cad gsang ba'i rgyud ces bya ba le'u lnga pa/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gnyis yod do/ /mi g.yo ba gsang ba'i rgyud chen po le'u bzhi pa ste/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gnyis
yod do/ /'di gsum gyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal/ dze tI ri pa/ mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ rol pa'i rdo

rje/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson seng / blo brtan/ sangs rgyas dpal/ lo mchog blo chen/ bde ba can pa/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor nas gong bzhin no/ /bzhi pa ni/
rdo rje bdud rtsi'i rgyud kyi rgyal po le'u bcu gcig pa/ 'di la dkyil 'khor bzhi yod cing / rin po che'i rigs su rgyud 'grel du gsungs so/ /lnga pa ni/ dpal pad ma 'bar ba'i
rgyud chen po las phyung ba/ rigs kyi 'jig rten mgon po lnga bcu pa le'u bzhi pa/ paNDi ta bi ma la shrI dang / lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la
rgyud na dkyil 'khor mi gsal/ slob dpon dag gi dkyil 'khor yang bshad do/ /brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas nas rol pa'i rdo rje bar gong bzhin no/ /de nas don yod rdo rje/ ba
ri lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson seng / don chen/ chos seng / blo brtan/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog man gong bzhin no/ /sgrol ma ku ru kulle'i rtog pa le'u lnga/ kr-iShNa paNDi
ta dang / tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ bhU mi kIrti/ gze ba blo brtan/ jo bde/ don grub ye shes/ de gnyis la khams pa shAkya
rdo rjes zhus/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog sgra tshad pa rin rgyal/ chos rgyal/ bla ma gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje nas gong bzhin no/ /drug pa ni/
sgrol ma mngon par 'byung ba'i rgyud le'u lnga brgya bdun cu pa nas phyung ba'i sgrol ma phyag 'tshal nyi shu rtsa gcig bstod pa phan yon dang bcas pa/ 'di nyi ma sbas
pas rnal 'byor bla med du bkral zhing / rdul tshon dang / lus dkyil gnyis su bkral lo/ /'di pha rgyud phyogs kyi lha mo'i phyogs su gtogs sam brtag par bya'o/ /brgyud pa
ni/ sangs rgyas/ kun dga' bo/ kr-iShNa'i gos can/ sha na'i gos can/ nyi ma'i gung

pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen/ nyi ma sbas pa/ dze tA ri/ ngag dbang grags pa/ ma na kA shrIH mal lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson seng / mchims blo brtan/ dbang phyug rin
chen/ khams pa shAkya rdo rje/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog bag ston pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba nas/ gong bzhin no/ /rdo rje phur pa rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi dum bu chos
rje sa skya pas bsgyur ba/ 'di rtsa rgyud las phyung ba yin pas gleng gzhi med cing / brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ klu sgrub/ ArYa de ba/ ma tanggi/
bi khyA ta de ba/ paN chen shAkya shrIH ta thA ga ta shrI/ chos rje sa paN/ rin po che skyob pa dpal/ rgyal tsha lung mangs po/ blo chen/ bde ba can pa/ gar thig pa/ mkhan

/ rA chos rab kyi bsgyur ba 'di la mngon rtogs kyi phye na dkyil 'khor drug tu 'gyur ro/ /brgyud pa ni/ bha ro/ rwa lo tsA ba chos rab/ rwa ye shes seng ge rgwa lo/ rwa
shes rgyal/ blo chen pa/ bde ba can pa/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen pa nas gong bzhin no// ! //ji bzhin bsnyes pa nam mkha' dang mnyam pa'i rgyud le'u lnga pa/ paNDi ta kSha

thing pa sku mched/ klog kya shes rab rtsegs/ mal lo tsA ba/ rje sa chen/ slob dpon pa/ rje btsun pa/ chos rje sa skya

chen po thabs kyi rgyud la/ mi skyod pa dang / rnam snang dang / rin 'byung dang / 'od dpag med dang / don yod grub pa dang / drug pa rdo rje 'chang gi rigs gtso bor ston
pa'i rgyud nga drug las dang po la/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa rtsa ba'i rgyud le'u bcu bdun pa/ paNDi ta shrAddha kA ra warmma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba/
'di la gtso bo 'pho ba'i dbye bas dkyil 'khor sum cu rtsa gnyis su 'phags skor ba rnams bzhed do/ /rgyud 'di nyid/ pha chos kyi rje las thob mod/ 'on kyang rgyud pa'i slad
du/ slar mnyan pa'i rgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ klu sgrub/ ArYa de ba/ klu'i byang chub/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ rdo rje dril bu pa/
dza landha ra pa/ DoM bhi he ru ka bai ra Di pa/ ma tangki pa/ niska langka de ba/ re wandre bha dra/ chag lo tsA ba/ 'dzims pa 'jam dbyangs chen po/ bde ba can pa yes mgon/
gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba man 'dra/ de'i rgyud phyi ma le'u bco brgyad pa/ 'gyur dang / rgyud pa gong bzhin no/ /gsang ba 'dus pa'i bshad rgyud/
dgongs pa lung ston le'u bcu gnyis pa 'gyur sngar bzhin no/ /bshad rgyud rdo rje phreng ba mngon par brjod pa/ rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud thams cad kyi snying po gsang

ta de nyid dang / nag tsho lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bcos shing gtan la phab pa'o/ /'di ni rgyud de'i bde ba chen po'i le'u zhes bya ba le'u gnyis pa logs su phyung

no// ! //ca pa la/ gnyis pa rnam par snang mdzad kyi rigs su gtogs pa'i rgyud la/ 'phags pa sgyu 'phrul drwa ba stong
