ni pa/ gu na bha dra/ wa gi shwa ra kIrti/ di ba A kA ra tsandra/ nyin 'byung zla ba/ a mo gha badzra/ zhang shes rab bla ma/ saM gha badzra/ gcen rdo rje rtse mo/ gcung
tsA 'od/ g.yul las rnam rgyal/ bstan bzangs pa/ sangs rgyas 'byung ba/ 'dzims pa/ 'jam dbyangs/ ye shes mgon/ seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen pa man 'dra'o/ ! /dpal
rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud rtog pa bdun pa paNDi ta ba ro phyag bsdum dang / rwa chos rab kyi 'gyur/ 'di la dngos su dkyil 'khor gcig paNDi ta 'gas gsum du dgongs par bkral
lo/ /'jigs byed kyi rgyud rtog pa gsum pa dang / gshin rje'i gshed nag po'i 'khor lo las thams cad sgrub par byed pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ sdom tshig gsum
gyis bsdus pa/ paNDi ta ba ro phyag bsdum dang / rwa chos rab kyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la dngos su dkyil 'khor gcig snang / bla ma dag gsum du byed do/ /brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje
'chang / DA ki ma/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pra dznyA rakShi ta/ manydze gling pa/ rwa rdo rje grags/ rwa chos rab/ rwa dar ma seng ge rwa dkon seng / rwa shes rgyal/ khams
pa byang chub dpal/ lo mchog blo chen/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon/ bde ba can pa seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen pa man 'dra/ gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa/ shrI ri pa/ chos
rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ bdag go ! /rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi rgyud kyi rgyal po'i las dngos grub kyi rtog pa zhes bya ba rtog pa bzhi par grags pa/ mar pa chos dbang
gi 'gyur/ dpal gshin rje gshed dmar po zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ le'u bcu

dgu pa/ paNDi ta ra hU la shrI bha dra dang / shongs blo brtan gyis bsgyur ba/ 'di la dkyil 'khor bcu yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ manydzu shrIH ratna shrI/ shAkya shrIH
bhu mi shrIH 'gro mgon 'phags pa/ chag lo/ lo tsA ba grags rgyal/ lo mchog blo chen/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor nas gong bzhin no/ /gsum pa/ rin po che'i rigs
kyi rgyud ni ma rnyed do/ /bzhi pa/ pad ma'i rigs kyi brgyud ni/ bcom ldan 'das ral pa gcig pa'i brtag pa rgyud kyi rgyal po/ paNDi ta ra hU la shrI dang khro phu lo tsA
ba'i 'gyur/ 'di la rgyud nas dkyil 'khor gcig gsal/ mi pham sbas pa'i bshes gnyen gyis gnyis su bkral lo/ ! /lnga pa las kyi rigs kyi rgyud ni ma rnyed do/ /drug pa rdo
rje 'chang gi rigs kyi rgyud la/ zla gsang thig le gsang ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po shin tu dgyes pa rdo rje gdon mi za ba'i dam tshig dkyil 'khor chen po rgyas pa mchog
tu gsang ba'i rgyud/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor lnga yod do/ /brgyud pa sangs rgyas mnyam sbyor dang 'dra'o/ ! /gnyis pa rnal 'byor rgyud
la thabs gtso bor ston pa dang / shes rab gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud gnyis kyi dang po la/ rtsa ba'i rgyud/ bshad pa'i rgyud/ 'phros pa'i cha mthun pa'i rgyud dang gsum gyi
dang po ni/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi de kho na nyid bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ rigs lnga rigs bzhir bsdus nas mnyam par ston pa/ rtsa ba'i rgyud dum bu bzhi/ rgyud
phyi ma/ phyi ma'i phyi ma/ rgyud nye bar bsdus pa dang bcas pa 'di la dkyil 'khor nyis brgya dang bcu gsum yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ rab gsal zla ba/
sgra gcan 'dzin/ swa sti pha la/ ye shes rdo rje/ pra dznyA siddhi/ kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA wa li ta pa/ rab

'byor skyangs/ dharmma pha la/ rin chen bzang po/ gu shrI brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ gnur nyi ma seng ge rtsa skya ston grags/ mnyam skad pa chen
po/ tsaskya shAka 'bum/ 'dzims pa/ 'jam dbyangs pa/ seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje nas gong bzhin no// ! /gnyis pa ni/ rdo rje rtse mo'i rgyud rtog
pa bcu las/ 'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal ba'i rtog pa yan chad rdzogs nas/ phyi rol rdo rje rigs kyi mtshan rgya rtsas gsol ba btab pa yan chod/ paNDi ta karmma badzra
dang / lo tsA ba gzhon nu tshul khrims kyi 'gyur/ 'di yan chad la dkyil 'khor dngos su gsungs pa dgu yod/ 'di'i 'phro la da dung rtog pa phyed dang lnga ma tshang ngo
/ /brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ byams pa/ gaM ga dha ra/ sa manta bha dra/ kha che dznyA na shrIH gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ gnur nyi ma seng ge glan chos 'byung / tsaskya shAka
'bum man rtsa rgyud de nyid bsdus pa dang 'dra'o/ /thams cad gsang ba zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po padmA ka ra warmma dang / lo tsA ba rin
chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ tsaskya shAka 'bum yan rtsa rgyud dang 'dra'o/ /de nas/ sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog blo chen/ seng rgyal/
gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor nas gong bzhin no/ /'di dum bu dang po'i bshad rgyud de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs gtso bor ston pa'o/ /'jig rten gsum las rnam par rgyal
ba'i rtog pa'i rgyal po/ rtsa ba'i rgyud/ rgyud phyi ma dang bcas pa 'di la dkyil 'khor bzhi bcu zhe drug yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ tsaskya shAka 'bum yan rdo rje rtse mo
dang 'dra/ de nas bla ma khri brtan/ gnur ye rgyal/ gnur chos rgyal/ bka' bcu pa/ spru ston/ mkhan chen shes

rdor nas gong bzhin no/ /'di dum bu gnyis pa'i bshad rgyud rdo rje'i rigs gtso bor ston pa'o// ! /gsum pa dum bu gnyis pa'i ngan song dgug cing sdig pa dral ba la 'phros pa'i
rgyud dam/ cha mthun pa'i rgyud/ ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba gzi brjid rgyal po'i rtog pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po shAntiM garbha dang / lo tsA bandhe A tsArYa
rakShi tas bsgyur ba/ A tsarYa rin chen mchog gis skad gsar chad kyis kyang bcos shing gtan la phab pa'o/ /'di la dkyil 'khor bcu gnyis yod do/ /'phags pa ngan song thams
cad yongs su sbyong ba'i snying po'i gzungs de bzhin gshegs pa dgra bcom pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas ngan song thams cad yongs su sbyong ba gzi brjid kyi rgyal
po'i brtag pa phyogs gcig pa/ paNDi ta re wendra de ba dang / ma Ni ka shrI dznyA na dang / chag chos rje dpal gyi 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor bcu gcig yod do/ /brgyud
pa de nyid 'dus pa bzhin no/ /rab tu gnas pa mdor bsdus pa'i rgyud/ kha che paNDi ta dznyA na badzra dang / lo tsA ba 'bro shes rab grags kyi 'gyur/ brgyud pa ni/ sangs
rgyas/ phyag rdor/ rab gsal zla ba/ sgra gcan 'dzin/ swasti pha la/ ye shes rdo rje/ pra dznyA siddhi/ kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA wa li ta/ rab 'byor skyangs/ dharmma
pha la/ rin chen bzang po/ gu shrI brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan/ gnyal pa nyi ma shes rab/ gnur nyi ma seng ge tsaskya ston grags/ mnyam gad pa chen po/ tsaskya shAka 'bum/
dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can pa seng rgyal/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje nas gong bzhin no/ /'di de nyid
bcu'i sgo nas cho ga bsgrub par bshad pas/ bya ba'i rgyud du byed pa mi 'thad de/ rnal 'byor rgyud kyi cho ga las 'phros pa'o// ! //cha pa

la/ gnyis pa la de nyid bsdus pa'i cha mthun pa'i rgyud/ dpal mchog dang po zhes bya ba theg pa chen po rtog pa'i rgyal po ni/ dum bu dang po sher phyin gyi dum bu/ paNDi ta
A tsArYa shrAddha kA ra warmma dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ dum bu gnyis pa rtsa ba'i rgyud/ rgyud phyi ma/ dum bu dang po dang / gnyis pa'i rtog pa thams
cad bsdus pa'i rgyud dum bu gnyis pa nyid kyi rtog pa thams cad kyi rgyud phyi ma'i rtsa ba'i rgyud dang / gsang ba ras ris kyi cho ga dang / phyag rgya'i rgyud/ rtog pa
thams cad kyi rgyud/ phyi ma'i rtsa ba'i rtog pa dang / rtog pa thams cad bsgrub pa'i cho ga dang / phyag rgya'i rgyud thams cad kyi don gtan la 'bebs pa dang / rtog pa
thams cad bsdus pa'i mchog tu gsang ba'i cho ga dang / rgyud nye bar bsdu ba dang bcas pa rnams/ paNDi ta maNDa ka la sha dang / lo tsA ba lha btsan po zhi ba 'od kyis bsgyur
ba/ 'di la slob dpon kun snying gi dkyil 'khor brgyad cu rtsa bzhir bzhed/ slob dpon pad ma badzra zhabs kyi dkyil 'khor bdun cu rtsa brgyad du bzhed do/ /brgyud pa
ni/ tsaskya shAka 'bum yan chad rtsa rgyud de nyid 'dus pa dang 'dra/ de nas sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog blo chen/ seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor man 'dra'o/
/shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa tshul brgya lnga bcu pa 'di la dkyil 'khor bco lnga/ de la phye na/ nyi shur 'gyur bar 'grel pas bshad cing / 'di dpal mchog sher dum
dang 'dra bar 'dug go /brgyud pa mdo'i sher phyin phran rnams kyi brgyud pa dang mthun no/ /rdo rje snying po rgyan gyi rgyud paNDi ta bde bar gshegs pa'i dpal dang / chos
rje sa skya paNDi tas bsgyur ba'i 'phro/ dpangs lo tsA ba blo gros brtan pas bsgyur ba 'di la dkyil 'khor sum cu rtsa gnyis yod do/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa sgo
nyi shu rtsa lnga pa 'di rdo rje

snying po rgyan gyi rgyud na yod pa'i sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga po logs su phyung ba'am/ cha mthun pa'i rgyud do/ /de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs gsang
ba rgyan gyis bkod pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ paNDi ta su ga ta shrI dang / chos rje sa skya pa'i 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor bdun yod do/ /gsang ba nor bu thig
le'i rgyud/ paNDi ta bde gshegs dpal dang sa skya lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /'di rnams kyi brgyud pa/ phur pa rtsa dum dang mthun no/ /gsum pa
spyod pa'i rgyud la/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang / pad ma dang / rdo rje'i rigs gtso bor ston pa'i rgyud sde gsum las/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs gtso bor ston pa rnam par snang
mdzad chen po mngon par byang chub pa rnam par 'phrul ba byin gyis rlob pa'i rgyud/ rtsa ba'i rgyud rim par phye ba nyi shu rtsa drug dang / rgyud phyi ma gsang ba mchog
gi rim par phye ba la/ rim par phye ba bdun/ paNDi ta shi leNDa boddhi dang / lo tsA ba dpal brtsegs kyi 'gyur/ 'di la rtsa ba'i rgyud la dbang bskur ba'i dkyil 'khor
gsum/ rgyud phyi ma la gcig yod/ 'di'i rgyud phyi ma da dung ma rdzogs pa 'dra ste/ 'grel par rgyud phyi ma nas drangs pa'i lung rnams ma byung ba'i phyir ro/ /brgyud pa
ni/ sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal/ dze ta ri/ mya ngan med pa'i dpal/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ ba ri ba nas sa skya pa la'ang rgyud/ ba ri ba nas mchims pa lnga la brgyud pa ni/ brtson
seng / don ne/ chos seng / blo brtan/ nam mkha' grags/ chos rgyal 'phags pa/ blo chen/ seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba man 'dra'o/ /de bzhin gshegs pa'i
rigs kyi yum la sogs pa ston pa'i rgyud ni ma rnyed la/ de'i rigs su gtogs pa'i bka' nyan/ mi g.yo ba'i rgyud ni/ de bzhin

gshegs pa thams cad kyi khro bo'i rgyal po ni mi g.yo ba'i stobs dpag tu med pa brtul phod pa 'dul bar gsungs pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po/ paNDi u pa sha ma rakShi
ta dang / lo tsA ba glan dar ma blo gros kyi 'gyur 'di la dkyil 'khor gsum tsam yod cing / rnam snang mngon byang dang cha mthun par yod pas spyod pa'i rgyud do/ /pad ma'i
rigs kyi rgyud ni ma rnyed do/ /gsum pa/ rdo rje'i rigs kyi rgyud la/ phyag na rdo rje dbang bskur ba'i rgyud dum bu gsum pa 'og min du gsungs pa dang / grong khyer dpal
yon 'byung ba'i gnas su gsungs pa gnyis/ bam po bcu gnyis pa/ paNDi ta shrI lendra boddhi dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor bzhi yod cing / da dung
cung ma rdzogs pa 'dra'o// ! //ja pa la/ lha mo brgyad kyi gzungs/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gnyis yod cing / phyag na rdo rje dbang bskur ba'i skabs nas phyung pa 'dra'o/ /phyag
na rdo rje gos sngon po can le'u bcu gsum pa/ paNDi ta tsi lu dang / lo tsA ba zangs dkar ba 'phags pa shes rab kyi 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /brgyud pa
ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ Ao tsArYa dmar po/ sog tshul khrims bla ma/ ye shes 'bar/ zhang chos grags/ jo btsun sangs rgyas/ rig sngags rdo rje/ chos sgong pa skye med/
chos rgyal/ gzi brjid rgyal mtshan/ mtha' dong pa/ zhang blo rin/ bsod seng / gar thig pa/ bka' bcu pa/ spru ston/ mkhan chen shes rdor man gong bzhin no/ /rdo rje sa 'og
gi rgyud le'u bdun pa ni/ paNDi ta dI paM kA ra dang / lo tsA ba bya'i gdong can gyis 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo
rje/ spyod mdzad chos kyi rdo rje/ kun tu bzang po/ 'gro bzangs snying po/ rin chen rdo rje/ bram ze saddza

na/ te dzo de ba/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba/ grags seng / sangs rgyas don grub/ dpal ldan seng ge rgyal tsha lung mangs pa/ lo mchog blo chen/ seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen
shes rdor nas gong bzhin no/ /rdo rje sa gsum du rgyu ba'i rtog pa le'u lnga pa/ paNDi ta ku mA ra karmma badzra dang / rwa bying lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa lag na rdo
rje gos sngon po can zhes bya ba 'jig rten gsum 'dul ba'i rgyud le'u lnga pa/ paNDi ta dI paM kA ra dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor bzhi
yod/ brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas nas/ gshen ston gyi bar drag po gsum 'joms dang 'dra/ de nas dmar chos rgyal/ dmar thub pa shes rab/ mar shes rab rdo rje/ dmar brtson 'grus
seng ge dmar shAkya grub/ slob dpon ston seng / bla ma kun dga' bsod nams/ gan pa rin rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje nas gong bzhin no/ ! /bzhi pa bya ba'i rgyud la/
rigs so so'i rgyud dang / rigs thams cad kyi spyi'i rgyud dang gnyis kyi dang po la/ de bzhin gshegs pa dang / pad ma dang / rdo rje dang / nor can dang / lnga rtsen dang
/ 'jig rten pa'i rigs dang drug gi dang po la/ rigs kyi gtso bo dang / rigs kyi bdag po 'khor los bsgyur ba dang / rigs kyi yum dang / gtsug tor dang / rigs kyi khro bo
khro mo dang / rigs kyi pho nya pho mo dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su btu ba'i bya ba dang / gnas gtsang ma'i lha la sogs pa'i rgyud dang / brgyad du bshad pa la dang
po ni/ dam tshig gsum bkod pa'i rgyal po'i rgyud/ bikShu kr-iShNa paNDi ta dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal ba'i 'gyur/ 'di dang gong gi phyag rdor dbang bskur ba'i
rgyud gnyis kyi brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal/ dze tA ri pa/ a shwo ka

shrI/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ don yod rdo rje/ ba ri ba nas sa skya pa yab sras la brgyud cing / yang ba ri ba nas mchims pa bzhi ni/ brtson seng / don ne/ chos seng / blo gros brtan
pa/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog blo chen/ bde ba can pa seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje nas gong bzhin no/ /de bzhin gshegs pa bdun gyi smon
lam gyi khyad par rgyas pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ shlau ka brgyad brgya pa/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / shI lendra boddhi dang / lo
tsA ba bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur ba'o/ /sman gyi bla bai DUrYa 'od kyi sngon gyi smon lam byed par rgyas pa'i mdo/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la
dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba bandhe ye shes sde la sogs pas bsgyur zhing zhus te skad gsar chad kyis bcos nas gtan la phab pa/ gnyis kyi brgyud pa/ mdo'i brgyud rim bzhin
no/ /'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi stobs bskyed pa bai DUrYa'i 'od ces bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / su rentra
boddhi dang / bandhe ye shes sdes zhus te gtan la phab pa las/ phyis paNDi ta dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na dang / lo tsA ba tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba'o/ /sman la sngags
kyis btab pa ni/ 'di nyid kyi sman bla'i snying po logs su phyung ba yin pas rgyud tha dad du mi bgrang ngo / /nor bu zab mo rgyas pa'i gzhal med shin tu rab tu gnas
pa gsang ba dam pa'i cho ga zhib mo'i rgyal po le'u bdun pa/ paNDi ta birYa ka ra pra bha wa dang / lo tsA ba dpal gyis lhun pos bsgyur ba las/ slad kyi paNDi ta de nyid
dang / lo tsA ba dpal rtsegs kyis bsgyur ba/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po gsang ba ring srel gyi za ma tog ces bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta bidhya ka ra pra
bha wa dang / lo tsA ba rtsangs de bandhe rakShi tas

bsgyur ba/ byang chub snying po'i rgyan 'bum nas btus pa'i gzungs/ 'di'i rgyud tshang ba gcig bod du 'gyur yod par 'dug btsal bar bya'o/ /sangs rgyas bcu gnyis pa'i gzungs
paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / lo tsA ba bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur cing skad gsar chad kyis gtan la phab pa/ sangs rgyas bdun pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/
sangs rgyas thams cad kyi yan lag dang ldan pa'i gzungs/ sangs rgyas snying po zhes bya ba'i chos kyi rnam grangs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / lo tsA
ba bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur zhing gtan la phab pa/ yang de dang 'gyur 'dra ma 'dra lag len gcig paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / bandhe ye shes sdes
bsgyur ba/ 'phags pa me tog brtsegs pa zhes bya'i gzungs/ 'phags pa dri ma med pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa tsandan gyi yan lag ces bya ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa rten
cing 'brel pa 'byung ba'i snying po'i cho ga'i gzungs/ dge slong nor ban rakShi tas tho gar gyi yul nas rnyed pa/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba zhes bya ba theg pa chen
po'i mdo/ 'phags pa ye shes ta la la zhes bya ba 'gro ba thams cad yongs su sbyong ba'i gzungs/ sa'i snying po'i gzungs/ 'di dang rig sngags kyi rgyal mo kun nas 'od ces
bya ba gnyis 'gyur khyad ma gtogs pa cig go /'phags pa gdon mi za ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa sgo mtha' yas pa sgrub pa'i gzungs/ 'di phyag rdor dbang bskur ba'i rgyud las yum
du bshad mod kyi/ 'grel par thub pas gtso byas pa'i dkyil 'khor bshad pas de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyud du'ang mi 'gal bas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rgyud du'ang byas so/ /'phags
pa sgo drug pa zhes bya ba'i

gzungs/ chos thams cad kyi yon tan bkod pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'di'i lung ma thob/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po pra dznyA warmma dang / su rendra boddhi dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA
ba bandhe ye shes sde la sogs pas zhus cing gtan la phab pa'o/ /sgrol ma mchog gi gzungs zhes bya ba/ 'phags pa gzungs chen mo/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI
la dang / bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa'o/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa yi ge nyung ngu / 'di yum gyi rigs su byas na'ang rigs mod kyi/ gzungs
spyi'i cho ga kun snang gsal ba las thub pa'i gzungs su bshad cing / mdo'i nang nas thub pa'i snying po ston pa yin pas thub par yang mi 'gal lo/ /sher phyin gyi snying
po zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ paNDi ta bi ma la mi tra dang / lo tsA ba sgro rin chen sde'i 'gyur/ 'di yang yum gyi skor du byas shing rigs mod kyi/ slob dpon
klu sgrub kyi thub pa gtso 'khor lnga'i sgrub thabs mdzad pas de la brten nas thub par mdzad do/ /sangs rgyas 'khor dang bcas pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags
dang bcas pa la/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa 'di/ gzhan gyi mi thub pa zhes bya ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs
kyi gzungs chen po gcig yod par bshad/ de nas phyung ba yin pa 'dra'o/ /'di nyid nas/ gzhan gyis mi thub gzungs gsan nas/ /zhes gsungs pa'i phyir ro/ /shAkya thub pa'i
snying po'i gzungs/ 'phags pa rnam par snang mdzad chen po zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ snang ba mtha' yas rjes su dran pa'i gzungs/ 'di zlos sam brtag zla 'od kyi mtshan rjes
su dran pa'i gzungs/ de bzhin gshegs pa spyi'i snying po rjes su dran pa'i gzungs/ sangs rgyas rin chen gtsug tor can gyi mtshan rjes su dran pa'i gzungs/ mchod pa'i sprin
gyi gzungs/ 'phags pa pad ma can zhes bya ba'i

gzungs/ sU rU pa'i gzungs/ 'jigs pa chen po brgyad las bsgrol ba'i gzungs/ khyad par can gyi gzungs 'di la/ rgya gar na sbrul lo la sogs pa'i rnam bzhag med pa la/ stag lung
du/ bi kra ma shI la'i paNDi ta maM ga la shrI dznyA na'i phyag bris kyi gzungs 'dus kyi rgya dpe 'dug pa na/ nA ga sbrul lo barSha zhes rgyud nyid kyi gleng bzhi'i rgya
dpe na snang zhing rgya dpe tshang ma 'dug go de'i rnam bzhag byas pas/ the tshom gyi gzhi gcig tu snang mod kyi/ ratna rakShi tas byas zer ba'i gzungs spyi'i cho ga kun
snang gsal ba las/ 'jam dbyangs gzhon nus gsungs pa yi/ /khyad par can gyi gzungs la bstod/ /ces byas 'dug go /gnyis pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi 'khor los bsgyur ba
'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi skor la/ 'jam dpal gyi rtsa ba'i rtog pa sum cu so drug pa/ paNDi ta gzhon nu bum pa dang / lo tsA ba shAkya blo gros kyi 'gyur/ brgyud pa ni/ rdo
rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/ bram ze sa ra ha/ bde ba'i rdo rje/ dad byed go cha/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po/ rkyang po chos blo/ bra'o lha 'bum/ bra'o chos tshul/
bra'o mi mnyam rdo rje/ thang ston ye shes rdo rje/ zhang byang chub pa/ blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can pa seng rgyal/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor
nas gong bzhin no/ /dpa' bo gcig tu grub pa zhes bya ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po le'u bzhi pa/ paNDi ta dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA na dang / lo tsA ba dge ba'i blo gros
kyi 'gyur/ brgyud pa ni/ ba ri ba nas sa skya pa la brgyud nas/ ye pa'i bar dang / yang / bikSha de ba dang / shAkya shrIH glo bo lo tsA ba/ 'phags pa/ ye pa/ kun seng /
bde ba can pa seng rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje man gong bzhin no/ /'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi zhal nas gsungs pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs paNDi

ta dznyA na garbha dang / lo tsA ba klu'i dbang po'i 'gyur/ slad kyi paNDi ta bi shuddha singha dang / lo tsA ba de ba tsandras bsgyur ba/ 'jam dpal gyi dmod pa gtsugs pa zhes
bya ba'i gzungs/ 'jam dpal gyis dam bcas pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'jam dpal gyi mtshan zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'jam dpal gyi shes rab blo 'phel gyi gzungs/ 'jam dpal gyi
yi ge 'bru gcig pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs rnams so// ! //gsum pa ni/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa rnams dang / shes rab kyi pha rol phyin
pa ke'u shi ka zhes bya ba gnyis te/ de gnyis ni yum yin no/ /gser 'od dam pa mchog tu rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba'i mdo sde le'u sum cu so gcig pa/ mgos chos grub kyi
rgya dpe las bsgyur ba 'di la dkyil 'khor drug yod par gsal lo// ! //nya pa la/ gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po le'u nyi shu rtsa dgu pa/ paNDi ta dzI na mi
tra dang / shI lendra boddhi dang / bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur zhing / skad gsar chad kyis kyang gtan la phab pa'o/ /'di la'ang dkyil 'khor drug tu gsal lo/ /gser 'od dam
pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po zhes bya ba le'u nyi shu rtsa gcig 'di la dkyil 'khor gnyis su gsal lo/ /de gsum gleng gzhi dang bstun na de bzhin gshegs par yang gsal
mod kyis/ gser rgyal yum gyi gzungs yin cing de'i skabs su yum gyi cho gar gsungs pas 'dir yum gyis phyogs su byas kyi/ gzhan du ji ltar rig par bya'o/ /stong chen mo rab
tu 'joms pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ stong chen mo nas phyung ba sman la sngags kyi btab pa/ rigs sngags kyi rgyal mo rma bya chen mo/ rma bya'i yang snying / rigs sngags
kyi rgyal mo so sor 'brang ma zhes bya ba/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / lo tsA ba ye

shes sdes bsgyur ba/ rig sngags kyi rgyal mo gsil ba'i tshal chen mo'i mdo/ gsang sngags rjes su 'dzin ma zhes bya ba'i mdo/ paNDi ta shI lendra boddhi/ dznyA na siddhi dang
/ shAkya pra bha ba dang / lo tsA bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur cing / skad gsar chad kyis gtan la phab pa/ brgyud pa ni/ bhU mi kIrti dang / mar pa/ gze ba blo brtan/ jo
bod/ don grub ye shes gnyis ka la khams pa shAkya rdo rjes zhus/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo mchog sgra tshad pa rin rgyal/ chos rgyal/ gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rab
rdo rje nas gong bzhin no/ /'phags ma 'od zer can zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta a mo ghas phyung ba'i rtog pa'i rgyal po dang / 'od zer can gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga 'od
zer 'byung ba'i rgyud stong phrag bcu gnyis pa las phyung ba/ mchog tu snying por gyur pa'i 'od zer can gyi rtog pa brgya phrag bdun pa las phyung ba 'od zer can gyi rtog
pa 'di bya ba'i rgyud min pa 'dra yang / 'od zer can phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i phyir ro/ /rig sngags kyi rgyal mo rgyal ba can zhes bya ba/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang /
dA na shI la dang / bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa/ 'phags pa rgyal ba can zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ de'i ming du de bzhin gshegs pa'i snying po dang
phyag rgya zhes bya ba gsungs pas/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi lha mor byas so/ /'phags pa dbang bskur ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI
la dang / bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur cing zhus te skad gsar chad kyis gtan la phab pa'o/ /'phags pa dbyig dang ldan pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'gyur gong bzhin no/ /'phags
pa dug sel zhes bya ba'i rigs sngags/ 'phags pa klags pas 'grub pa sor mo can zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa gtsug gi nor bu zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ dzi

na mi tra dang / shI lendra boddhi dang / bandhe ye shes bsgyur ba/ 'phags pa yi ge drug pa'i rig sngags/ sher phyin stong phrag brgya pa'i gzungs/ stong phrag nyi shu lnga
pa'i gzungs/ 'phags pa brgyad stong pa'i gzungs/ phar phyin drug gi snying po'i gzungs/ phar phyin thob par 'gyur ba'i gzungs/ phar phyin bcu thob par 'gyur ba'i gzungs/
tshad med bzhi thob par 'gyur ba'i gzungs/ phar phyin stong phrag brgya pa gzung bar 'gyur ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa phal po che gzung bar 'gyur ba'i gzungs/ sdong po bkod
pa gzung bar 'gyur ba'i gzungs/ ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po gzung bar 'gyur ba'i gzungs/ rma bya chen mo gzung bar 'gyur ba'i gzungs/ so sor 'brang ba chen mo gzung bar 'gyur
ba'i gzungs/ lang kar gshegs pa'i mdo thams cad klags par 'gyur ba'i gzungs so/ /'di rnams gzhan gyi nang nas bsdus par snang ste/ gang nas btus pa de'i khongs su gtogs
par shes par bya'o/ /yum gyi skabs 'di tsho nye bar gzung nas gzhag gi khro mo dang / pho nya mor ci rigs pa yod par blta'o/ /bzhi pa la/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad
kyi gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs dkar mo can gzhan gyis mi thub pa phyir bzlog pa'i rig sngags kyi rgyal mo chen mo 'di la 'grel pas dkyil 'khor bzhir bshad do/ /de bzhin
gshegs pa thams cad kyi gtsug tor nas byung ba'i gdugs dkar mo can gzhan gyis mi thub ma phyir bzlog pa chen mo mchog tu grub pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta pa ra
he ta dang / lo tsA ba zu dga' ba'i rdo rje'i 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug tor nas byung ba gzhan gyis mi thub ma zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug
tor nas byung ba gzhan gyis mi thub ma zhes bya ba'i

gzungs/ lha yul ma chung bar grags pa kha che'i paNDi ta ma hA dza na'i rang 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma zhes bya ba'i gzungs rtog pa
dang bcas pa/ yang de bzhin gshegs pa'i gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs rtog pa dang bcas pa/ paNDi ta chos kyi sde dang / ba ri lo tsA ba'i 'gyur/ yang
gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs rtog pa dang bcas pa chung ba/ 'phags pa ngan 'gro thams cad sbyong ba gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/
paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / su rendra boddhi dang / bandhe ye shes sde'i 'gyur ro/ /gtsug tor rnam par rgyal ma'i gzungs zhes bya ba'i rtog pa rab byed dang po/ mkhan
chen nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di la sngags oM dgu ma dang / lha sum cu so gsum gyi dkyil chog yod/ kun nas sgor 'jug pa'i 'od zer gtsug tor dri ma med
par snang ba'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi snying po dang dam tshig la rnam par lta ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'di la 'grel pas dkyil 'khor brgyad gsungs so/ /shes pa
thams cad mthar phyin par grub pa'i mchod rten zhes bya ba'i gzungs 'di gtsug tor dri med kyi lag len du snang ste/ rgyud rang yin min the tshom za'o/ /mchod rten gcig btab
pas bye ba btab par 'gyur ba'i gzungs dang cho ga ni/ rnam snang 'od kyi rgyal po'i gzungs nas/ bod kyis gang mkho ba rnams bsdus par snang ngo / /'od zer dri ma med
pa rnam par dag pa'i 'od ces bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta bidhya ka ra singha dang / lo tsA ba dpal gyi lhun po'i sdes bsgyur ba'o/ /'di gtsug tor dngos ma yin kyang gtsug tor
dang cha mthun zhing mchod rten bya ba'i tshul dang cho ga mthun pas phyogs gcig tu bkod do/ /snying rje'i mchog ces bya ba'i

gzungs 'di gtsug tor yin te/ gtsug tor nas byung ba'i snying rje'i mchog ces bya ba'i phyir ro/ /lnga pa khro bo rnam par rgyal ba shin tu gsang ba'i rgyud/ rtsa ba'i rgyud/
rgyud phyi ma dang bcas pa'i le'u nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa'o/ /'phags pa rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi gzungs/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang / skyo 'od 'byung gi 'gyur/ 'phags pa
be con chen po'i gzungs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shi la dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ gzhan gyis mi thub pa rin po che'i phreng ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi
ta su rendra boddhi dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ bar du gcod pa thams cad sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / bandhe ye shes
sde'i 'gyur// ! //ta pa la/ 'phags pa thams cad la mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa zhes bya ba lo paN gong bzhin/ 'phags pa 'gro lding pa'i gzungs/ lo paN gong bzhin/ 'di 'phags pa
ra wi ta'i rig sngags dang gnad gcig go /tshigs su bcad pa gnyis pa'i gzungs/ 'di sngags don la khro bor gsal lo/ /khro mo'i skor la/ rgyal mtshan rtse mo'i dpung rgyan zhes
bya ba'i gzungs/ lo paN gong bzhin/ 'phags ma bskul byed ma'i gzungs rnams so/ /drug pa la/ 'phags pa sgo bzang po zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'di la khro bo'am/ pho nya mo
ci rigs su yod do/ /'phags pa bu mang po ston pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa ro langs bdun pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta bi shuddha singha dang / bandhe ye shes
snying pos bsgyur ba las/ slad kyi paNDi ta bidhyA ka ra singha dang / bandhe ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa mtshan mo bzang po zhes bya ba'i mdo/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra
dang / dA na shI la dang / bandhe ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ mdangs phyir 'phrog pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/

'phags pa mig rnam par sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i rigs sngags/ 'phags pa mig nad rab tu zhi bar byed pa zhes bya ba/ 'phags pa gzhang 'brum rab tu zhi bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i
mdo/ lo paN gong bzhin/ 'phags pa nad rab tu zhi bar byed pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ rims nad zhi bar byed pa'i gzungs/ 'phags pa rims rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i gzungs/ 'brum
bu'i nad rab tu zhi bar byed pa'i gzungs/ mdangs phyir mi 'phrog pa zhes bya ba/ 'phags pa yangs pa'i grong khyer du 'jug pa'i mdo/ paNDi ta su rendra boddhi dang / bandhe
ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa mi rgod rnam par 'joms par zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa bar du gcod pa thams cad sel ba'i gzungs sngags pho nya'i 'khor du gtogs pa
bka' nyan pho nya mo la/ 'phags pa mi g.yo ba'i gzungs le'u dgu pa/ paNDi ta dharmma shrI mi tra dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ khro bo'i rgyal po rtog pa
bsdus pa'i rgyud ces bya ba le'u bcu pa/ 'phags pa gser can zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ bdun pa la/ de bzhin
gshegs pa'i rigs su bsdud pa'i byang chub sems dpa'i skor la/ spyan ras gzigs kyi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa/ byams pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa
brgyad pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa/ nam mkha'i snying po/ kun tu bzang po/ lag na rdo rje/ 'jam dpal/ sgrib pa rnam sel/ sa'i snying po rnams kyi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad
pa gzungs sngags dang bcas pa ste/ brgyad po 'di sngar gyi glegs bam rnams su sangs rgyas kyi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa dang sbrel nas 'byung zhing / gleng gzhi bzhi
phal cher 'brel nas 'dug pas/ rgyud gcig nas phyung ba yin na de'i khongs su gtogs la/ sems dpa' so

so'i rgyud/ rang byung ba yin na sems dpa'i khongs su gtogs pas brtag par bya'o/ /'dir re zhig sems dpa'i dbang du byas so/ /'jam dpal gyi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad snying po
dang bcas pa/ byams pas dam bcas pa'i gzungs/ 'phags pa dkyil 'khor brgyad pa'i gzungs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ bdud rtsi
'byung ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ yi dwags kha nas me 'bar ba la skyabs mdzad pa'i gzungs/ yi dwags kha nas me 'bar ma la dbugs dbyung ba'i gzungs/ ye shes skar mda'i snying
po/ 'di bzhi byang sems kho na'i rigs su nges pa med kyang / byang chub sems dpa'i bya ba yin pas byang sems kyi rigs su bkod do/ /shes rab bskyed pa'i gzungs/ thos pa
'dzin pa'i gzungs/ 'phags pa rgyal ba'i bla ma'i gzungs/ rgyas pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su gtogs pa'i gnas gtsang ma'i lha la sogs pa la mdo chen po 'dus pa chen po'i
mdo zhes bya ba/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dzI na mi tra dang / pra dznyA warmma dang / bandhe ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa chos kyi rgya mtsho zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi
ta su rendra boddhi dang / pra dznyA warmma dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ gegs sel ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ mdo chen po kun tu rgyu ba dang / kun tu rgyu ba ma yin pa dang
mthun pa'i mdo zhes bya ba/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / pra dznyA warmma dang / bandhe ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ sprin chen po'i mdo las char dbab pa zhes bya ba le'u drug
cu rtsa bzhi pa cho ga dang bcas pa/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / su rendra boddhi dang / bandhe ye shes sdes bsgyur cing skad gsar chad kyis bcos nas gtan la phab pa/
'phags pa sprin chen po'i rlung gi dkyil 'khor gyi le'u klu thams cad kyi snying po zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo klu'i rgyal po gzi can gyis zhus pa zhes

bya ba'i gzungs/ gza' yum 'gyur mi 'dra tsam pa gnyis/ nor gyi rgyun gyi gzungs/ nor rgyun ma'i rtog pa/ tshogs kyi bdag po'i snying po/ tshogs bdag gi rgyud le'u bco lnga
pa/ jo bo rje dang / 'brom rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas kyi 'gyur/ nag po chen po'i rgyud le'u brgyad pa/ paNDi ta don yod rdo rje dang / lo tsA ba phur bu 'od kyi 'gyur/ dpal
mgon po nag po zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa nag po chen po'i gzungs rims nad thams cad las thar bar byed pa zhes bya ba/ lha mo nag mo chen mo'i gzungs/ dpal lha mo la
bstod pa'i rgyud/ lha mo nag mo'i mtshan brgyad pa/ de ltar de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs kyi rgyud bkod nas/ gnyis pa pad ma'i rigs kyi rgyud bkod na/ rigs kyi gtso bo dang
/ rigs kyi bdag po dang / rigs kyi yum dang / rigs kyi khro bo khro mo dang / rigs kyi bka' nyan pho mo'i rgyud dang lnga'i dang po la/ 'phags pa tshe dang ye shes dpag
tu med pa zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ oM gsum byas pa bar na paNya yod pa gcig dang / oM gnyis byas pa bar na puNye med pa gcig ste cha gnyis/ 'phags pa tshe dang
ye shes dpag tu med pa zhes bya ba'i snying po 'chi med rnga sgra'i gzungs/ paNDi ta shU nya tA saM bha ba dang / pa tshab nyi ma grags kyi 'gyur/ snang ba mtha' yas kyi
gzungs/ snang ba mtha' yas rjes su dran pa'i gzungs/ yon tan sngags pa dpag tu med pa'i gzungs/ bde ldan gyi snying po 'di rnams sngags dang ston pa po'i mtshan nyid la dpyad
na/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i rigs su gsal yang / bla ma dag 'od dpag med pad ma'i rigs kyi gtso bor bzhed do/ /gnyis pa rigs kyi bdag po 'khor los bsgyur ba/ spyan ras gzigs
kyi rgyud la/ spyan ras gzigs rtsa ba'i rgyud kyi rgyal po pad mo drwa ba

zhes bya ba le'u bcu gnyis pa/ paNDi ta so ma shrI bha dra dang / lo tsA ba kyu ra tshul khrims 'od zer gyi 'gyur/ 'di la dkyil 'khor nyi shu rtsa bdun du byas so/ /brgyud
pa ni/ paNDi ta dharmma shrI bha dra dang / 'gar lo tsA ba/ glan ston shes rgyal/ dbab byang sems/ dmar ston/ ye ston dar yes/ chos dbang / lo mchog lo chen/ gar thig pa/
mkhan chen shes rdor nas gong bzhin no// ! //tha pa la/ 'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i bsgyur 'phro bam po nyi shu rtsa bzhi tshang ba bzhugs/ don yod zhags pa'i snying po
zhes bya ba theg pa chen po'i mdo/ paNDi ta a mo gha badzra dang / lo tsA ba ba ri rin chen grags kyi 'gyur/ 'di cho ga zhib mo'i 'go na yod pa'i snying po dang spyir 'dra
ba la/ sngags la mang nyung khyad che bar snang ngo / /don yod zhags pa'i snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs ni/ gsan yig na/ 'phags pa don yod zhags pa'i pha rol du phyin
pa drug yongs su rdzogs par byed pa'i gzungs blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur zhes pa dang gcig gam btag dkar chag na so so/ mi cig na lung ma thob bo// sngar gyi gzungs las
snying po logs su bkol nas khrus chog byed tshul dang bcas pa bod kyi logs su phyung bar snang ngo / /'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug lag pa stong dang mig stong dang
ldan pa'i cho ga zhib mo 'di la dkyil 'khor gcig yod do/ /'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug phyag stong spyan stong dang ldan pa thogs pa mi mnga' ba'i thugs rje chen
po'i sems rgya chen yongs su rdzogs pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ mgos chos grub kyi rgya'i dpe las bsgyur ba/ 'di snga ma dang gnyis 'dra la ming 'dra cig snang ngo / /'phags
pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gsang ba'i mdzod thogs pa med pa yid bzhin gyi 'khor lo'i snying po'i le'u drug pa/ bandhe chos grub kyi rgya'i dpe las bsgyur ba/ 'phags
pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug

zhal bcu gcig pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug zhal bcu gcig pa'i rigs sngags kyi snying po bandhe chos grub kyi rgya'i dpe las bsgyur ba/ spyan
ras gzigs dbang phyug gi gzungs/ 'phags pa nI la kantha zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ snying rje mi shom pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ kun tu bzang po zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ 'jig rten
dbang phyug gi rtog pa/ paNDi ta dzambha la dang / lo tsA ba ba ri'i 'gyur/ 'di bya rgyud yin min brtag go /thugs rje chen po pad ma cod paN gyi rgyud le'u bcu gcig pa
paNDi ta dharmma shrI mi tri dang / lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang po'i 'gyur/ 'di'i brgyud pa pad ma drwa ba dang mthun no/ /seng ge sgra'i rgyud/ paNDi ta pra dznyA ka ra dang
/ lo tsA ba mgos khug pa lha btsas kyi 'gyur/ spyan ras gzigs seng ge sgra'i gzungs/ rje btsun ma rdo rje sems ma dang / lo tsA ba 'gar shes rab 'byung gnas kyi 'gyur/
seng ge sgras dam bcas pa'i gzungs/ paNDi ta ngag gi dbang phyug dang / lo tsA ba klog kya shes rab brtsegs kyi 'gyur// ! //da pa la/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug
gi mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa/ rgyal ba thams cad kyi ring srel za ma tog ces bya ba/ yang de dang don 'dra ba la mtshan brgya rtsa lhug par yod pa gcig lung ma thob/
'di gnyis 'gyur khyad ma gtogs pa gcig tu snang ngo / /'phags pa lus kyi dbyibs mdzes pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta pra dznyA warmma dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/
'phags pa gzhan gyi mi thub pa mi 'jigs pa sbyin pa zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ lo paN gong bzhin/ stong 'gyur ba zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ shlau ka rgya lobs pa cha gnyis/ stong
lobs pa cha gnyis/ mi brjed pa'i gzungs/ shes rab bskyed pa'i gzungs/ paNDi ta dznyA na garbha dang / klu'i dbang po'i

'gyur la/ biddhyA ka ra singha dang / de ba tsandras bcos pa/ yang shes rab bskyed pa'i gzungs/ thos pa 'dzin pa'i gzungs/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin gyis brlabs

dbang phyug gi yum zhes bya ba'i gzungs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / lo tsA ba bandhe ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum sgrol

gda' kha ye shes dang / 'phags pa sangs rgyas kyi mdzod kyi chos zhes bya ba bam po bzhi pa/ 'di dpyad gzhi can du 'dug gsan yig na 'dug pas lung ni nyan/ (nya)pa la/ 'phags
pa rgyan stug po'i bkod pa ji snyed pa'i mdo bam po bzhi le'u brgyad pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi byin rlabs sems can la gzigs shing sangs rgyas kyi zhing
gi bkod pa kun tu ston pa/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / su rendra boddhi dang / klu'i rgyal mtshan dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'dir tshig kha shas mi gsalbkod pa'i rgyal
po zhes bya ba/ paNDi ta pra dznyA warmma dang / su rendra boddhi dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa bde ba can gyi bkod pa dang / 'phags pa za ma tog bkod pa bam po
bzhi/ dkon mchog za ma tog ces bya ba bam po bzhi/ ratna rakShi ta'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa dkon mchog 'byung gnas zhes bya ba bam po bdun pa dang / 'phags pa rin po che'i mtha'
zhes bya ba/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ (ta)pa la/ 'phags pa gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po che ba theg pa chen po'i mdo bam po
bcu pa/ le'u nyer dgu/ paNDi ta dA na shI la dang / lo tsA ba rnam par mi rtog pa'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa gser 'od dam pa mdo sde'i dbang po'i rgyal po chung ba/ le'u nyi shu
rtsa gcig pa/ bam po lnga pa dang / gser 'od dam pa mchog tu rnam par rgyal ba mdo sde'i rgyal po le'u sum cu so gcig pa bam po bcu/ lo tsA ba mgos chos grub kyi 'gyur/ 'phags
pa gser gyi bye ma lta bu zhes bya ba/ paNDi ta su rendra boddhi dang / pra dznyA warmma dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ (tha)pa la/ chos thams cad kyi rang bzhin
mnyam pa nyid rnam par spros pa 'phags pa ting nge 'dzin rgyal po bam po bco lnga/ le'u sum cu so brgyad/ paNDi ta shI lendra boddhi dang / lo tsA ba dharmma shI la'i

'gyur/ chos nyid rang gi ngo bo nyid las mi g.yo bar tha dad par thams cad snang ba'i mdo bam po gsum/ 'phags pa rab tu zhi ba rnam par nges pa'i cho 'phrul gyi ting nge 'dzin
bam po gsum/ le'u so brgyad/ paNDi ta dze na mi tra dang / dA na shI la dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin le'u dgu paNDi
ta su rendra boddhi dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i ting nge 'dzin bam po gnyis/ ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ 'phags
pa dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin bam po lnga/ le'u bcu dgu/ paNDi ta shAkya pra bha dang / lo tsA ba ratna rakShi ta'i 'gyur/ skad gsar bcad kyis bcos pa/ (da)pa la/
'phags pa da ltar gyi sangs rgyas mngon sum du bzhugs pa'i ting nge 'dzin/ bam po bdun/ le'u nyer lnga/ paNDi ta shAkya pra bha dang / lo tsA ba ratna rakShi ta'i 'gyur/
'phags pa bsod nams thams cad bsdus pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi mdo/ bam po bzhi/ le'u lnga bcu/ paNDi ta pra dznyA warmma dang / shI lendra boddhi dang / lo tsA ba ye shes
sde'i 'gyur/ bar 'di nas rdo rje'i ting nge 'dzin zer ba'i brdzun ma cig 'dug pa gsan yig na med pas bton/ 'phags pa khyi'u bzhi'i ting nge 'dzin/ bam po gsum/ le'u/ paNDi

bcu gnyis/ paNDi ta shI lendra boddhi dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ rdo rje snying po zhes bya ba'i gzungs kyi mdo/ bam po/ le'u/ paNDi ta shI lendra boddhi dang

'gyur/ sangs rgyas kyi sa zhes bya ba'i mdo/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / shI lendra boddhi dang / pra dznyA warmma dang / lo tsA ba ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ sangs rgyas mi spang

rigs thams cad mkhyen pa'i bshes gnyen/ klu sgrub/ ArYa de ba/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ ratna a kA ra shanti/ rdo rje gdan pa che ba bar pa/ chung ba/ paN chen shAkya shrI/
dpyal chos kyi bzang po/ dpyal pad ma can/ mkhan po gzhon nu ye shes/ rong pa sher seng / shab pa bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ bla ma mgon po 'bum/ spru ston bsod rgyal/
mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ slob dpon bsod nams seng ge rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags pa/ chos kyi rje shAkya rgyal mtshan/
des bdag la'o// ! //yang bag ston gzhon tshul gyi/ shab stod kyi g.yu dga' ldan du rong pa shes rab seng ge la mdo mangs kyi lung gsan rjes su/ mkhan po gzhon nu ye
shes dang / bla ma rong pa sher seng gi bar du hor khung yod zer ba dang / pad mo can pa dang / gzhon ye'i bar na'ang hor khung yod dam zer ba la brten nas/ lung dag par
bya ba'i phyir/ sa skya pas dgon pa bla ma zhang kun dga' 'od zer la/ paN chen nas brgyud pa'i lung dag po yod zer nas gsan pa'i brgyud pa ni/ paN chen yan sngar dang 'dra
la/ paN chen shAkya shrI nas/ lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ rkong nag ral gri/ jo gdan zas gtsang / shangs pa grags seng / zhal snga ba bsod rin/ mkhan po gzhon nu ye shes/
se ston 'byung ldan 'od/ mang mkhar ba byang chub seng ge zhang kun dga' 'od zer/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ slob dpon mgon po 'bum/ spru ston bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen
shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal

shes rab/ slob dpon bsod nams seng ge rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags/ rje btsun dam pa shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o// ! //'di la'ang paN chen yan chad
la brgyud pa'i nges pa mi 'dug cing / paN chen la yang dpyal chos bzang gi khro phur gsan pa'i dus lho pas kyang gsan pa yin nam zer ba las/ gsan pa'i nges pa tig pa mi
'dug nas/ yang mdo mangs kyi brgyud pa spyi dang / so so nas brgyud pa dag par btsal nas gsan pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma chos kyi rgyal po 'gro ba'i mgon po 'phags pa'i gsung
gis spyil phu ba stag ston shes rab 'od zer la mdo mangs kyi lung dag pa cig tshol gsung nas btsal bas/ shangs pa grags seng la mnga' bdag nyang ral nas brgyud pa'i lung
dag po yod zer nas gsan no/ /de nas brgyud pa/ sa skya yang dgon pa blo chen la yod zer ba slob dpon gzhon tshul pas gsan nas/ gzhon tshul gyis blo chen la lo gsum du
rdzogs par gsan pa'i grangs ni/ sngar gyi mdo nyi brgya nyer lnga po rnams dang / de'i steng du/ gser 'od dam pa klag pa tshe'i mdo/ byams pas dam bcas pa/ rdo 'phang ba
bam po gnyis/ ting nge 'dzin gyi chos kyi yi ge mau'u 'gal gyi mdo bam po gcig mdzod dang 'jig rten brjod pa'i mdo bam po gcig bar mtshams ma lus par 'grel ba/ klu'i rgyal
po rnga sgra'i tshigs su bcad pa/ chos kyi rgyal mo/ 'di la bam po gnyis wa pa'i zhabs na 'dug the tshom can du 'dug go/ dgra bcom pa dge 'dun 'phel lung bstan pa/ sangs
rgyas rjes su dran pa'i ting nge 'dzin gyi rgya mtsho/ 'jig rten gzhag pa bam po brgyad/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad/ phyag 'tshal ba'i bstod pa/ nor
bu rin po che thabs la mkhas pa/ tshangs pa'i drwa ba/ byams pas zhus pa/ rnam par mi rtog pa la

'jug pa'i gzungs/ byang chub kyi phyogs bstan pa/ sangs rgyas kyi stobs bskyed pa'i cho 'phrul bstan pa/ rgyal ba'i blo gros kyi zhus pa/ gnas gsum du skye ba blangs pa'i mdo/
sangs rgyas rjes su dran pa'i mdo/ li yul lung bstan pa/ theg pa chen po chos kyi mdzod/ rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i dang po rnam par dbye ba bstan pa/ sangs rgyas
dbang bskur ba'i bstod pa rin chen bzang po/ las gdags pa/ dam pa'i chos dran pa nye bar gzhag pa'i tshig le'ur byas pa/ byams pa dga' ldan du skye ba blangs pa'i mdo/
ljon shing gi mdo/ rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyi bsngo ba/ mtshan mo bzang po gsung gi snying po zhes bya ba'i le'u/ 'phags pa thabs la mkhas pa'i mdo/ nor bu rin po che thabs
la mkhas pa yongs su bsngo ba'i rgyal po/ sangs rgyas kyi mdzod chos kyi yi ge 'di ja pa la 'dug pa dpyad gzhi can no// shes pa mthar phyin par grub pa'i mchod rten gyi
gzungs/ ting nge 'dzin mchog dam pa/ theg pa chen po gcig tu bstan pa/ don dam par grub pa'i le'u/ chos bstan pa'i mdo/ yon tan mdo sde rnam par gdon mi za ba'i mdo/ las
bden don thob pa yongs su bstan pa/ theg pa chen po'i chos kyi rgya mtsho/ mau'u 'gal gyi bus ma dmyal ba nas drangs pa'i mdo/ 'phags pa chos thams cad kyi yon tan bskyed
pa'i mdo/ spyan ras gzigs kyis zhus pa'i chos bdun pa'i mdo ste/ mdo zhe drug po dang bcas te nyis brgya don gcig rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ byams
pa/ thogs med/ dbyig gnyen/ sangs rgyas bskyangs/ sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ dri med sbas pa/ rin chen rdo rje/ dharmma a kA ra shAnti ba/ de la paNDi
ta dznyA na shrI dang / jo bo puNya shrI gnyis kyi mdo mangs rnams gsan nas/ de gnyis las brgyud pa gyes

pa mang ba yin zhes dag par smra ba rnams zhal 'cham par gsung / de gnyis ka'i slob ma paNDi ta su ma ti kIrti/ de la smr-i ti dznyA na kIrti/ de la rong zom lo tsA ba chos
kyi bzang pos zhus/ des mnga' bdag ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ des mnga' bdag nyang ral pa can/ lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ spang khang pa grags rgyal/ shangs pa grags seng
/ spyil phu ba stag ston shes rab 'od zer/ sa skya yang dgon pa blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mgon po 'bum/ spru ston bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen

rngog lo'i bu chen gro lung pa chen pos/ stengs pa lo tsA ba la khyod rgya gar du song la/ bye brag bshad mdzod dang / skye rabs dpag bsam 'khri shing la sogs pa sngar bod
du ma 'gyur ba rnams dang / khyad par du mdo mangs kyi lung dag pa tshang ba gcig tshol la shog gsung nas brdzangs te/ der stengs pa lo tsA bas rgya gar du byon te rtsad
bcad pas/ paNDi ta dznyA na shrI dang / puNya shrI gnyis las mdo sum brgya rtsa dgu re'i lung rnam par dag pa yod zer la/ de gnyis kyang puNya shrI dag cing rgya yang
che zer nas/ puNya shrI la zhus so/ /de la stengs los gsan pa de khungs dag par dgongs nas lho pa thams cad mkhyen pas zhus/ de'i brgyud pa/ srang phag khur ba la yod zer
ba/ slob dpon gzhon nu tshul khrims pas tshor bas/ sngar nas kyis thob zin kyang / skyar nas gsan pa sngar gyi mdo sna nyi brgya don gcig po rnams dang de'i steng du/ sngar
ma thob pa lhag po zhus pa ni/ mdo khang bu rtsegs pa/ ye shes can gyis zhus pa'i mdo/ ye shes pad dkar gyi mdo/ bkod pa'i

kyi lung bstan pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i bgro ba/ sangs rgyas kyi sde snod tshul khrims ngan pa tshar gcod pa/ dad pa'i stobs bskyed pa/ nam mkha' mdzod kyis zhus pa'i
mdo/ tshangs pa khyad par sems kyis zhus pa/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i gzugs brnyan gzhag pa'i phan yon kun du rgyu sen rings kyis zhus pa/ rten 'brel gyi mdo/ sangs rgyas kyi
rtogs pa brjod pa shes ldan gyi mdo/ phyir mi ldog pa 'khor lo'i mdo/ chos kyi phyag rgya'i mdo/ sgres mos zhus pa/ theg pa chen po la dad pa rab tu bsgom pa/ sbyin pa'i
pha rol tu phyin pa'i mdo/ mi'am ci'i rgyal po ljon pas zhus so/ /yang dag par spyod pa'i tshul gyi nam mkha'i mdog gis 'dul ba'i bzod pa'i mdo/ bsod nams kyi rtogs pa brjod
pa/ rgyu gdags pa/ rgyal bu don grub kyi mdo sde thams cad sgrol gyi rtogs brjod/ mngon par 'byung ba'i mdo/ mdo chen po stong pa nyid ces bya ba/ mdo chen po stong
pa nyid chen po zhes bya ba/ blo gros mi zad pa bstan pa/ drin lan bsab pa/ gsal rgyal gyi tshigs bcad/ me tog gi tshogs kyi mdo/ las kyi sgrib pa rgyun gcod pa/ don dam
pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs/ byang chub sems dpa'i spyod pa bstan pa/ rnam par 'thag

pa thams cad bsdus pa/ bud med 'gyur ba lung bstan pa/ bu mo zla mchog lung bstan pa/ mar me 'bul ba'i mdo/ chos kyi phung po'i mdo/ blo gros rgya mtshos zhus pa/ glang po'i
rtsal gyi mdo/ sangs rgyas kyi dbu rgyan/ de bzhin gshegs pa'i ye shes kyi phyag rgya'i ting nge 'dzin/ chos kun 'gro ba/ sA lu ljang pa/ ma dros pas zhus pa/ sa'i snying
po 'khor lo bcu pa/ khyi'u bzhis zhus pa'i ting nge 'dzin/ klu'i rgyal po rgya mtshos zhus pa/ klu'i rgyal po rgya mtshos zhus pa chung ba/ zung gi mdo'i chos kyi rnam
grangs/ dpa' bar 'gro ba'i ting nge 'dzin/ rab tu zhi ba rnam par nges pa'i cho 'phrul gyi ting nge 'dzin/ ma skyes dgra'i 'gyod pa bsal ba/ rnga bo che chen po'i mdo/ da
ltar gyi sangs rgyas mngon sum du bzhugs pa'i ting nge 'dzin/ 'phags pa chos bzhi pa/ gnas 'jog gi mdo/ bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rgyal po'i mdo/ chos thams cad 'byung ba
med par bstan pa/ pha rol du phyin pa lnga bstan pa'i le'u re re la rdzogs so re yod pa/ spyod yul yongs su dag pa'i mdo ste/ mdo bdun bcu don lnga dang / de'i steng du
thar los bsgyur pa'i/ chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i mdo/ skyes rabs kyi gleng gzhi'i bshad pa/ lcang lo can gyi pho brang gi mdo/ 'dus pa chen po'i mdo/ byams pa'i mdo/ byams
pas bsgom pa'i mdo/ tshul khrims lnga'i phan yon bstan pa'i mdo/ tshe dang ldan pa ri'i kun dga'i mdo/ klu rgyal dga' bo dang nye dga' 'dul ba'i mdo/ gnas brtan 'od srungs
chen po'i mdo/ nyi ma'i mdo/ zla ba'i mdo/ bkra shis chen po'i mdo sde bcu gsum dang bcas pas brgyad cu gya brgyad kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'phags
pa 'jam dpal/ ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ sman zhabs/ rgyal bas byin/ ratna

shrI/ shAnti badzra/ karmma badzra/ puNya shrI/ dza ya shrI/ bi dza ya rakShi ta/ thar lo nyi ma rgyal mtshan/ phag 'khur dkon mchog bla ma/ bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims/
slob dpon mgon po 'bum/ spru ston bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ slob dpon bsod nams seng ge rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags
pa/ bla ma rin po che shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ /'dus pa rin po che tog gi gzungs kyi le'u'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag rdor/ dze ta ri/ rdo rje gdan pa
che ba/ bar pa/ chung ba/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ gnyan ston grags pa rgyal mtshan/ gnyan rin chen grags pa/ gnas brtan dkon mchog seng ge de'i sras sdog dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/
lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ blo chen sangs rgyas sras/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon/ bde ba can pa seng ge rgyal mtshan/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor/ chos dpal
shes rab/ bsod nams seng ge rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma dam pa shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ ! /'phags pa sangs rgyas bdun pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag
rdor/ rdo rje gdan pa/ bar pa/ chung ba/ puNya shrI/ stengs pa lo tsA tshul khrims 'byung gnas/ so thams cad mkhyen pa/ so 'dzam gling rgyan/ lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa/
rkong nag ral gri/ jo gdan zas gtsang / shangs pa grags seng / rin chen 'bum/ bde ba can pa ye shes mgon/ gar thig pa/ shes rdor ba/ chos dpal shes rab/ bsod nams seng
ge rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ ! /gsum pa ni/ gzhan yang mtshungs myang 'das chen mo/ pa ma mchis pa'i bka' drin can/ chos kyi rje
chos kyi mdzod chen po de las/ mdo

myang 'das chen mo rgya nag 'gyur bam po zhe brgyad dam nga gnyis ma dang / gtsug tor bam po dgu pa las bdud kyi le'u nyi tshe phyung ba 'di dpyad dgos/ le'u dang po dang /
le'u gnyis pa bcom ldan 'das kyi gtsug tor chen po'i mdo las bam po gnyis 'di yang de ltar ro// yod pa dang / gser 'od dam chen bam po bcu pa dang / thabs la mkhas pa sangs
rgyas kyi drin lan bsab pa dang / tshe dpag med rgyas pa/ ri bo chen po'i mdo/ 'od zer can gyi mdo rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'jam dpal/ klu sgrub/
paNDi ta byang chub bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs sprul pa zhu thun/ gyim btsun ja/ ten zhi du go zhi/ tshing lang go zhi/ gyi'i hU~M/ hA'i hri tha'i/ gyi ju/ seng chen gyin/
sing ga sang / gying ju/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ ra sa pa ston shAka bag ston gzhon tshul/ mgon po 'bum/ chos rje thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams
rgyal mtshan/ mkhan chen shes rdor/ chos dpal shes rab/ puNya singha / rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags/ rje btsun dam pa shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/
! /yang / myang 'das brgyud pa gcig ni/ mgon po 'bum yan 'dra/ spru ston bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor/ chos dpal shes rab/ mtha' rtsa'i mkhan chen grags pa rdo rje/
rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags pa/ bla ma dam pa shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / mkhan chen shes rdor/ 'bri khung lo tsA/ khams pa byang rgyal/
bla ma bsod shes/ bla ma gzhon nu dar/ rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags pa/ chos rje shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la gnang ba'o/ ! /de yang spyir mdo
sde rin po che'i bka' lung 'di la/ rgya gar du paNDi ta puNya shrI

dang / dznyA na shrI gnyis kyis 'bad pa byas par grags la/ bod du dang po stengs pa lo tsA ba dang / lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa gnyis kyis/ bla ma dang brgyud pa mi gcig pa
mang po la gsan nas dka' ba cher spyad la/ dus phyis bla ma bag ston gzhon nu tshul khrims kyis dka' spyad mang po mdzad/ bla ma 'di snyed cig la yang dang yang du zhus
shing gtugs pas/ bod na yod pa'i brgyud srol thams cad mnga' ba yin pas/ de nyid las brgyud pa'i lung bka' 'di dag pa yin no/ /bla ma 'di nyid la slob dpon mgon po 'bum gyis
mdo mangs kyi lung thams cad rdzogs par gsan cing / de la spru ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ de la thog ston mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ de la spru ston chos dpal shes
rab/ de la slob dpon bsod nams seng ge de la 'tshal yang dgon gyi rin po che grags don pa/ de la bla ma rin chen grags pa/ de la bla ma rin po che shAkya rgyal mtshan/
de la thu ston kun dga' rnam par rgyal ba bdag gis thob pa'o// ! //yang swa lu ljang pa'i mdo'i brgyud pa gcig ni/ slob dpon ston chos/ dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ chos rgyal
'phags pa rin po che/ tshad ma'i skyes bu/ bu ston rin chen grub/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ chos dpal shes rab/ puNya singha / rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma shAkya rgyal
mtshan/ des bdag la'o// ! //yang / phal chen/ bla ma dam pa de nyid las/ dam pa'i chos shin du rgyas pa chen po sangs rgyas phal po che/ smad ga chad/ sdong po bkod pa/
bzang spyod kyis mjug bsdud dang bcas pa/ shlau ka sum khri dgu stong sum cu/ bam po brgya dang sum cu dang shlau ka sum cu pa legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ yang dag
par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal/ klu sgrub/ de la paNDi ta byang

chub bzang po dang / paNDi ta dga' ba gnyis kyis zhus so/ /de gnyis kas rgya nag tu 'gyur mdzad cing / des thu thu zhun/ gyim btsun dza/ ten zhi du go zhi/ tshing lang go zhi/
gyi hU~M/ ha'i hrI tha'i/ gyi ju/ son chen gyin/ sing ga sang / gying ju/ des dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bsod nams seng ge gar
thig pa bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes rab/ mtha' rtsa'i mkhan chen grags pa rdo rje/ rin po che grags pa don grub/ dgra bcom pa rin
chen grags pa/ bla ma shAkya rgyal mtshan zhabs/ des bdag la'o/ ! /yang / mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ 'bri khung lo tsA ba/ khams pa mtsho dkar ba byang rgyal/ bla ma bsod
shes/ mtha' rtsa'i bla ma gzhon dar/ rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags pa/ bla ma shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des bdag la gnang ba'o// //shu bhaM// //@/ /bla ma dam
pa shAkya rgyal mtshan pa las mdo sde dkon mchog brtsegs pa thob yiggzhan yang / sems dpa' chen po shAkya'i mtshan can de'i zhal sgor/ mdo sde dkon mchog rtsegs pa chos
kyi rnam grangs le'u stong phrag brgya pa las/ bod du le'u 'am dum bu lnga bcu tham pa 'gyur ba yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i chos kyi rnam grangs dang brgyud pa

ni// (ka)pa la/ sdom pa gsum bstan pa'i mdo bam po phyed bzhi dang shlau ka bcu'o/ /dum bu gnyis pa 'phags pa sgo mtha' yas pa rnam par sbyong ba chos kun nas gsang ba'i mdo
bam po bzhi'o/ /dum bu gsum pa gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdo bam po bcu gcig shlau ka nyi brgya/ le'u nyi shu rtsa lnga pa'o/ /dum bu bzhi pa rmi lam nges par bstan
pa'i mdo/ bam po gsum dang shlau ka brgya'o/ /dum bu lnga pa bde ba can gyi zhing bkod bstan pa bam po gsum pa'o// (kha)pa la/ dum bu drug pa 'phags pa mi 'khrug pa'i
zhing bkod bstan pa/ bam po lnga dang shlau ka bzhi bcu'o/ /dum bu bdun pa 'phags pa go cha bkod pa bstan pa/ dum bu brgyad pa chos dbyings rang bzhin gyis dbye ba med pa
bstan pa'i mdo/ dum bu dgu pa theg pa chen po chos bcu bstan pa'i mdo/ bam po phyed dang gnyis dang / shlau ka lnga bcu pa'o/ /dum bu bcu pa 'phags pa kun nas mdo/ shlau
ka nyi brgya drug bcu'o/ /dum bu bcu gcig pa 'od zer kun du skye ba bstan pa'i mdo/ bam po lnga'o/ /dum bu bcu gnyis pa 'phags pa 'jam dpal gyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing gi
yon tan bkod pa bstan pa'i mdo/ bam po phyed dang bzhi pa'o// (ga)pa la/ dum bu bcu gsum pa 'phags pa byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod kyi mdo bam po nyi shu/ le'u bcu gnyis
pa'o/ /dum bu bcu gsum pa dga' bo mngal du 'jug pa bstan pa'i mdo bam po gcig pa'o/ /dum bu bco lnga pa dga' bo rab tu byung ba'i mdo/ bam po phyed dang bzhi'o// (nga)pa
la/ dum bu bcu drug pa 'phags pa yab sras mjal ba de kho na nyid nges par bstan pa'i mdo/ bam po bco lnga pa'o/ /dum bu bcu bdun pa 'phags pa gangs pos zhus pa'i mdo/
le'u brgyad bam po drug pa'o/ /dum bu bco brgyad pa/ 'phags pa

yul 'khor skyong gis zhus pa'i mdo bam po gsum dang / shlau ka bdun cu rtsa bdun pa'o/ /dum bu bcu dgu pa khyim bdag drag shul can gyis zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po gsum pa'o// (ca)pa
la/ dum bu nyi shu pa/ 'phags pa klog thob kyis zhus pa mdo/ bam po gnyis so/ /dum bu nyer gcig pa sgyu ma mkhan bzang po lung bstan pa'i mdo/ bam po gcig dang shlau
ka brgyad cu rtsa gsum pa'o/ /dum bu nyer gnyis pa cho 'phrul chen po bstan pa'i mdo/ bam po gsum mo/ /lha'i bu ded dpon gyis zhus pa'i mdo yang zer/ dum bu nyer gsum pa
'phags pa byams pa seng ge'i sgra sgrogs pa'i mdo/ bam po bzhi'o/ /dum bu nyer bzhi pa 'phags pa nye bar 'khor gyis zhus pa'i mdo/ 'dul ba bstan la 'bebs par byed pa bam
po gnyis pa'o/ /dum bu nyer lnga pa lhag pa'i bsam pa bskul ba'i mdo bam po gnyis pa'o/ /dum bu nyer drug pa 'phags pa lag bzangs kyis zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po gnyis dang shlau
ka brgya'o/ /dum bu nyer bdun pa/ 'phags pa des pas zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po gcig shlau ka brgya dang bdun cu rtsa brgyad do/ /dum bu nyer brgyad pa byang chub sems dpa'
dpal sbyin gyis zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po gcig pa'o/ /dum bu nyer dgu pa bad pa'i rgyal po 'char byed kyis zhus pa'i mdo shlau ka nyis brgya'o/ /dum bu sum cu pa bu mo blo
gros bzang mos zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po phyed do/ /dum bu so gcig pa ganggA'i mchog gis zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po phyed do/ /dum bu so gnyis pa mya ngan med kyis sbyin pa lung bstan
pa'i mdo/ bam po phyed dang gnyis pa'o/ /dum bu so gsum pa/ 'phags pa dri ma med kyis sbyin pa lung bstan pa'i mdo/ bam po gnyis pa'o/ /dum bu so bzhi pa 'dir yi ge
gsal gyi mi 'dugzhus pa'i mdo/ bam po phyed do/ /dum bu so lnga pa sangs rgyas kyi yul

bsam gyis mi khyab par bstan pa'i mdo/ bam po gnyis pa'o/ dum bu so drug pa 'phags pa de bzhin gshegs pa lha'i bu blo gros rab gnas kyis zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po bzhi pa'o// (cha)pa
la/ gong gi bam po gsum pa nas/ dum bu so bdun pa 'phags pa seng ges zhus pa'i mdo shlau ka drug bcu pa'o/ /dum bu so brgyad pa sangs rgyas kyi gsang chen thabs la
mkhas pa'i mdo/ bam po bzhi pa'o/ /dum bu so dgu pa 'phags pa bzang skyong gis zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po gnyis dang / shlau ka sum cu'o/ /dum bu bzhi bcu pa bu mo rnam dag dwang
bas zhus pa'i mdo bam po gcig pa'o/ /dum bu zhe gcig pa/ 'phags pa byams pas zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po gcig dum bu zhe gnyis pa 'phags pa byams pas zhus pa'i chos brgyad
pa'i mdo/ shlau ka brgyad cu rtsa gsum pa'o/ /dum bu zhe gsum pa/ 'phags pa 'od srungs kyis zhus pa'i mdo/ bam po gnyis pa'o/ /dum bu zhe bzhi pa rin po che'i phung po'i
mdo/ bam po gnyis dang shlau ka brgyad cu pa'o/ /dum bu zhe lnga pa/ 'phags pa/ blo gros mi zad pas zhus pa lung bstan pa'i mdo shlau ka nyis brgya'o/ /dum bu zhe drug pa/

po sum cu dang shlau ka brgya/ le'u sum cu so gsum pa'i brgyud pa/ gser gling pa/ jo bo rje/ dge bshes 'brom ston pa/ nam mkha' go cha/ chag dbang phyug rgyal mtshan/ la
stod dkon mchog 'khar/ la stod dbang rin/ bla ma bkra shis rdo rje/ spong khrod 'dul 'dzin/ rta nag pa sgom she/ bla ma dar ma 'od zer/ bla ma blo gros rgyal mtshan/ bla
ma byang chub 'bum/ bla ma mtsho dkar ba byang rgyal/ bla ma yar lungs pa bsod nams shes rab/ bla ma gzhon nu dar/ rin po che grags don pa/ rje btsun shAkya rgyal mtshan
des bdag la'o/ /shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa rab kyi rtsal gyis rnam par

gnon pas zhus pa bam po bdun dang shlau ka drug cu/ shes rab kyi pha rol du phyin pa bdun brgya pa/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lnga brgya pa/ shI lendra boddhi dang /
dznyA na singha dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ rdo rje gcod pa bam po gcig shI lendra boddhi dang / ye shes sde'i 'gyur/ sdud pa bam po gcig tshul brgya lnga bcu pa/ kau'u
shi kas zhus pa shlau ka sum cu so gcig shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa shlau ka sum cu/ sgo nyi shu rtsa lnga pa/ yi ge nyung ngu / de bzhin
gshegs pa thams cad kyi yum yi ge gcig ma/ shes rab snying po/ shlau ka nyer lnga ste/ de rnams rim pa yin la/ de dag kyang / sdud pa/ shes rab snying po/ yi ge nyung ngu
/ yi ge gcig ma rnams la zab mo'i chos bzhir grags pa dang / bdun brgya pa/ lnga brgya pa/ brgya lnga bcu pa/ mtshan brgya rtsa brgyad pa/ tshul brgya lnga bcu pa/ sgo
nyi shu rtsa lnga pa ste/ grangs las mtshan du btags pa'i mdo drug rab rtsal gyis zhus pa/ kau'u shi kas zhus pa ste zhu ba po las mtshan du btags pa gnyis/ rdo rje gcod
pa rnams te/ de dag gi brgyud pa ni/ kha che dznyA na shrI/ su ma ti kIrti/ smr-i ti dznyA na kIrti/ ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ lho pa thams cad mkhyen pa/ bla ma grags pa
seng ge spyil bu ba bod she/ bla ma dar ma 'od zer/ bla zhig byang chub rdo rje/ bla ma ye shes mgon/ bla ma seng ge rgyal mtshan/ gar thig pa bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes
rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ slob dpon bsod nams seng ge rin po che grags don pa/ bla ma rin chen grags pa/ chos rje shAkya rgyal mtshan/ de'i bka' drin gyis
thu btsun kun dga' rnam par rgyal ba bdag la'o/ /shu bhaM// //

@/ /chos kyi rje shAkya dhwa dza las 'dul ba lung thob yigyang / bla ma dam pa rgyal ba'i gsung gi mdzod 'dzin de las/ dam pa'i chos 'dul ba lung gi lung tshang mar thob pa'i/
(ka)pa la/ thog mar rtsa ba'i lung dge slong gi so sor thar pa shlau ka bdun brgya bam po gnyis dang / dge slong ma'i so sor thar pa shlau ka brgyad brgya/ bam po gnyis/
kha che bye brag tu smra ba'i slob dpon dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba bandhe klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa dang / lung sde
bzhi'i dang po 'dul ba bzhi shlau ka sum khri nyis stong bdun brgya/ bam po brgyad dang dgu bzhugs pa'i bam po nyi shu pa yan bzhugs// (kha)pa la/ bam po nyer gcig pa nas
zhe gnyis pa'i bar bzhugs// (ga)pa la/ bam po zhe gsum pa nas re bzhi pa yan bzhugs// (nga)pa la/ bam po re lnga pa nas gya bdun pa yan bzhugs// (ca)pa la/ bam po gya brgyad
pa nas brgya dang dgu pa yan gyis 'dul ba bzhi rdzogs pa/ pusti 'di la 'gyur mi 'dug chos 'byung dang gsan yig mthun par/ paNDi ta sarbba dznyA de ba dang / bidyA ka
ra pra bha dang / dharmA ka ra dang / lo tsA ba bandhe dpal gyi lhun pos sgyur cing / slad kyi paNDi ta bidyA ka ra dang / lo tsA ba bandhe dpal rtsegs kyis zhus te gtan
la phab pa rnams bzhugs/ lung sde bzhi'i gnyis pa lung rnam 'byed la/ dge slong pha'i rnam 'byed shlau ka nyi khri bzhi stong pusti 'di na nyi khri lnga stong zer ba 'dug
dgu cu bam po brgyad cu rtsa gsum bzhugs// (cha)pa la/ bam po nyer gnyis pa yan bzhugs// (ja)pa la/ bam po nyer gsum pa nas zhe bzhi pa yan

bzhugs// (nya)pa la/ bam po zhe lnga pa nas re drug pa yan bzhugs// (ta)pa la/ bam po re bdun pa nas gya gsum pa'i bar bzhugs/ paNDi ta dzi na mi tra dang / zhu chen gyi lo
tsA ba bandhe klu'i rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur cing zhus te gtan la phab pa dang / dge slong ma'i rnam 'byed bam po nyi shu rtsa brgyad bzhugs pa'i bam po so drug pa yan bzhugs//
(tha)pa la/ bam po bdun pa nas nyer brgyad pa'i bar bzhugs pa kha che'i mkhan po sarbba dznyA de ba dang / dharma ka ra dang / rgya gar gyi mkhan po bidyA ka ra pra
bha dang / lo tsA ba bandhe dpal gyi lhun pos bsgyur cing / slad kyis paNDi ta bidyA ka ra pra bha dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba bandhe dpal rtsegs kyis bsgyur cing zhus
te gtan la phab pa/ lung sde bzhi'i gsum pa/ gzhung bla ma'am dam pa zhu ba rdzogs pa bam po lnga bcu rtsa gsum tshang ba dang / zhu ba ma rdzogs pa bam po bcu gnyis bzhugs
pa'o// (da)pa la/ zhu ba rdzogs pa'i bam po nyer gcig pa yan bzhugs// (na)pa la/ bam po nyer gnyis sad nas/ bam po zhe gnyis pa yan bzhugs// (pa)pa la/ bam po zhe gsum
pa man tshang ma dang / zhu ba ma rdzogs pa bam po bcu gnyis/ pusti 'di la 'gyur byang mi 'dug gsan yig na klu'i rgyal mtshan 'gyur/ lung sde bzhi'i bzhi pa lung phran
tshegs sgo brgyad kar rdzogs pa bam po lnga bcu rtsa dgu chos 'byung dang mthun/ bzhugs pa'o// (pha)pa la/ bam po nyi shu pa yan bzhugs// (ba)pa la/ bam po nyer gcig pa
nas so dgu pa yan bzhugs/ de nas pusti mtha' ma/ (ma)pa la/ bam po bzhi bcu pa nas/ drug bcu yan bzhugs pa rgya gar gyi mkhan po bidyA ka ra pra bha dang / dharmma shrI
pra bha dang / lo tsA ba bandhe

dpal 'byor gyi sgyur ba/ 'di rnams kyi brgyud rim ni/ yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas 'od srung chen po/ kun dga' bo/ sha na'i gos can/ nyer sbas/ bha shrA nanta/ dhi
dhi ka me tsA ka rnag pa/ purNaya/ gang po/ de rnams dgra bcom pa'o/ /slob dpon rta dbyangs/ ku mA ra la/ gzhon nu rol pa/ shrI ma ti/ blo gros dpal/ ha ri bha dra/ seng
ge bzang po/ shu ra ba/ dbyig gnyen/ shu ra zer ram/ dpa' bo/ ba su mi tra/ dbyig bshes/ ba su li/ dbyig bshes/ 'di rnams rgya gar gyi paNDi ta'o/ /saM gha bha dra/ dge 'dun
bzang po/ I shwa ra/ dbang phyug kaMndha li/ phung sa len/ saM gha bha dra/ dge 'dun bzang po/ mi gang pa'i bshes/ tra/ dharmma tattra/ chos sbyin datta e yin/ buddha
de ba/ sangs rgyas lha/ dha ra tattra/ sa sbyin/ 'di rnams kha che'i slob dpon no/ /puNya se na/ bsod nams sde/ saM ga se na/ dge 'dun sde/ puNya nanta/ bsod nams dga'/
dznyA na tsandra/ ye shes zla ba/ dznyA na so ma/ ye shes zla ba/ a sho rakShi ta/ mya ngan med pa'i 'tsho/ sarba rakShi ta/ thams cad srungs ba/ dharmma ko sha/ chos kyi
mdzod/ 'di rnams khu sen gyi slob dpon no/ /dharmma rakShi ta/ chos kyi srung ba/ ka lya Nya rakShi ta/ dge srungs/ pra dznyA rakShi ta/ shes rab srungs/ shrI mArga u pa
de sha/ dpal lam nye bar ston/ mokShaM rakShi ta/ so sor srungs ba/ ka lya Na rakShi ta/ thar srungs ba/ pi dzi ta pra bha/ rnam rgyal ba'i 'od/ a mri ta warmma/ bdud rtsi
go cha/ 'od kyi 'byung gnas sde pa/ pra bha ka ra se na/ mdo mdzod ste/ a dhi dhya se na A di tya se na nyi ma'i sde/ mArga/ lam nyer ston/ nyer ston/ u pa de she/ las
ka'i sde/ saM gha se na/ dge 'dun sde/ shI la ta pa/ tshul khrims sde 'od/ ta pa dngos su tsha gdung gi ming ste 'od la'ang rung bas/ ya sha ta pa/ grags pa'i sde 'od/ buddha
ta pa/ sangs rgyas sde 'od/ shikSha bha dra/ bslab pa bzang po/ gu Na so ma/ yon tan zla ba/ a sho ka mi dra/ mya ngan med pa'i bshes gnyen/ shu la dkar po'i bshes
gnyen/ mi dra/ dkar po'i bshes gnyen zhes pa ltar na shAkya mi tra thob/ shAkya mi dra/ shAkya bshes

gnyen/ de rnams yu gur gyi slob dpon gyi ming ngo / /de nas ka yol gyi slob dpon shI la mi tra/ de la bod kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen sangs rgyas 'bum gyi gsan/ de la bla ma chos
rgyal po rin po che dang / slob dpon ston pa bkra shis dpal gnyis kyi gsan/ slob dpon bkra shis dpal la/ dpal ldan sa skyar skyor mo lung gi slob dpon mngon pa bas gsan/
tshul khrims bshes gnyen/ de la skyor mo lung gi slob dpon mkhan po thams cad mkhyen pas gsan/ de gnyis ka la yang dbyen gyi mkhan po thams cad mkhyen pas gsan/ de la
thang po che'i 'dul ba 'dzin pa dpal gyis gsan/ de la mkhan po rin chen bzang pos gsan/ de la khu ston bkra shis bzang pos gsan/ de la chos sgo ba shI la bha dras gsan/
de la gu ru sing ha'i mtshan gyis gsan/ de la spyan snga ba grags pa don grub kyis gsan/ de la chos kyi rje shAkya rgyal mtshan gyis gsan/ des bdag la'o/ /shu bhaM// //@/
/chos rje shAkya rgyal mtshan pa las bstan 'gyur nas thob yigna mo manydzu nA tha ya/ byams brtser ldan pa'i shes rab mchog mnga' 'jig rten gnyen gcig gshin rje'i dgra/
/zhi la rab gzhol 'chi ba'i 'jig 'jams rtag tu bdud kyi tshogs kyi bdud/ /gdod nas grol yang 'gro ba rnams kyi thar pa'i slad du gzhon nu'i sku/ /rgyal sras mthu bo mtha'
dag rgyal ba'i yab gcig 'jam dpal dbyangs la 'dud/ /rgyal ba'i bka' yi tshogs pa dgongs 'grel bcas/ /gangs can 'di na ji snyed 'gyur mang gi /de

snyed glegs bam lung la mnga' mdzad pas/ /bdag cag thos mang mdzad pa khyod phyag 'tshal/ /gang bka' lung dri ma med pa mang du gsan pa'i chos kyis phyug pas/ bstan pa'i srog
shing chen por gyur pa chos kyi rje shAkya rgyal mtshan gyis zhabs las/ bod du 'gyur ba'i bstan bcos mtha' dag gi nang nas/ lung nod pa'i rim pa rnams bri bar bya ba ni/
rgyud sde thams cad kyi gong ma/ gnyis su med pa'i rgyud kyi gtso bo yin pa la sogs pa tshul gsum dang ldan pa'i gtan tshigs du ma'i sgo nas 'thad pa dang bcas par grub
pa'i phyir/ dpal kyai rdo rje'i skor rnams thog mar 'god par rigs mod/ 'on kyang re shig snga rabs pa 'ga' yis khrigs su sdebs pa'i ka tho'i lugs bzhin gsan pa ni// (ka)pa
la/ dpal dus kyi 'khor lo'i bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgya cher 'grel pa stong phrag bcu gnyis pa dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba/ byang chub sems dpa' spyan ras gzigs dbang
phyug gis mdzad pa las/ le'u dang po 'jig rten khams le'u mdor bsdus bcu'i bdag nyid/ le'u gnyis pa nang gi le'u mdor bsdus bdun gyi bdag nyid gnyis so// (kha)pa la/ le'u
gsum pa dbang gi le'u mdor bsdus drug gi bdag nyid/ le'u bzhi bcu pa sgrub thabs kyi le'u mdor bsdus lnga'i bdag nyid dang / le'u lnga pa ye shes kyi le'u mdor bsdus bzhi'i
bdag nyid rnams pad ma dkar pos mdzad pa/ kha che paNDi ta chen po so ma nA tha dang / 'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags kyis bsgyur ba las/ dus phyis shongs lo tsA ba
rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis bcos shing gtan la phab pa/ legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ dang po'i sangs rgyas/ dus kyi 'khor lo/ dpal ldan rgyu skar gyi dkyil 'khor chos dbyings
ngag dbang / shAkya thub pa/ 'bras dpung / zla ba bzang po/ shambha lar/ lha dbang / gzi

brjid can/ zla bas byin/ lha'i dbang phyug sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i dbang ldan/ grags pa/ pad dkar/ 'jam dbyangs sprul pa/ lho phyogs su/ tsi lu paNDi ta/ bhang ga lar/ si wa
rendra/ to A tsArYa/ dus zhabs che ba/ or 'bi par/ dus zhabs chung ba/ na lendrar/ lho phyogs su/ manydzu kArti/ sa manta shrI/ ser rang du/ rwa chos rab/ ne'u me tog rwa
ye shes seng ge kho lung seng khyi ru/ rwa 'bum seng / chos zhing dgon pa ru/ rje btsun rgwa lo/ e dmar du/ bla ma shes rab seng ge sham 'bar du/ bla ma rdo rje rgyal
mtshan/ rgyal po'i pho brang du/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin po che/ zhwa lu ri phug tu/ bla thar pa gling du/ ma chos dpal shes rab/ rin po che grags pa don grub/ chos
kyi rje bka' 'gyur ba shAkya rgyal mtshan/ des thu btsun kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po bdag la'o/ /de ni rwa lugs kyi brgyud pa'o// ! /'bro lugs kyi brgyud pa ni/
dang po'i sangs rgyas/ dus 'khor zhabs/ thub pa/ zla bzang lha dbang / gzi brjid can/ zla bas sbyin/ lha'i dbang phyug sna tshogs gzugs/ lha'i dbang ldan/ grags pa/ pad dkar/
bzang po/ rnam rgyal/ bshes gnyen bzang po/ phyag dmar/ khyab 'jug sbas pa/ nyi ma grags/ shin tu bzang / rgya mtsho rnam rgyal/ rgyal dka'/ nyi ma rgya/ sna tshogs
gzugs/ zla ba'i 'od/ mtha' yas/ sa skyong / dpal skyong / dus zhabs che ba/ dus zhabs chung ba/ kha che so ma nA tha/ kha che khri brtan du/ 'bro lo tsA ba shes rab grags/
rgya bod kyi/ bla ma lha rje sgom pa dkon mchog srungs/ 'phan yul ba/ sgro ston gnam la rtsegs/ co reg mgo bla ma yu mo mi skyod rdo rje/ dbang phyug tshul khrims/ sras
dharme shwa ra/ co reg mgo mkhas pa nam mkha' 'od zer/ co reg mgo grub btsun pa nam mkha' rgyal mtshan/ thob se mo che/ chos rje 'jam dbyangs gsar ma/ rje btsun rgwa

lo/ bla ma dus 'khor ba shes rab seng ge bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan pa/ thams cad mkhyen pa bu ston rin chen grub/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje
pa/ des bdag la'o// (ga)pa la/ spyan ras gzigs gyi sprul pa pad ma dkar pos mdzad pa'i don dam bsnyen pa paNDi ta zla ba mgon pos bsgyur ba'i brgyud pa ni/ byang chub
sems dpa'i sprul pa gcig la/ dge slong bsod snyoms pa chen pos gsan/ de la lho phyogs kyi bram ze dA ri ka pa/ tsi lu paNDi ta/ dus zhabs pa che chung / boddhi bha tra/ sA
dhu su tra/ a bha yA ka ra gupta/ rtsa mi sangs rgyas grags/ a bhi dzu ka pa/ dharmma pA dhU su tra/ dharmma a ka ra ta/ bhas ka ro ma/ se lo tsA ba tshul khrims gzhon
nu/ a bha ya ka ra la tshar gcig rtsa mi la tshar gnyis/ a bhi dzu ka la bstod gcig bhas ka ro la tshar gcig gsan/ de la gnyos 'od mas tshar gsum gsan/ se lo tsA ba bkra
shis rin chen/ sangs rgyas rdo rje/ grub chen u rgyan pa/ chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma gar thig pa/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags
don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o/ /dus kyi 'khor lo dbang mdor bstan gyi 'grel bshad don dam bsdus pa zhes bya ba/ phyag rgya chen po grub pa dpal nA ro zhabs kyis mdzad
pa/ kha che'i paNDi ta dharmma dha ra dang / lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba las/slar yang sgra tshad pa rin rgyal gyis dpal sa skyar bcos shing gtan la
phab nas zhus dag byas pa thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ nA ro pa/ dpe med mtsho/ a bha ya/ u pa tha na/ go taM shrI/ kIrti paNDi ta/ lo tsA ba grags pa rgyal mtshan/ rong pa
sher seng / chos skyong dpal/ bka' bcu ba gzhon seng / sa skya'i mngon dga' ba spru ston bsod

rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o// (nga)pa la/ dus 'khor lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/
paNDi ta buddha shrI dznyA na dang / lo tsA ba byams pa dpal gyis bsgyur ba thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ khro phu lo tsA ba byams pa dpal/ 'dzal phu ba sangs rgyas bsod dbang
/ khro phu rin po che bsod nams seng ge slob dpon zhang pa la/ bla ma gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ grags don pa/ chos rje
pa/ des bdag la'o/ /sbyor ba yan lag drug gi man ngag phyag rgya chen po grub pa zhes bya ba/ dang po'i sangs rgyas kyi rgyud las gsung pa/ a nu pa ma rakShi tas mdzad pa/
paNDi ta bi bhu ti tsandra dang / lo tsA ba mi mnyam bzang pos bsgyur ba/ de'i 'grel pa slob dpon nyi ma dpal ye shes kyis mdzad pa/ bi bhu ti tsandra'i rang 'gyur/ rnal
'byor gsum gyi snying po gsal ba zhes bya ba/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal rgyal po grags par skye ba bzhes nas mdzad pa/ paNDi ta so ma nA tha dang / lo tsA ba 'bro shes rab grags

ma gzhon nu tshul khrims/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o// ! /dus kyi 'khor lo'i man ngag nyi zla sgrub
pa zhes bya ba/ dus zhabs pas mdzad pa/ bi bhu ta tsandra'i rang 'gyur/ sha ba ra pa'i sbyor drug gzhung chung ngu grags pa/ bi bhu ta tsandra'i rang 'gyur gnyis thos pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ dus zhabs pa/ kha che zla ba mgon po/ lce sbrang yul ba/ pa tshab khrod pa'i dbon po zhang chung

ba/ mang yul gyi ston pa shrI dharma/ g.yor ru'i mgar ston/ 'dis bris nas phyag dpe blangs pas 'khyags nas phyag sor brul skad/ de la grwa pa mngon shes/ jo btsun tshul rin/
smon gro'i ljang sgom/ nye gnas mang yul ba/ 'phan yul gyi grab ston dkon mchog srungs/ sgro ston gnam la rtsegs/ yu mo mi skyod rdo rje/ sras dharmma shwa ra/ mkhas pa

tshig gi snying po bsdus pa zhes bya ba dang / de'i 'grel pa gnyis paN chen shAkya shrIs mdzad pa de nyid dang / lo tsA ba dpyal chos bzangs kyis bsgyur ba thos pa'i brgyud

'thag ces bya ba/ a nu pa ma rakShi tas mdzad pa/ paNDi ta su ga ta shrI dang / lo tsA ba dharmma kirti dang / rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis bsgyur ba thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ shongs

mkhar khyung / g.yu phug pa rgyal mtshan dge ba/ shongs lo tsA ba blo brtan/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ sgra tshad pa rin rgyal/ lha rje chos rgyal/ bla ma bsod rgyal/ bla
