chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o// (da)pa la/ mkha' 'gro rgya mtsho rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i 'grel pa gru rdzings zhes bya
ba/ slob dpon padma badzras mdzad pa shlau ka stong phrag brgyad pa/ le'u lnga bcu pa/ paNDi ta

rgyal ba'i sde dang / lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi yon tan gyis bsgyur ba thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ padma badzra/ padma badzra chung ba/ DoM bhi ba/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ rdo
rje gdan pa/ dha byang sems/ a bha ya/ dha shrI/ rgyal ba'i sde/ lo tsA ba chos kyi yon tan/ de'i dbon po sa mu dra/ sras seng rgyal/ bar thang pa yab sras/ sangs rgyas 'bum/
chos 'od/ zhang shes rgyal/ bla ma bsod nams 'phel/ ye shes mgon/ seng rgyal/ bka' bcu pa/ spru ston bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/
chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o// (na)pa la/ bcom ldan 'das 'khor lo sdom pa'i mngon par rtogs pa lU hi pas mdzad pa/ kha che ba'i mkhas pa/ shrAddha ka
ra warmma dang / zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur ba las/ slad kyi rdo rje slob dpon chen po rje btsun na ba ko ti pa ti'i zhal snga nas dang / bod kyi lo
tsA ba mgos lhas btsas kyis yul shar phyogs kyi dpe dang bstun te bcos pa/ dus phyis shar phyogs dza ga ta la'i paNDi ta chen po dA na shI las 'grel pa dang bstun nas cung
zad bcos pa thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen gzhon nu mgon/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o//
! /bde mchog lha lnga'i mngon rtogs yid bzhin nor bu rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti kIrti dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug
gis bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma seng rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des
bdag la'o// ! /'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang bskur ba'i rim pa mdor bsdus pa/ slob dpon rdo rje dril bus

mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po paNDi ta kriShNa dang / bod kyi lo tsA ba chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur ba/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i sgrub thabs kyi man ngag phyag rgya chen po grub
pa/ dpal dril bu zhabs kyi mdzad pa/ paNDi ta pra dznyA bha dra dang / lo tsA ba mal gyo blo gros grags pas bsgyur ba/ 'khor lo sdom pa'i rim pa lnga pa/ slob dpon dril
bu pas mdzad pa/ kriShNa paNDi ta dang / dge slong tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba las/ phyis su ma ti kIrti dang / dge slong blo ldan shes rab kyis bcos pa thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ bla ma seng rgyal ba/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o// ! /dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi
dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga rin po che rab tu gsal ba'i sgron ma'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon zla ba pas mdzad pa/ su ma ti kIrti dang / mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis
bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ thang tshul khrims mgon po/ slob dpon dkon mchog rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/
des bdag la'o// ! /nag po gzhung drug la/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi mngon rtogs nag po pas mdzad pa/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog gi dkyil chog nag po pas mdzad pa/ buddha
shrI shAnti dang / rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur las/ ga ya dha ra dang / lhas btsas kyi gtan la phab pa/ des mdzad pa'i sbyin sreg dharma bha dra dang / rig pa gzhon nus bsgyur
ba/ des mdzad pa'i dpyid kyi thig le zhes bya ba/ paNDi ta blo gros bzang po dang / lo tsA ba mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis bsgyur ba/ des mdzad pa'i rnal 'byor ma'i
rgyud kyi rgyal po'i rdzogs rim bshad pa gsang ba'i de kho na nyid rab tu gsal ba ga ya dha ra dang / mgos lhas btsas kyis

bsgyur ba las/ slad kyis su ma ti kIrti dang / mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis gtan la phab pa/ chos kyi phung po brgyad khri bzhi stong las bstan pa'i rim pa bzhi pa'i don/
slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po su ma ti kIrti'i zhal snga nas/ dge slong grags pa shes rab kyis bsgyur ba rnams thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma 'phags
pa/ bla ma dus 'khor ba/ bla ma 'jam dbyangs pa/ bla ma bag ston pa/ mkhan chen shes rdor ba/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag
la'o// ! /bde mchog yi ge bdun pa'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po ngag gi dbang phyug dang / klog kya shes rab rtsegs kyis bsgyur ba las/
phyis mar pa chos kyi dbang phyug gis zhus te gtan la phab pa thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ nag po gzhung drug dang mthun no/ /bde mchog gi mngon rtogs kyi rnam 'byed jo bo
rjes mdzad pa/ bde mchog lhan skyes kyi sgrub thabs rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ paNDi ta rdo rje gdan pa niska laM ka'i zhal snga nas dang / dpyal chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur
ba thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje gdan pa niska laM ka'i zhal snga nas/ dpyal lo tsA ba/ bla ma pad mo can pa/ nyi ma dpal/ mkhan chen gzhon yas/ dpal rin chen bzang
po/ rje btsun arYa shrI/ 'gro mgon kun dga' nyi ma/ kun mkhyen chos rgyal shes rab/ bla ma chos dpal ba/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o// (pa)pa la/
rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs slob dpon chen po dpal u rgyan gyi mi dbang indra buddhis mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dpal nA lendra pa dang / lo tsA ba dge slong
pra dznyA kIrtis bsgyur ba thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gzhung drug dang gcig go /rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sngags kyi de kho na

nyid nges par bstan pa/ slob dpon indra boddhis mdzad pa/ lo tsA ba ye shes sdes bsgyur cing gtan la phab pa thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ phag mo gzhung drug dang gcig go rnal 'byor
ma dmar mo'i sgrub thabs ri khrod dbang phyug gis mdzad pa thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen shes rab 'od zer/ bla ma chos dpal shes rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos
rje pa/ des bdag go /rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs gnam lcags lakShmi kA ras mdzad pa'i brgyud pa'ang / phag mo gzhung drug dang mthun no/ /rdo rje rnal 'byor ma
dkar mo'i sgrub thabs indra boddhis mdzad pa/ paNDi ta bai ro tsA na'i 'gyur thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma 'byung gnas grub/ blo gros brtan pa/ mkhan chen shes rab 'od zer/
bla ma chos dpal ba/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag go /phag mo gzhung drug ni/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i sgrub thabs zhal gnyis ma chung ba ri khrod dbang
phyug gis mdzad par grags pa/ paNDi ta bsod nams 'byung gnas bzang po dang / lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ phag mo'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid ye shes yang dag
par grub pa zhes bya ba zhal gnyis ma che bar grags/ paNDi ta stong nyid ting nge 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ paNDi ta bha rentra ru tsi dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi
'gyur/ don grub ma chung ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon a wa dhu ti pas mdzad pa dang / don grub ma che ba'i sgrub thabs ye shes dbab pa zhes bya ba/ dpal stong nyid ting nge
'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ dbu gcad ma chung ba'i sgrub thabs/ lha mo dpal gyi blo gros mas mdzad pa dang gsum/ paNDi ta ba rentra ru tsi dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab
kyi 'gyur/ dbu gcad ma'i sgrub thabs che ba zhes bya ba/ dpal birWa pas mdzad pa/ paNDi ta ba rentra ru tsi dang / lo tsA ba rma ban chos 'bar gyi 'gyur/ rdo rje

rnal 'byor ma'i gsang ba sbyin sreg gi cho ga sangs rgyas byin gyis mdzad pa/ paNDi ta bha rentra ru tsi dang / lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab kyi 'gyur/ gzhung drug sbyin sreg
dang bcas pa bod na grags pa'i rim pa ltar thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje phag mo/ lcam lakShmi ka ra/ birWa pa/ a wa dhu tI pa/ sha ba ra dbang phyug stong nyid ting
nge 'dzin bzang po/ bal po ha ngu dkar po/ dpyal kun dga' rdo rje/ rje btsun kun dga' grags/ lha lung pa rtag pa jo bzangs/ dpyal chos kyi bzang po/ pad mo can pa nyi ma
dpal bzang po/ mkhan chen gangs pa gzhon nu ye shes/ dpal rin chen bzang po/ kun dga' nyi ma dpal bzang po/ kun mkhyen chos rgyal shes rab/ bla ma chos dpal ba/ chos rje
grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o/ /rdo rje rnal 'byor ma rus sbal zhabs kyi sgrub thabs dang / kurma pA da ser mo thugs kyi sgrub thabs gnyis/ paNDi ta a nanda kA
ra'i zhal snga nas/ dpyal lo tsA ba chos kyi bzang pos bsgyur ba thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje phag mo/ sha ba ra pa/ mai tri pa/ na ya ka pa/ da pa ba la shrI/ bikSha
ta de wa/ paNDi ta A nanda ka ra/ dpyal lo/ rong pa rgwa lo/ bla ma shes rab seng ge bla ma kun dga' nyi ma dpal dang / bla ma kun mkhyen pa/ yang / dpyal lo/ padmo can
pa/ bla ma dga' ldan pa/ bla ma nyi ma dpal/ bla ma chos grub gzhon nu dpal/ bla ma kun dga' nyi ma dpal/ bla ma kun mkhyen pa/ bla ma chos dpal ba/ chos rje grags don pa/
chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o// ! /rnal 'byor ma'i bzhed kyi sbas pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon kongka byin gyis mdzad pa/ paNDi ta dha pa la ha'u dang / lo tsA ba rin
chen grags pas bsgyur ba/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma'i dgongs pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga slob dpon kongka byin gyis

rab/ chos rje grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o/ ! /mkha' spyod ma dkar mo'i bstod pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa/ paNDi ta de nyid dang / lo tsA ba rin chen bzang pos bsgyur

tsA ba rgya brtson 'grus seng ges bsgyur ba/ rnal 'byor ma'i bstod pa paNDi ta dI paM ka ra shrI dznyA nas mdzad pa/ paNDi ta de nyid

dang / lo tsA ba khu ne tsos bsgyur ba thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkha' spyod ma dkar mo'i bstod pa jo bo rjes mdzad pa dang mthun no// (ba)pa la/ dpal kye'i rdo rje'i bsdus pa'i
don 'grel byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje'i snying pos mdzad pa'i le'u lnga pa yin/ rgya gar gyi mkhan po dA na shI la dang / lo tsA ba 'bro se dkar shAkya 'od kyis bsgyur
ba/ slad kyis rgya gar gyi mkhan po su bhu ti shrI shAnti dang / lo tsA ba cog gru ting nge 'dzin bzang pos bsgyur ba/ yang / slad kyi rgya gar gyi mkhan po rgyal po'i
sras 'jigs med lha'i zhal snga nas dang / lo tsA ba snyel cor dge slong pra dznyA kirtis yul dbus kyi rgya dpe las gtan la phab/ slar yang / pang blo gros brtan pas gtan
la phab pa dang / kye'i rdo rje nges don gyi 'grel pa le'u drug pa man chad byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje snying pos mdzad pa/ paNDi ta mai tri zhabs dang / bod kyi lo tsA
ba 'bro shes rab grags pas bsgyur ba thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje snying po/ rdo rje DA ki ma/ a nu pa ma rakShi ta/ sA dhU pu tra/ dharmma mi tra/ bi khya te de ba/

badzra dang / shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ de phyin rdo rje mkha' 'gro las rtsa'i 'khor lo'i skabs zhes pa/ shAkya ye shes kyis bsgyur ba dang / dur khrod brgyad kyi bshad

/ kye'i rdo rje'i maNDal gyi cho ga slob dpon mtsho skyes kyis mdzad pa dang / kye'i rdo rje'i bstod pa/ bsham na

gos med sku la phyag 'tshal bstod/ ces pa yod pa dang / kye'i rdo rje'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga mtsho skyes rdo rjes mdzad pa dang / kye'i rdo rje dpa' bo gcig pa'i sgrub thabs/
slob dpon rdo rje dril bu pas mdzad pa/ ga ya dha ra dang / shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ slob dpon Dombhi pas mdzad pa'i de kho na nyid bcu pa mar me mdzad ye shes dang /
dge ba'i blo gros kyis bsgyur ba dang / des mdzad pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i don gyi gdams ngag brjod pa/ pra dznyA shrI dznyA nas bsdus pa/ des mdzad pa'i tshogs kyi 'khor
lo'i cho ga dznyA na a ka ra dang / mar pa chos kyi blo gros kyis bsgyur ba dang / des mdzad pa'i slongs mo'i 'grel pa dze ta karNaN dang / nyi ma rgyal mtshan dpal bzang
po'i 'gyur dang / kye'i rdo rje'i dran pa gcig pa/ slob dpon garbha ri pas mdzad pa pra dznyA indra ru tsi dang / shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ kye'i rdo rje'i sgrub thabs
mtsho skyes kyi mdzad pa'i mdor bshad pa dag pa rdo rje sgrol ma zhes bya ba dzwa landha ra pas mdzad pa/ manydzu shrI dang / nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyi 'gyur dang / slob
dpon mi thub zla bas mdzad pa'i yan lag drug pa'i sgrub thabs ratna shrI dznyA na dang / shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur/ kye'i rdo rje'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga bzang po yongs
su gzung ba zhes bya ba/ dpal thub dka' zla bas mdzad pa/ ratna shrI dznyA na dang / shAkya ye shes kyi 'gyur dang / 'byung po thams cad kyi gtor ma'i cho ga slob dpon mi

thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma seng rgyal ba dang / bla ma chos

skor/ ro bsreg pa'i cho ga slob dpon nag po pas mdzad pa/ de nyid dang / lhas btsas kyi 'gyur dang / kye'i rdo rje'i sgrub thabs de kho na nyid gsal bar byed pa zhes bya

ga ga ya dha ra dang / lhas btsas kyi 'gyur dang / des mdzad pa'i dpal dgyes pa rdo rje'i gzhung 'grel gyi dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga paNDi ta de nyid dang / mgos lhas btsas

rab seng ge 'bri mchams pa ye shes mkhar/ chos 'od/ zhu lan pa bsam gtan/ bla ma bka' bcu pa/ spru ston bsod rgyal/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ bla ma chos dpal ba/ chos

la'o// (ha)pa la/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i sgrub thabs mdor byas pa/ slob dpon klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ shrAddha ka ra warmma dang / rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur dang / yang gsang 'dus
sgrub thabs mdo dang bsres pa zhes bya ba mdzad byang dang / 'gyur snga ma bzhin no/ /dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga nyi shu pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa/ su bha shi ta dang /
rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur dang / des mdzad pa'i rdo rje bzlas pa'i rim pa dang po dang thams cad dag cing rnam par dag pa'i rim pa dang / slob dpon shAkya bshes gnyen gyis
mdzad pa ste rim pa gnyis pa dang / bdag byin gyis brlab pa'i rim pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa ste rim pa gsum pa/ des mdzad pa'i mchog tu gsang ba'i bde ba mngon par byang
chub pa'i rim pa ste rim pa bzhi pa/ des mdzad pa'i zung du 'jug pa'i rim pa ste rim pa lnga pa shrAddha kA ra warmma dang / rin chen bzang po'i bsgyur las/ ka ma la gupta
dang / rin chen bzang pos yul dbus kyi dpe dang yang gtugs te gtan la phab pa dang / slob dpon klu'i byang chub kyis mdzad pa'i bskyed rim rnam gzhag rim pa dang / spyod
pa bsdus pa'i sgrol ma/ slob dpon ArYa de bas mdzad pa/ shrAddha kA ra warmma dang / rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur dang / sems kyi sgrib pa rnam par sbyong ba zhes bya ba'i
rab tu byed pa/ arYa de bas mdzad pa dznyA na ka ra dang / tshul khrims rgyal bas bsgyur ba dang / de rnams thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje bzlas pa'i rgya cher bshad
pa bzhin no// (a)pa la/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga slob dpon mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa/ padma ka ra warmma dang / rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur dang
/ gsang ba 'dus pa'i cho ga bzhi brgya lnga bcu pa'i 'grel pa/ ratna A kA ra shAntis mdzad pa/ bidyA pra bha wa dang / rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur

thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ 'jam dpal dbyangs/ ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad bzang po/ 'jam dpal grags pa/ yan lag med pa'i rdo rje/ karNa pa/ dznyA na shrI mi tra/ ba liM A tsArYa/

kun bsod/ chos skyong dpal man 'dra'o// (ki) pa la/ slob dpon chen po mar me mdzad bzang pos mdzad pa'i gsang ba 'dus pa'i sgrub thabs kyi rnam par bshad pa dkyil 'khor chen
po'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon mkhas pa chen po dpal kun du bzang po'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ su ga ta kirtis bsgyur nas gtan la phab pa/ dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i mngon par
rtogs pa zhes bya ba'i sgrub thabs/ slob dpon chen po bsod snyoms pas mdzad/ shrAddha ka ra warmma dang / rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur dang / dpal mi skyod rdo rje'i sgrub
thabs slob dpon dpal rin chen rdo rjes mdzad pa/ padmA ka ra warmma dang / rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur dang / 'dus shing rtogs sla ba'i 'jam dpal rdo rje'i sgrub thabs/ pu
pu na ya/ Nya shrI mi tra paNDi tas mdzad pa/ klog kya gzhon nu 'bar gyis bsgyur ba dang / 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dbang phyug gi sgrub pa'i thabs dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i

dang / dpal 'jam dpa'i rdo rje zhes bya ba'i dkyil chog don yod pa'i zhabs kyis mdzad pa/ de nyid dang / rdo rje grags kyi 'gyur dang / 'jigs byed kyi tshogs kyi 'khor lo
ratna a kA ra shAntis mdzad pa/ dI paM kA ra rakShi ta dang / rwa rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur ba dang / tstshundha tstshundha ra'i rtog pa rwa rdor grags kyi 'gyur dang /
dpal rdo rje 'jigs byed kyi drag po'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga a mo gha badzras mdzad pa/ rwa rdo rje grags kyis bsgyur ba dang / las rgyud kyi grogs bstan pa dang / dam rdzas
bdud rtsi za ba'i rtog pa dang / gtam rgyud kyi rtog pa dang / de rnams thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gshin rje gshed nag po'i dkyil chog dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa dang 'dra'o/
/'jigs byed kyi phyag mtshan gyi rnam par dag pa zhes bya ba ta thA ga ta rakShi tas mdzad pa/ mal gyo blo gros grags pas bsgyur ba'i brgyud pa 'jigs byed kyi sgrub thabs
dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa bzhin no/ /gshin rje gshed dmar po lha lnga'i sgrub thabs slob dpon shrI bi ru pas mdzad pa/ dA na shI la'i rang 'gyur dang / gshin lhan skyes/

chen gyi 'gyur dang / gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sgrub thabs/ dpal dpa' bo'i rgyal pos mdzad pa/ 'gyur gong bzhin dang / gshin rje gshed kyi 'khrul 'khor gyi phreng ba zhes
bya ba rgyud chen 'bum phrag gsum pa las byung ba/ bi ru pas mdzad pa dA na shI las srin po rir bsgyur ba dang / gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sgrub thabs dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad
pa/ nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang / chag lo'i 'gyur dang / gshin rje gshed dmar po'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ nyi ma'i dbang po'i 'od zer dang

lo tsA bas bsgyur ba dang / gshin rje gshed dmar po'i sgrub thabs dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ nyi ma rgyal mtshan gyis thar pa gling du bsgyur ba dang / gshin rje gshed dmar
po'i ting nge 'dzin gyi cho ga dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ dA na shI las bsgyur ba dang / de'i sgrub thabs rnam par snang mdzad bsrung bas mdzad pa 'gyur gong bzhin dang

gyis mdzad pa/ de ba A kA ra dang / rin chen bzang po'i 'gyur las/ darpan A tsArYa dang / zhe sdang rdo rjes bcos pa dang / 'od 'chang ma'i sgrub thabs ting nge 'dzin gyi

po'i mchod rten gyi sngags btu ba/ lha mo bzhi'i las tshogs rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / bi ru pa/ DoM bhi wa/ dpal 'dzin/ a bhya ka ra/ blo bzang snying po/

bcu

pa/ rtsa ltung bcu bzhi pa slob dpon dpa' bos mdzad pa/ de'i bshags pa indra boddhis mdzad pa/ 'chi ba bsrung ba/ 'khor lo'i gsal byed dA na shI las mdzad pa/ 'khor lo'i don
rgyas par bshad pa/ tshogs kyi 'khor lo/ ngo sprod 'grel pa dpal 'dzin gyis mdzad pa/ mchod rten sgrub pa'i cho ga mdor bsdus/ bsrung ba'i 'khor lo'i sgrub thabs/ maNDal
gyi cho ga gnyis/ mchod chog nag po pas mdzad pa/ mdun bskyed maNDal gyi cho ga gnyis/ mchod chog nag po pas mdzad pa/ mdun bskyed maNDal gyi cho ga ka ma la ra tri tas
mdzad pa/ chos kyi sku'i snang ba'i cho ga ro bsreg rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ dA na shI la/ g.yag sde lo tsA/ bsod nams seng ge slob dpon byang chub tshul khrims/ phyar smyon/
mnga' ris pa sangs rgyas dpal/ slob dpon kun legs/ bla ma ArYa/ chos dpal ba/ grags don pa/ chos rje pa/ bdag go/ (phi )pa la/ mtshan yang dag par brjod pa'i 'grel pa
mtshan don gsal bar byed pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/ slob dpon bi ma la mi dras mdzad pa/ gnyags dznyA na ku ma ra'i 'gyur thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bla ma gser sdings pa/

gyi sgrub thabs zhi ba 'od kyi

rim pa zhes bya ba/ bla ma sdom pa bzang po'i thugs dam lo tsA ba dar ma birYas bsgyur ba dang / 'jam dpal khro bo'i sgrub thabs rdo rje 'od kyi rim pa zhes bya ba bla ma sdom
pa bzang po'i thugs dam dar ma birYas bsgyur ba dang / thun mong gi dngos grub sgrub pa'i thabs kyi man ngag las nang tshan rgyud kyi rgyal po 'jam dpal gyi dkyil 'khor
gyi cho ga sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa dang / skyabs 'gro sems bskyed dbang bzhi'i gdams pa/ sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa/ rdo rje glu'i gdams ngag phyi khrus/ nang khrus/
sdom pa bzang po'i thugs dam dar ma birYas bsgyur ba dang / gtor ma'i cho ga rdo rje'i rab gnas kyi cho ga ro bsreg pa'i cho ga sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa/ tsha tsha gdab
pa'i cho ga sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa dang / rab tu gnas pa'i cho ga sdom pa bzang pos mdzad pa dang / des mdzad pa'i sbyin sreg gi cho ga des mdzad pa'i thun mong gi
dngos grub sgrub pa rin po che'i gter sgrub/ bla ma yi dam gyi maNDal gyi cho ga 'bro lo tsAs bsgyur ba rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ shAkya'i rgyal po/ 'jam dpal/ spyan ras gzigs/

rje/ 'bras dkar ba man gong bzhin no/ /rnal 'byor pa rang gi sems ngal gso ba'i man ngag tshigs su bcad pa nyi shu rtsa lnga pa spyan ras gzigs la dngos su mi tras gsan nas/
shrI dza ga ta mi tras mdzad pa/ snubs lo tsA bas byams pa dpal gyis bsgyur ba gnyis thos pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / kha sarpa Ni/ byang sems blo gros rin chen/

ldan bla ma mchog gi rje/ /de lta bu'i rje btsun dam pa 'di nyid spyir mtha' yas pa'i yon tan brjod kyis mi lang ba dang ldan pa las/ lhag par yang bka' lung man ngag
gi rgya mtsho chen por gyur pa'i phyir/ bdag cag la chos kyi bskal ba bzang por mdzad pas na/ bka' drin dran zhing thob pa'i rnam grangs mi brjed par bya ba'i slad du yi
ge bkod par bgyi ba las/ dang por/ mchog gi dang po'i sangs rgyas dus kyi 'khor lo'i bsdus pa'i rgyud kyi rgyal po'i 'grel chen dri ma med pa'i 'od ces bya ba'i rgya cher
bshad pa nges pa'i don gyi

gsal byed ces bya ba/ chos rje dpal ldan bla ma dam pas mdzad pa'i lung gi brgyud pa ni/ thams cad mkhyen pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po'i zhabs/ rgya ma ba yon tan
'od/ shangs pa kun mkhyen pa/ mkhas grub gzhon nu dpal/ rtsa ba'i bla ma bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ des bdag thu btsun kun dga' rnam par rgyal ba la dgyes bzhin du gnang ba'o/
/yang na/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ lo chen byang rtse/ sang rin pa/ yid sangs rtse pa/ rje bla ma/ bdag go/ //yang / zur bka' shin tu dkon pa'i rnam grangs thob pa la/
dpal bde mchog gi rgyud mngon brjod bla ma'i le'u nyi shu rtsa gnyis pa las gsung pa 'khor lo sgyur drug gi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi rdzogs par thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ dpal 'khor lo bde mchog phyag na rdo rje/ sa rA ha/ nA gardzu nA/ sha ba rA pa/ lU hi pa/ dA ri ka pa/ gandha rA/ kurma pA da/ dza landha ra pa/ karNA tsarYa/
gu hya pa/ bi dza ya pA da/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ pham mthing pa/ klog kya shes rab rtsegs/ mal lo tsA ba/ rje sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos

rgyal/ klu seng pa mkhan po bsod nams dar/ dmar ston pa/ rje btsun bla ma/ des bdag la'o/ /de ni sa lugs te/ mar lugs ni/ rdo rje 'chang / DoM bhi ba/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/

las gsung pa/ 'khor lo bde mchog lha lnga

rigs gsum gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / badzra pA Ni/ dznyA na DA ki nI/ ratna badzra/ brahma pu

chos rin/ gan pa rin chen rgyal mtshan/ thog ston shes rab rdo rje/ gnyal pa bde legs pa/ gnas rnying mkhan po rin chen rgyal mtshan/ bla ma chos grags pa/ mkhan po bsod
nams rgyal mtshan/ dmar ston pa/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o// ! //rnam par snang mdzad sgyu 'phrul drwa ba lha bzhi bcu rtsa gsum gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bskur ba thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas/ phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po rab gsal zla ba/ ye shes rdo rje/ kun dga' snying po/ pra dznyA siddhiH mu ti ta ko ShaH shrAddha ka raH lo chen
rin chen bzang po/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ sum ston yes 'bar/ 'or ston lha'i dbang phyug sangs rgyas 'bar/ so thams cad mkhyen pa/ chos kyi seng ge skyi ston chos mgon/
dbus pa sangs rgyas 'bum/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan/ blo chen/ bde ba can pa/ dkon mchog seng ge seng ge rgyal mtshan/ bla ma chos rgyal/ 'phags 'od/ bla ma dpal ldan seng
ge lo chen byang rtse/ lo tsA ba grags rgyal/ bo dong chos rgyal/ mkhan po kun rgyal/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o// ! //kye rdor mtshon cha can nam/ drag po gdan can du grags
pa lha bcu bdun gyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ badzra dha raH nai rAtmAH bi ru paH Dombhi he ru kaH a la la
badzraH sha ba ra/ garbha ri pa/ dzA ya shrI dznyA naH durga tsantraH shU rAM gA badzraH

'brog mi shAkya ye shes/ bla ma dkon mchog rgyal po/ rje sa chen/ slob dpon rin po che/ rje btsun rin po che/ chos rje sa skya paN chen/ khang ston 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ bla
ma gzhon nu seng ge gnyal pa bde legs pa/ dpal ldan don grub/ sa bzangs gzhon nu blo gros/ rje kun dga' bzang po/ dmar ston pa/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o// ! //kyai rdor
mai tri lugs lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor du dbang bzhi yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ badzra dha raH badzra nai rAtmA/ bi rU pakShaH kriShNa pa/ kri yA'i Dha/ a
ba dhU tI pa/ shAnti ka raH shrI dharma pA la/ dznyA nA nadhi/ ma ti dhwa dzaH a mo gha shrIH si he shwa raH nA gI shwa raH rA hU~M la gupta/ tsantra de baH shrI ba na tanta
pA daH swA mi gu ruH des bdag la'o// ! //yang / bka' drin bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i rje bla ma de las/ phag mo zhal gnyis ma/ dbu bcad ma/ don grub ma gsum gyi rjes gnang
thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje phag mo/ mkha' 'gro ma dpal gyi blo gros/ bi rU pa/ a wa dhU tI pa/ gdong ngar rigs ngan dngos grub mnyes pa gdong ngar ba/ nya ba ra yin
yang / ba/ bsod snyoms pa chung ba/ bla ma ha ngu / rab byung ming ha ngu bla btags ha ngu dkar por grags/ gsang mtshan bha rendra ru rtse/ mtshan dngos bsod nams 'byung

des bdag la'o/ /yang dpyal kun rdor nas zar ston lo tsA ba/ snar ston zhig po/ grags pa tshul

dmar bskur ba'i lugs bzhin thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bzhi bcu rtsa brgyad kyi dbang / rdo rje 'chang / DA ki nI/ darpan A tsarYaH sa manta bha draH dznyA na dzyo tiH shrI ha

nas/ zhag re la dkyil 'khor re rer 'jug cing dbang bzhi rdzogs par gsan pa mdzad 'dug cing / phyis kyang 'jam rdor rdul tshon dang / gzhan rnams ras bris la rten nas/ dkyil
'khor thams cad du so sor bcug nas dbang gcig tu bskur te/ rgyas bsdus tshar gnyis gsan par gnang 'dug pa des na/ paN chen rin po che las rgyud pa'i phreng ba thob pa'i
brgyud pa ni/ badzra dha ra/ badzra yo gi nI/ a bhya ka ra gupta/ nA ya ka pA da/ da sha pha la shrI/ bi khya ta de ba/ shrI bha trA/ la li ta badzra/ dharmma gupta/ ratna
ka ra/ padma badzra/ ratna kirti/ buddha gho Sha/ ma hA sthA bi ra siddhi shwa ra shrI ba na ratna pA da/ bhaTTa ra ka puNya dzwa dza pA da/ des bdag la'o/ /gal te/ rgyud
sde phyi ma phyi ma'i khyad par yod pas thob par mi 'gyur ro snyam na/ a bhyas ma phye bzhin du/ phye nas/ byas pa rnams kyis kyang thob par sems na ci'i slad du mi mtshungs/
'jug pa phyogs gcig pas kyang 'grub ste/ dkyil 'khor bzhir bcug pas 'grub pa dang khyad par med do/ /'on te dngos cag gis dkyil 'khor so sor dbang ma thob pas mi
rung ngo snyam na'ang ma yin te/ hU~M mdzad gsum dang bdud rtsi gsum ma gtogs pa'i dkyil 'khor sum cu rtsa dgu snga nas thob cing / hU~M mdzad phyi ma gsum paN chen brgyud
pa rje 'di nyid la so sor zhus yod pas slan chad bdag gis phreng ba'i dbang so sor byas na/ nyan pa po/ 'di thams cad thob par 'gyur ro/ /sngar gyi rigs pa de'i phyir/
phreng ba'i 'byung khungs tha pa rnams kye rdor/ bde mchog rdo rje bdud rtsi/ hU~M mdzad la sogs pa rnams re res chog pa'i lugs su byas nas/ gong gi grangs yig nag po rnams/
dkyil 'khor nyi shu rtsa brgyad du dbang bskur zhing / gtso bo 'pho badbye na lnga bcu'am lnga bcu rtsa lngar yang dbyer 'dod pa de ltar nyer brgyad kyi dbang gi

pa/ sngags pa rtogs ldan rang rig lcang rwa ba gzung ston lha dar/ gzung ston rin chen rgyal po/ yol ston 'phags pa/ yol kun dga' rin chen/ ldan pa brtson 'grus rin
chen/ gtsang pa blo bzang pa/ yang rdzong pa dpal ldan bzang po/ me sna ba rnam rgyal 'od zer/ rje btsun bla ma dam pa/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i bka' babs so so ni/ mkha' 'gro
ma las kyi dbang mo che/ bi ma/ hU~M ka ra/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ slob dpon klu sgrub/ slob dpon pad ma/ dha na saM kri ta/ rom bu gu ya de ba/ shantiM garbha rnams
so/ /de rnams re re la mkha' 'gro ma nyid kyis gnang / de thams cad kyi bcud 'dus pa ni/ slob dpon pad ma yin la/ de rnams la rnying ma'i lugs kyi rgya gar gyi grub chen
brgyad ces bya'o/ /bod kyi grub chen brgyad ni/ zhang dri med zla shar/ gnyags dznyA na ku mA ra yang zer/ sangs rgyas ye shes/ nam mkha'i snying po/ ngal lam rgyal ba mchog
dbyangs/ mkhar chen mtsho rgyal/ dpal kyi ye shes/ dpal gyi seng ge bai ro tsA na/ khri srong lde'u btsan rnams yin la/ slob dpon gyi bka' brgyad kyang de thams cad la
so sor bka' babs so/ /de rnams kyi bcud 'dus pa

ni/ chos rgyal khri srong lde'u btsan yin no/ /de nas brgyud pa gong bzhin no// ! /bka' brgyad bka' ma yang 'di kas thob par bzhed pas/ bka' brgyad bka' ma'i brgyud pa ni/
chos sku kun bzang yab yum/ slob dpon dga' rab rdo rje/ gu ru shrI ri singha / slob dpon pad ma 'byung gnas/ gnyags dznyA na ku mA ra/ snubs sangs rgyas rin po che/ snubs
ston yon tan rgya mtsho/ snubs pad ma dbang rgyal/ rag shi tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ khams pa ldan ston/ khams pa dar rgyal/ shangs kyi dpa' grub thob/ las stod kyi dpa'
grub thob dngos grub/ myang ral nyi ma 'od zer nas gter ma ji bzhin no/ /bka' brgyad yongs rdzogs zhes bya ba/ gter kha 'og ma gu ru chos dbang nas brgyud pa'i dbang bskur
che mo thob sngar las thos so/ pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun bzang yab yum/ longs sku rgyal ba rigs lnga/ sprul sku dga' rab rdo rje/ gu ru shrI ri singha / slob dpon
pad ma 'byung gnas/ gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug sras pad ma dbang chen/ sras kun grol/ bla ma chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ bla ma rang byung rin chen/ ldan pa brtson 'grus rin
chen/ des man gong ma bzhin no// //bka' brgyad yongs rdzogs kyi brgyud gsang ba 'dus pa le'u bzhi bcu zhe gnyis pa/ slob dpon pad mas rang 'gyur du mdzad pa'i lung gi brgyud
pa ni/ kun tu bzang po/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ phyag na rdo rje/ mkha' 'gro ma las kyi dbang mo che/ slob dpon pad ma/ gu ru chos dbang / sman lung pa mi bskyod rdo rje/
'bro rdo rje mgon po/ de'i sras kun dga' bzang po/ de'i sras u rgyan badzra/ de'i sras yon tan lhun grub/ bla ma sher mgon pa/ me sna ba rnam rgyal 'od zer/ chos rje bsod
nams rgyal mtshan nyid/ des bdag la'o/ /bka' brgyad skor gyi yig cha thams cad kyang chos 'di pa

rang gi lugs bzhin yod/ lung du ma tshang ba med par legs par thob bo// //tsa ri'i zhing skyong seng gdong bka' gter gyi rjes gnang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ btsal bar bya'o//
yang sgyu 'phrul zhi ba lha bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis dang / khro bo khrag mthung lnga cu rtsa brgyad kyi dkyil 'khor so sor phyi rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du/ phan pa'i dbang
bcu/ nang lus kyi dkyil 'khor du nus pa'i dbang lnga/ gsang ba bha ga'i dkyil 'khor du gsang ba'i dbang / rang bzhin 'od gsal gyi dkyil 'khor du shes rab ye shes kyi dbang
/ bden pa dbyer med kyi dkyil 'khor du shin tu brtan pa'i dbang rnams thob pa'i brgyud pa la/ dang po rgyal ba dgongs brgyud ni/ rgyal ba kun tu bzang po/ rgyal tshab
rigs lnga/ rgyal sras sems dpa'/ 'joms byed khro bo'i dkyil 'khor dang bcas pa la dgongs te brgyud/ gnyis pa rig 'dzin rig pa'i brgyud pa ni/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/
dam pa'i rigs can dra ma lnga la rig pa nas rig par brgyud/ gsum pa gang zag snyan brgyud ni/ gsang bdag ku ku rA dza/ rgyal po dza/ siddhi ra dza/ sring mo go pA li/
yang ku ku rA dza/ ro langs bde ba'i dngos grub/ rdo rje bzhad pa/ za hor gyi rgyal po pra hasti/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba/ bi ma la mi tra/ sma rin chen mchog mkhas
pa gtsug gye rnam gnyis/ zhang rgyal ba'i yon tan/ snubs pa sangs rgyas ye shes/ khu lung yon tan rgya mtsho yab sras/ myang sher mchog myang ye shes 'byung gnas/ zur po
che shAkya 'byung / zur chu shes rab grags/ glan shAkya byang chub/ gsang bdag shAkya seng ge rtsad tsha shwa ka rdor/ tsags ston shAkya 'byung / glan ston rdo rje 'od
po/ glan bsod nams rgyal mtshan/ dpal ldan chos kyi seng ge glan sangs rgyas dpal/ glan bsod nams mgon

po/ 'bro ban bsam grub rdo rje/ 'bro ston sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhas grub gzhon nu dpal/ rje btsun bla ma rin po che/ des bdag la'o// //kun tu bzang po rig pa stsal gyi dbang
yang zer/ na raka dong sprugs lha dam pa rigs brgya yang zer ba'i rdul tshon gyi dkyil 'khor du dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ drug pa kun tu bzang po/ ston pa rdo rje
sems dpa'/ dpal rnam par snang mdzad/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/ skal ldan rgyal po dza/ slob dpon hU~M ka ra/ slob dpon sangs rgyas gsang ba/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra/
gnyags lo tsA ba dznyA na ku mA ra/ sog po dpal gyi seng ge snubs sangs rgyas rin chen/ snubs legs pa'i sgron ma/ sras gzhon nu snying po/ zhu bsod nams shAkya/ zur po
che shAkya 'byung gnas/ zur chung shes rab grags pa/ glan shAkya byang chub/ mgar ston/ bsregs ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ glan rdo rje 'od po/ glan ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
dpal ldan chos kyi seng ge glan ston sangs rgyas dpal/ glan bsod nams mgon po/ 'jam dbyangs bsam grub rdo rje/ chos rje sgron ma ba/ 'gos lo tsA gzhon nu dpal/ rje
btsun bla ma/ des bdag la'o// ! //'jam dpal tshe bdag nag po'i dkyil 'khor chen por dbang yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / phyag na rdo rje/
sprul sku dga' rab rdo rje/ rigs 'dzin 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ mkhas pa gtsug lag dpal dge slob dpon shantiM garbha/ rgya gar dha na dha la/ mthu stobs khrag mthung nag po/
bal po ba su dha ra/ snubs ban sangs rgyas ye shes/ khu lung yon tan rgya mtsho/ sras mchog ye shes rgya mtsho/ bla ma rdo ston lcags ye/ mkhas pa me ston dran chung /
de sras bran ston mtha' bral/ gu ru me ston kun

rig skyes mchog mkhas pa chen po/ lho ston rin chen grags pa/ sngo tsha bsod nams dbang phyug kun mkhyen sangs rgyas rin chen/ mkhan chen shes rab rdo rje/ mkhas btsun dkon
mchog bzang po/ 'jam dbyangs bsam grub rdo rje/ sgrol ma ba sangs rgyas rin chen dpal bzang po/ mkhas pa chen po gzhon nu dpal/ nam mkha' blo gros/ rje btsun bla ma/ des
bdag la'o// ! /phur pa rtsa thung gi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ 'khor lo rgyas 'debs ma/ u rgyan pad ma/ ye shes mtsho rgyal/ 'dre a tsar sa le/ lang lab byang chub rdo rje/
sna nam tshul khrims shes rab/ khyung po 'phyal chen/ 'phyal chung / khyung po blo gros rgyal mtshan/ go rub yang dag 'gos ston dbyangs 'bar/ khyung po seng ge khyung po
khro bo/ gnyal pa ston grags/ chos kyi seng ge rgyal ye shes mgon po/ dpal ldan rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ bla ma tshul rgyal/ ri gdong pa shes rab rgyal mtshan/ slob dpon bsod
nams bzang po/ slob dpon bkra shis rgya mtsho/ mkhas grub gzhon nu dpal/ rje btsun bla ma/ des bdag la'o/ /'di gter ma yin zhing / gu ru chos dbang gi mchan yang zhib mo
snang ngo // ! //yang / phur ba lha nag gi dbang dbang gong ma dang bcas pa dpal ldan rdo rje rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i yig cha'i steng nas thob pa'i brgyud pa'ang rtsa
thung 'di kho na'o/ /phur pa yang gsang spu gri'i dbang yongs su rdzogs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku thugs rje chen po/ sprul sku
pad ma 'byung gnas/ gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug yar lungs sprul sku/ sangs rgyas 'gar ston/ tshul bzhon pa/ mkhas grub chos dpal ba/ bla ma sangs rgyas rin chen/ chos spyan
ldan pa gzhon nu dpal/ rje btsun bla ma rin po che/ des

bdag la'o// ! /phur pa man ngag drug pa'i dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / rdo rje sems dpal/ rigs bzhi'i sangs rgyas dang / bsdud pa po phyag rdor/ lha dbang
brgya byin/ nye dbang / sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi gtso bo/ lha dbang dbang phyug 'bar/ mkhan po pra hasti/ slob dpon pad ma/ de la 'bangs mi bzhi mchis pa las/ rtsa ba'i brgyud
lugs la/ jo mo mkhar chen mtsho rgyal/ mkhar chen dpal gyi dbang phyug la byi ye shes rtsegs pa/ me bu rgyal ba'i snying po/ lo dpal gyi blo gros/ lce yon tan bzang po/
lce mo dpal sgron/ ngam 'bro gsal le byang chub/ lang lab byang chub rdo rje/ sna nam 'bro ban byang chub/ mgon ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ me ston byang 'bar/ me ston
lcam me/ me ston dkon mchog me ston kun dga'/ spug ston grags g.yung / sangs rgyas 'gar ston/ rgya ston zhig po/ gu ru shI la ku mA raH mkhas grub chos dpal bzang po/ bla
ma sangs rgyas rin chen/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o// ! /rta mgrin lha bzhi'i dbang lho 'grims su grags pa thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ kun tu bzang po/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ snang
ba mtha' yas/ spyan ras gzigs/ nA gardzu naH ArYa de baH singha dharma rA dzaH shing gi lha mo gdong bzhi/ pad ma 'byung gnas/ ba su dha ra/ bal rje shAkya pu ri/ rgyud
dpal phre 'od zer/ slob dpon phyag na rdo rje/ grub thob glang bu go cha/ grub thob khri bzher shing / rgyal mtshan mchog dbyangs/ myang de bzhin gshegs pa/ 'bre za bzang
mo/ snang ba dpal gyi lha/ 'o ma ti phyag na/ rgyan pa rin chen/ dpa' bo rab mchog gnyags rgyal ba rin chen/ 'tshams mchog ye shes/ zungs shAka shog kam sgom ye shes rgyal
mtshan/ ye

zho 'od zer rgyal mtshan/ jo sras 'jigs byed/ jo sras byang chub rdo rje/ myang byang chub sems dpa'/ bla ma brag dkar ba/ gu ru shrI la ku mA raH chos dpal bzang po/ sangs
rgyas rin chen/ rje bla ma/ des bdag go/ ! /rta mgrin shwa na bzhi skor jo bo lugs su grags pa'i rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ spyan ras gzigs/ rta mgrin/ yum gsang ba ye
shes/ sangs rgyas zhi ba/ sangs rgyas gsang ba/ ku sa li che chung / di pangka ra shrI dznyA na/ yol grub thob/ mtha' bzhi grub thob/ rin chen smon lam/ rin po che lam pa/
lha bla ma ye shes 'od/ slob dpon legs pa shes rab/ bla ma byang chub rin chen/ slob dpon byang chub gzhon nu/ mkhan chen byams pa rin chen/ mkhas btsun byang seng ba/
sa bzangs 'phags pa gzhon nu blo gros/ kun dga' bzang po dmar ston pa/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o/ /yang na/ dang po'i sangs rgyas/ dge slong ma dpal mo/ dge slong dpal gyi
bzang po/ ye shes bzang po/ jo bo nas sngar bzhin no// ! /shangs pa nas brgyud pa'i rta mgrin bsang sgrub kyi brgyud pa ni/ pad ma 'byung gnas/ skyer rgang pa dar ma seng
ge gnyan ston chos kyi shes rab/ sangs rgyas brtson 'grus seng ge mkhas grub shangs ston/ gser gling pa bkra shis dpal/ bla ma rdo rje dpal/ chos sgo ba chos dpal shes
rab/ chos rje grags 'byung ba/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o// ! /ma ning drags pa'i srog dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku snang ba mtha' yas/ longs sku thugs rje chen
po/ sprul sku pad ma 'byung gnas/ mkha' 'gro ye shes mtsho rgyal/ gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug yar lung sprul sku mgon po rdo rje/ sprul sku shAka 'bum/ sprul sku shAka seng
/ rin po che byang chub rdo

rje/ chos rje brtan pa ba/ zur dben pa chos bzangs bla ma/ rje bla ma'i zhabs/ des bdag la gnang ba'o// ! //sems sde ma bu bco brgyad kyi dgongs pa ngo sprad pa'i thabs/ rig
pa rtsal gyi dbang bco la dkyil 'khor gcigbrgyad thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang po/ longs sku rigs lnga'i sangs rgyas/ sprul sku gsang bdag phyag rdor/ yang
sprul dga' rab rdo rje/ mkhas pa nyi shu rtsa gcig sgra bsgyur bai ro tsA na/ rgyal mo g.yu sgra snying po/ mkhas pa ye shes gzhon nu/ sog po dpal gyi ye shes/ snubs
chen sangs rgyas ye shes zhabs/ snubs chung yon tan yab sras/ mkhas pa nyang chen sher mchog nyang ban ye shes 'byung gnas/ zur chen shAkya 'byung gnas/ zur chung shes rab
grags pa/ skyo ston shAkya ye shes/ gsang bdag mnga' tsha hor po/ 'gro mgon dam pa shAka rgyal/ mkhas pa lce ston yab sras/ bla ma thar ston 'bum me/ chos rje bla skyabs
rdo rje/ drin can mkhas pa chen po/ mkha' 'gro dpal gyi ye shes/ ma cig drin can zur mo/ zur mo dge 'dun 'bum/ zur shAkya bshes gnyen/ bra bo chos 'bum/ dkon mchog bzang
po/ ka thog pa rdo rje rin chen dpal bzang po/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o/ /lung a nu yo ga las kun 'dus rig pa'i mdo dang / de'i bshad rgyud sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dgongs
pa 'dus pa'i mdo las 'byung ba'i tshogs chen 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor chen po yan lag dang dngos gzhi dkyil 'khor sgo gcig sbag gzhan dkyil 'khor brgyad zhi khro la shar
du dbyer rung ba A yu dmar po tshe dbang de dngos su dkyil 'khor gcig bcas par dbang bskur ba'i brgyud pa'i rim pa ni sku lnga'i bdag nyid kun tu bzang po/ gsang ba'i
bdag po phyag na rdo rje/ rgyal po dza/ sras intra bhu ti/ khyi'i rgyal po ku ku rA dzA/ ro langs bde

ba/ rgyal po pra hasti/ shAkya seng ge dha na rakShi ta/ sthI ra la ti/ bde ba gsal mdzad/ dharma boddhi dang lo tsA ba che btsan skyes kyis snubs sangs rgyas ye shes rin po
che/ snubs yon tan rgya mtsho/ sras ye shes rgya mtsho/ rgya blo gros byang chub/ tho gar nam mkha'/ des zur po che/ zur chung shes rab grags/ yang khyeng bla ma/ sgro
phug pa/ de las brgyud pa'ang yod/ zur chung pa la glan shAkya bzang po/ shangs pa lha rje 'gar/ sreg ston rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ glan rdo rje 'od/ glan brtson 'grus seng
ge glan bsod nams rgyal po/ lha rje lha 'bum/ glan ston chos kyi seng ge glan sangs rgyas dpal/ glan bsod nams mgon po/ 'bro bsam grub rdo rje/ zur shAkya 'byung gnas/ zur
mo dge 'dun 'bum/ zur shAkya bshes gnyen/ bra bo chos 'bum pa/ rngo rked dkon mchog bzang po/ ka thog pa chen po rdo rje rin chen dpal bzang po/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o//
! //rdzogs pa chen po sa gcig pa/ man ngag gi rgyal po rdzogs pa chen po'i bsam gtan byang chub kyi sems sgom/ 'di la sems sgom thig le drug pa yang zer/ rtsal chen
sprug pa/ khyung chen lding ba/ rdo rje sems pa/ lta ba nam mkha' che/ 'di rnams shi ri singha dang / bai ro tsA nas bsgyur/ de kho na nyid rdo la gser bzhin byang chub sems
sgom slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ rdzogs pa chen po byang chub kyi sems lta ba nam mkha'i rgyal po/ slob dpon rA dzA hastis mdzad pa/ byang chub kyi
sems de kho na nyid bde ba 'phra bkod sras mos mdzad pa/ rje btsun dam pa/ kha che rgyal po rab snang bsten pas mdzad pa/ spros pa med pa byang chub kyi tig slob dpon rnal
'byor ma a ra lis mdzad pa/ byang chub kyi sems rin po che kun 'dus slob dpon klu sgrub

kyi mdzad pa/ srog gi 'khor lo dga' rab rdo rjes mdzad pa/ rdzogs pa spyi gcod rmi khrod kyi rgyal po ku ku rA dzas mdzad pa/ lung rtse mo byung rgyal phreng ba dam pa slob
dpon ma hA rA dzas mdzad pa/ byang chub sems yid bzhin nor bu rin chen slob dpon mar me mdzad kyi mdzad pa/ byang chub sems bde klong yangs pa'i dkyil 'khor bde 'byam rgyal
po de ba rA dzas mdzad pa/ byang chub sems sgom don drug pa slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa/ spyi bcings sngags kyi lung slob dpon bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa ste bcu
gsum po 'di mkhan po bi ma la mi tra dang / lo tsA ba g.yu sgra snying pos bsgyur gong ma lnga la snga 'gyur lnga ste ma dang 'dra/ phyi ma bcu gsum bu dang 'dra bas sems
bde ma bu bco brgyad du grags pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ kun tu bzang po/ rdo rje sems dpa'/ dga' rab rdo rje/ 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ shrI ri singha / bai ro tsA
na/ ye shes snying po/ ye shes rgyal mtshan/ ye shes tshul khrims/ lha rje chen po/ zhig po bdud rtsi/ snyi ba nyi ma grags/ zur mo 'od 'bum/ yon tan dpal 'bum/ bla ma
shAkya 'bum/ kun dga' rdo rje/ bsam grub rdo rje/ shAkya 'byung gnas/ zur mo dge 'bum/ shAkya bshes gnyen/ zla ba rgyal mtshan/ tshul khrims rgyal mtshan/ ka thog pa rdo
rje bzang po/ rje bla ma/ des bdag la'o// ! /sems bde ma bu bco brgyad kyi dbang brgyud dang / 'di'i lung brgyud gcig pa 'dra snyam du yang rtog ste/ bla ma'i gsan yig la
'di snang gsung ngo / /'di'i rtsa rgyud kun lus rig pa'i lung brgyud gong bzhin thos la/ bshad rgyud dgongs 'dus gzhan du thos cing brgyud yig kyang gzhan na yod la/ mdo
dbang gi cho ga bla ma ka thog pas mdzad la de'i lung yang tshang ma ste mdor na cha lag thams cad rdzogs

par thob pa'o/ /dam tshig gsal bkra'i lung yang thob ste/ bla ma ka thog pa la gsan par snang ngo // ! //dang lung khra mo brag gi gter kha las/ gter ston sprul sku tshul rdor/
gsang mtshan pad ma las 'brel stsal/ dpa' bo sgang du byon pas dpa' bo sgang par yang grags pa des gdan drangs pa'i yid dam dregs pa kun 'dul gyi chos skor thob pa la/
phyag na rdo rje dregs pa kun 'dul gyi dbang chog bzhin dbang rdzogs pa dang / so so'i las bsgrub pa'i dbang bskur ro zhes pa'i skabs su/ phyi sgrub/ nang sgrub/ sku/
gsung / thugs/ yon tan/ phrin las so so'i sgrub thabs kyi skabs nas bshad pa'i lha sgom pa dang / sngags kyi bzlas lung / de nas dkyil 'khor gyi dbus gru gsum 'bar ba'i gtso
bo'i mdun du gza' mchog chen po/ dzambha la dmar po/ ba ru Na rnams rim pas bskyed/ dpal gsang ba'i bdag po'i bka' las ma 'da' bar/ rdo rje slob ma'i mthun rkyen bsgrub
pa 'gal rkyen sel/ ji ltar bsgom pa'i phrin las sgrubs shig ces gtor ma lag tu gtad pa'i bka' gtad mdzad pa phyag len la gnang ba dang bcas pa thob pa dang / rgyud klu
'dul nag po/ phyi sgrub rtsa ba'i sgrub thabs/ de'i las tshogs khyad par ba gsum la/ ser ba dbab pa/ byad kha zlog pa/ mdze nad bsrung ba/ thun mong gis las mtha' la/ las
bzhi'i sbyin bsreg sa bdag klu gnyan 'dul ba/ klu gnyan gsad pa/ drag po'i thun bdun/ las kyi zer bdun/ zlog pa/ gnod byed dgug pa/ thog ser dbab pa/ thog ser zlog pa/
klu'i gtad khram/ rdo rje'i las mtha'o/ /nang bsgrub rtsa ba/ de'i las mtha' la/ bum pa'i las mtha'/ nad pa bso ba/ gtor sgrub/ spu gri'i reg gcod/ gza' rgod wa thod lags/
dom lag ma/ nye 'byed si shing

ma/ dzambha la dmar po/ 'phran men 'khor lo gsum ma/ khang sel ra dam ma/ ngag mnan rang 'og ma/ rang bshed sde brgyad gnad 'khor/ gsang ba'i sgrub thabs rtsa ba/ las bzhi'i
sbyin bsreg sku sgrub rtsa ba/ de'i las byang / ser phur gyi las nyer gcig klu gter gzhug pa/ klu rten spo ba/ byad 'grel/ klu gta' bsdam pa/ char chog klu'i gdon 'grol/
gsung sgrub rtsa ba/ klu gsad pa/ yungs kar las mtha'/ seng phur las mtha'/ ral gri'i las mtha'/ rdzas ngan las mtha'/ 'khor lo'i las mtha'/ ngan thabs las mtha' 'o/ /thugs
sgrub rtsa ba/ gsang ba thugs kyi phur gcig ma/ gdab las/ las byang / tshogs las/ phyag rdor dril sgrub/ lcog brdungs dug gi spu gri/ yon tan gyi sgrub pa/ phrin las

lugs gcig la/ mtshur ston/ gnyags sgom/ bla ma ro bhi ba/ rog thams cad mkhyen pa/ bla ma dpal ldan chen po/ rin po che kun dga' don grub/ bla ma bde legs dpal/ rin
po che bsod bzang pa man gong dang 'dra'o// ! /dpal dud sol lha mo'i rjes su gnang ba thob nas/ de'i chos skor la/ dngos grub 'byung ba'i rgyud kyi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje
'chang / mkha' 'gro ma su ma ti/ skal pa bzang mo/ tai lo pa/ nA ro pa/ mar pa/ chos rdor/ mdo sde/ kun dga'/ gzi brjid/ rin chen bzang po/ rin chen dpal/ dpal gyi rdo rje/
slob dpon bzang po dpal/ chos rje byang chub dpal/ bla ma bsod nams don grub/ des bdag la'o// ! /yang / slob dpon sangs rgyas seng ge dpal gyi rdo rje man gong dang 'dra/!
/lha mo'i las byang rgya mtsho gsal ba'i sgron me zhes bya ba/ slob dpon kun rgyal dang / dpal gyi rdo rje gnyis kyis bsgrigs pa'i

brgyud pa ni/ dpal gyi rdo rje nas/ slob dpon bzang po dpal/ byang chub dpal/ bsod nams don grub/ des bdag la'o/ /lha mo'i sgrub thabs nA ro pa nas mdzad pa/ lha mo'i zhal
gdams/ ltas ngan dbab pa la sogs pa'i yig chung phran tshegs/ las tshogs zhe sdang rdo rjes mdzad pa/ rang rang rtsom pa po nas/ bla ma don grub pa'i bar/ de la bdag gis
so//! /de ltar thob cing sgrub thabs dkyil chog rnams 'grel pa rnams su ma tshang ba med pa'i phyir/ zhar las thob pas zur du mi dgos pa bzhed pa yin gyi/ rin po che'i gsan
yig na'ang zur du ma bris pas nges pa rnyed cing / mdor na/ rngog skor ma tshang ba med par thob bo//gzhan yang / bla ma de las/ chos drug 'ba' rwa ba nas brgyud pa/ bla
ma rgyal mtshan bzang po nyid kyi yig cha yongs su rdzogs pa'i steng nas thob cing / bla mas thugs sras nam mkha' ba la gsan/ des 'ba' rwa ba nyid la thob par 'dug yang
/ de nyid las/ 'jam dpal nag po'i man ngag thob cing bla mas/ mkhan chen seng ge dpal ba la gsan par snang ngo // ! /yang / nag po chen po zhal bzhi pa khyung zhal can
gyi sgrub skor dang / zhal bzhi pa'i rjes gnang / gi yi ge rje btsun chen pos mdzad pa'i lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje 'chang / klu sgrub/ ba li ta pa/ sangs rgyas
ye shes zhabs/ mar me mdzad/ dpal sde ba/ bi ma la gupta/ rin chen rdo rje/ ratna kIrti/ ri sul rnal 'byor ma/ gnyan lo/ kha'u pa/ de gnyis ka la sa chen/ rje btsun/ chos
rje sa paN/ bla chen 'phags pa/ zhang / nam brag pa/ bla ma dam pa/ gzungs kyi dpal ba/ dge legs bzang po/ a nanta ma ti/ rgya bka' bzhi pa grags pa dpal/ rngog ston bsod
nams don grub/ des bdag la'o// ! /

yang / sum pa lo tsA ba'i blo sbyong thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rje btsun ma rdo rje phag mo dang / sgrol ma gnyis las/ sum pa lo tsA ba/ chos rje sa paN/ bla chen 'phags pa/
zhang dkon mchog dpal/ na bza' brag phug pa/ chos rje bla ma dam pa/ rgyal sras thog med pa/ sa bzangs paN chen pa/ mchog ldan pa/ mkhan chen yon blo ba/ rngog ston bsod
nams don grub/ des bdag thu btsun kun dga' rnam rgyal dpal bzang po la'o//! //spro lung pa'i tshe chog gi lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mkhan chen seng ge bas gsan yig las
shes par nus so/ /shu bhaM//// ! /rngog ston byang chub dpal ba'i drung du/ tshe dpag med lha dgu'i dbang thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ bcom ldan 'das tshe dpag med/ snying po
zhabs/ dze tA ri/ boddhi bha draH ting nge 'dzin bzang po/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri lo tsA ba/ mchims brtson seng / mchims thams cad mkhyen pa/ dbang phyug mgon po/ dbus pa
sangs rgyas 'bum/ bla ma rgyal ba don grub/ rin po che bkra shis dpal/ bla ma dkon mchog rdo rje/ rin po che don grub dpal/ chos rje byang chub dpal bzang po/ des bdag
la'o// //@/ /chos grwa gling smad rin po che la chos thob yigrnam dag tshul khrims brtan pa'i 'dzin ma'i lor/ /mang thos ljon pa du ma'i nags tshal stug /gzhan phan chu phran?chu
bran stong gi 'byung gnas che/ /mkhas grub ri bo mchog gi zhabs la 'dud/ /gang yang sde snod 'dzin pa chen por gyur pas/ dpal gsang phu'i gdan sa

mkhas mang seng ges bteg pa'i chos rin po che'i khrir zhabs pad bkod cing / zab don du ma thugs su chud pas man ngag la dbang 'byor zhing / bdag cag la yang dbu tshad sogs
mtshan nyid theg pa'i chos du ma'i sgo nas bka' drin chen po gyur pa/ chos kyi rje/ grwa ston rig pa'i ral gri/ mkhas grub shes rab dpal ldan pa'i zhal sngar/ bsnyen sgrub
rdo rje gsum gyi lam cha lag dang bcas pa yongs su rdzogs par thob nas/ de dag gi chos kyi rnam grangs bla ma brgyud pa'i rim pa dang bcas pa mi brjed cing bka' drin dran
la/ slar gzhan la'ang phan pa'i bsam pas bri bar bya ba ni/lam 'di'i mnga' bdag grub chen u rgyan pa'i rnam thar rin chen phreng ba zhes bya ba/ dang por thob pa'i brgyud
pa ni/ grub thob zla ba seng ge ra ga brag pa shAkya dhwa dza/ 'brom mdo ba bkra shis dpal ldan/ bla ma nor bu bzang po/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o//! /bla ma de las
brgyud pa'i lam smin grol gnyis las dang po dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang gong ma bskur ba'i cho ga zla ba seng gis mdzad pa'i steng nas dbang dang lung thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/
rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen u rgyan pa/ zla ba seng ge ra ga brag pa shAkya dhwa dza/ bla ma bkra shis dpal ldan pa/ bla ma nor bu ba/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o//!
/de nas grol lam nyams khrid du legs par thob pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ grub chen u rgyan pa/ mkhas btsun bsod nams 'od zer/ zla ba seng ge de gnyis ka
la kun mkhyen gangs khrod pa/ sa bzangs ma ti paN chen/ theg chen chos kyi rgyal po kun dga' bkra shis rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ bla ma nor bu ba/ chos rje pa/ des bdag
la'o//! /de dag gi yig cha'i rim pa ni/ bsnyen sgrub rtsa ba rdo rje'i tshig rkang / grub thob u rgyan pa rang gis

mdzad pa'i lung brgyud ni/ u rgyan pa/ mkhas btsun bsod nams 'od zer/ 'bar rwa ba rgyal mtshan dpal bzang po/ 'bri sgom pa bsod nams bkra shis/ bla ma nor bu ba/ chos rje pa/
des bdag la'o/ /bsnyen sgrub yan lag dang po gnyis kyi khrid yig gcig snang rdo rje zla ba seng ges mdzad pa/ bsnyen sgrub yid bzhin nor bu/ bsnyen sgrub kyi sa bcad yid
bzhin nor bu/ bsnyen sgrub kyi sor sdud kyi ngo sprod/ bsnyen sgrub gsum gyi ngo sprod rnams zla ba seng gis mdzad pa'i lung brgyud ni/ zla ba seng ge ra ga brag pa shAkya
dhwa dza/ 'brom mdo ba bkra shis dpal ldan/ nor bu ba/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o//! /yang / zla ba seng ges mdzad pa'i gegs sel rgyas pa gces phrug brgya rtsa'am/ nyams
myong bdud rtsi'i phreng ba zla seng gis mdzad pa/ 'khrul 'khor ha 'don gyi khrid gab pa mngon phyung zla seng gis mdzad pa/ 'bebs kyi man ngag jo mo nang gi sgom chen
la gnang ba/ zla ba seng ge la grags byang gi zhus lan/ rgyal ba u rgyan pa'i zhal gdams zla seng gi yi ger bkod pa/ thugs rdo rje'i skabs kyi yar bud pa'i gegs sel snyan
rgyud ma chung ba zla seng gis yi ger bris pa/ yang bar rlung gi man ngag zla ba seng ge'i drung du grags byang gis zhus pa'i lan che chung gnyis/ u rgyan pa'i drung
du rtog ldan rin bsam gyis zhus lan zla seng gis zin bris/ yang rlung ltas kyis man ngag ces pa u rgyan pa'i drung du zla seng dang / chag ston ring mo'i zhus lan dang /
na ra ba bsod nams mgon po dang / dbu ri dbon po'i zhus lan zla seng gis zin bris su btab pa/ zla ba seng ge'i drung du ston pa dpal rgyal gyi zhus lan rnams kyi lung brgyud
ni gong dang 'dra/ zla ba seng ge'i grwa pa rtogs ldan 'jam dpal rgyal mtshan gyis mdzad pa'i bsnyen sgrub kyi chos skor tshe

sgrub lus sbyong / gegs sel dbyug gcos dang bcas pa'i lung brgyud ni/ rtogs ldan 'jam dpal rgyal mtshan/ ra ga brag pa shAkya dhwa dza/ bkra shis dpal ldan man 'dra/ gegs sel
bsdus par grags pa'i nang nas/ gegs sel che mo'i lde mig zhal gdams/ gces phrug brgya rtsa'am nyams myong gi yi ge bdud rtsi phreng ba'i zhal shes dgos 'dod 'byung ba
ngag dbang grags pas mdzad pa'i lung brgyud ni/ rong pa ngag dbang grags pa/ 'bri sgom pa/ nor bu ba/ chos rje ba/ des bdag la'o/ /rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub kyi zhal
gdams/ sgra gcan 'ching ba dang bcas pa zla seng gi grwa pa/ stan gcig pas shrI bsam gtan gling du mdzad pa'i lung brgyud ni/ stan gcig pa/ 'bri sgom pa man 'dra// ! /rdo

ga brag pa/ bkras dpal man 'dra/! /u rgyan pa'i phyag bzhes dngul chu'i ril bu sbyar thabs rdo rje mgon po la gnang ba dang / dug sman 'chi med bdud rtsi rnams kyi brgyud
pa ni/ mkha' 'gro ma nyi ma'i 'od zer/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng / rdo rje

mgon po/ 'bri sgom pa man 'dra/ yang / dngul chu'i sbyor thabs nad 'joms bdud rtsi rnam rgyal gyi brgyud pa ni/ sha ba ri pa/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng / rdo rje mgon po/ 'bri sgom
pa man 'dra/ ! /dngul chu ril bu'i sbyar thabs dngul chu'i dug dbyung ba dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paNDi ta nA landra pa gcig lo tsA ba mchog
ldan legs pa'i blo gros/ bsod dbang ba/ shAkya seng ge ratna singha / ra ga brag pa/ bkras dpal ba man 'dra/ ! /yang dngul chu sbyar thabs sngags dang bcas pa/ dug brtag
thabs/ 'dred kyi sman sogs/ dug bsrungs thabs/ btsan dug sngags kyis bsrung thabs rnams kyi brgyud pa ni/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng / ra ga brag pa/ bkras dpal ba man 'dra/
! /dug nad sngags kyis gso bar byed pa gser gzugs su grags pa'i brgyud pa ni/ sangs rgyas sman bla/ rgyal po si na/ u rgyan gyi rnal 'byor 'chi med rdo rje/ kha che'i paNDi
ta rgya mtsho 'od/ pu rangs kyi tsad po kong tshal/ tsad po rtsa/ des gcung po'i dge 'dun dpe'i dbon po a khu bstan chung la gnang / des rgya chu mig pa la/ des sman
pa tshul dar la/ des sman pa chos sde/ des sbar ston don zhags/ des tshas mtha'i dge bshes brtson rgyal la/ des dkon ston rta khra la/ des gnyer ston dbang rgyal la/ des
ra ga brag pa la/ des bkras dpal ba man 'dra/ ! /yang / gser gzugs gter ma'i brgyud pa ni/ sbar ston don zhags/ lha btsun sngon mo/ bya bral 'khrul zhig chen po/ bla ma
'bri sgom pa man 'dra/ ! /yang / lo ras nas brgyud pa'i dug sngags yig 'bru drug cu rtsa bdun pa'i brgyud pa ni/ mon gyi rgyal po/ lo ras bzang ril gyi zhang rin po che/
'di'i bar gyi brgyud pa btsal dgos rgyu yin/ bzang yul mon pa mdong gi rnal 'byor pa/ des 'tshal rin po che grags/ des nor bu bde man 'dra/ ! /bde chen dri bral rigs lnga'i
bcud len phyi nang

gzhan gsum rim par bcing ba'i thabs kyi brgyud pa ni/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng / ra ga brag pa/ bkras dpal ba man 'dra/ yang na/ u rgyan pa/ mkhas btsun bsod nams 'od zer/ 'ba'
rwa ba/ 'bri sgom pa man 'dra/ yang / 'ching byed lcags brgyad kyi rim pa phye ba ste rtogs pa phyi ma'i brgyud pa ni/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng / ra ga brag pa/ bkras dpal ba
man 'dra/ yang / dngul chu bcud du blangs pa/ shig bsrung ba'i gdams pa/ rin po che'i rigs rnams thal bar btang ba'i man ngag slob dpon klu sgrub nas brgyud pa'i dngul
chu'i sbyar thabs/ yang 'dre dang sngags kyi bsrung ba'i zhal gdams/ yang dngul chu tshwas 'dul ba sogs kyi brgyud pa ni/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng sogs gong bzhin/ yang /sha
ba ri pa'i dngul chu skor gsum gyi brgyud pa'ang / sha ba ri pa'i bcud len skor dang 'dra/ 'di yan glegs bam gcig go /yang / dug sman/ sman nag gi zur 'debs/ dngul chu dkar
'dul dang bcas pa'i brgyud pa ni/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng / ra ga brag pa shAkya dhwa dza/ 'brom mdo ba bkras dpal ba man 'dra/ yang / bsnyen sgrub kyi sman gyi skor zhes
dpe tshan gcig gi nang na/ dug sman sbyor thabs sde gcig zla ba'i gtso bkru bya thabs/ sman nag gi gzhung yid bzhin nor bu le'u lnga pa/ bdud rtsi lnga'i bcud len rnams
bla ma rnam rgyal bas mdzad pa'i brgyud pa nye brgyud ni/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng / rnam rgyal ba/ nor bu ba man 'dra/ ring rgyud ni/ dhi ka ri pa/ dznyA
la dhi ri pa/ shrI tsantra/ bha tra bha ba/ pa ru pa/ u rgyan pa/ zla seng / rnam rgyal ba/ nor bu ba man 'dra/ dngul chu rab tu bsgrub pa'i bstan bcos slob dpon bha
li pas mdzad pa/ rgya gar gyi paNDi ta shrI na lendra dang / lo tsA ba

u rgyan rgyal pos bsgyur ba'i lung brgyud ni/ u rgyan pa/ zla ba seng ge rnam rgyal ba/ nor bu ba/ chos rje shes rab dpal ldan pa/ des bdag la'o//! /'jam dpal nag po'i rjes
gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje gdan pa/ ba ri ba/ rje btsun khu dbon lnga/ zhang dkon mchog dpal/ brag phug pa/ ye shes dpal/ blo bzang dkar mo/ dkon mchog thugs rje/ chos
rje pa/ des bdag la'o//! /chos rje na bza' brag phug pa/ chen po chos rin pa/ byang sems bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa/ chos rje 'di nyid las sgom rim thog mtha' bar gsum
yang thob/ de yan tshad bcod rgyud/! /chos rje rong po las brgyud pa'i shes phyin gyi khrid phran sogs 'ga' yang thob ste/ 'phral du bri ba ma grub pas lus so//! /bcud 'bum
gyi lung gi brgyud pa ni/ rdo rje rnal 'byor ma/ gro sa dge bshes/ gzhon nu blo gros/ chos rje pa/ des bdag la'o/ /'di'i dpe'i rnam grangs ni/ rtag tu ngu'i bcud len lo
rgyus dang bcas pa/ cong zhi'i bcud len/ mu zi'i bcud len/ dbang lag gi bcud len/ dam pa'i lugs kyi rtag tu ngu'i bcud len gnyis/ yang dbang lag gi bcud len gnyis/ klu
sgrub la 'jog pos phul ba'i tshe sgrub bcud len/ sbrang rtsi rtag tu ngu'i bcud len/ yang cong zhi'i bcud len 'dul thabs sogs dang bcas pa/ yang rdo'i bcud len gnyis/ yang
rdo'i las tshogs gegs sel dang bcas pa/rDzogs chen Teachingsyang / bla ma dam pa rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po de dag las/ gsang sngags rnying ma dam chos rdzogs pa
chen po'i skor thob pa la/ thog mar rgyud bcu bdun gyi lung gi rnam grangs ni/ sgra thal 'gyur gyi rgyud/ nor bu 'phra bkod kyi rgyud/ rdo rje sems dpa' snying gi me long
gi rgyud/ nyi zla kha sbyor gyi rgyud/ rin po che yi ge

med pa'i rgyud/ rin po che sgron ma 'bar ba'i rgyud/ ngo sprod rin po che spras pa'i rgyud/ kun tu bzang po'i klong drug pa'i rgyud/ bkra shis/ mdzes ldan chen mo'i rgyud/
rang byung yi ge chen po'i rgyud/ rig pa rang grol chen po'i rgyud/ rin po che spungs pa'i rgyud/ sku gdung 'bar ba rtags kyi rgyud/ mu tig phreng ba'i rgyud/ rdzogs pa rang
byung gi rgyud/ kun tu bzang po thugs kyi me long gi rgyud/ seng ge rtsal rdzogs kyi rgyud/ de dag gi bla ma brgyud pa ni/ chos sku kun tu bzang yab yum/ longs sku zhi
khro rab 'byams/ ston pa rdo rje sems dpa'/ sprul sku rdo rje 'chang chen/ gsang bdag phyag na rdo rje/ rig 'dzin dga' rab rdo rje/ gu ru 'jam dpal bshes gnyen/ mkhas mchog
shrI singha / rgyal ba dznyA na su tra/ paN chen bi ma la mi tra/ nyang ban ting 'dzin bzang po/ gnas brtan ldang ma lhun rgyal/ lce btsun seng ge dbang phyug sprul
sku rgyal ba zhang ston/ gu ru mkhas pa nyi 'bum/ chos bdag gu ru jo 'ber/ 'khrul zhig seng ge rgyal ba/ grub chen zla ba mun sel/ rig 'dzin ku ma rA dza/ rgyal sras dri
med 'od zer/ gu ru khyab gdal lhun grub/ sprul sku grags pa 'od zer/ paN chen shes rab dpal ldan/ des bdag la'o/ /de rnams kyi snying po man ngag la snying tig gnyis las/
bi ma la snying tig la yang / dang por smin par byed pa'i dbang la/ spros bcas/ spros med/ shin tu spros med/ rab tu spros med kyi dbang bzhi so sor thob nas/ grol byed
lam gyi rim pa nyams khrid du thob cing / de rjes yig cha ma lus pa'i lung thob pa'i rim pa ni/ thog mar kha byang nyi ma'i snying po thob nas/ de nas de nyid kyi lugs bzhin
dang / lo rgyus rin po che'i phreng ba/ spros bcas kyi dbang chog tshangs pa'i drwa ba spros med kyi dbang

chog rin po che'i drwa ba/ shin tu spros med kyi dbang chog pad ma'i drwa ba/ rab tu spros med kyi dbang chog 'od kyi drwa ba/ de'i cha lags du maNDal 'bul chog yid bzhin drwa
ba/'di kha byang la med/ dam tshig gi rim pa rnam grol rgya mtsho/ tshogs mchod kyi rim pa yid bzhin rgya mtsho/ bla ma'i rim pa dngos grub rgya mtsho ste rgya mtsho
skor gsum/ sngon 'gro sems sbyang bdun gyi don khrid/ dngos gzhi 'od gsal snying po'i don khrid/ khregs chod ye babs sor bzhag gi don khrid de don khrid skor gsum/ khregs
chod kyi rgyab yig nam mkha' dri med/ thod rgal gyi rgyab yig nyi zla gza' skar/ btags grol gyi rgyab yig yid bzhin lhun grub te rgyab yig skor gsum/ bde stong bdud rtsi'i
sprin phung rlung sbyor ye shes sprin phung rtog med nam mkha' sprin phung ste sprin phung skor gsum/ gzhi snang ye shes sgron ma/ dpe don gsal byed sgron ma/ nyams len
gnad kyi sgron ma ste sgron ma skor gsum gnad gsum chos nyid 'khor lo/ nyin mtshan 'od gsal 'khor lo/ yang zab ye shes 'khor lo ste 'khor lo skor gsum/ bdud rtsi ljon shing
sgron ma gsal byed/ ye shes dri med de gegs sel skor gsum/ bla ma yid bzhin nor bu/ yi dam yid bzhin nor bu/ mkha' 'gro yid bzhin nor bu ste nor bu skor gsum/ 'chi ltas
dran pa'i me long / 'chi blu dran pa'i me long / 'dir me long skor gsum zer yang gnyis las ma byung / ye shes rang snang / 'od gsal rang snang / nges don rang snang ste
snyan brgyud bskor gsum/ sngags kyi bdag mo'i/ rA hU la'i/ rdo rje legs pa'i ste sgrub thabs snying gi dum bu skor gsum mo/ /'di rnams ni rdzogs chen tshul blos mdzad
pa 'ba' zhig ste/ tho yig ma med pa des mdzad pa'i bka' rdzogs pa chen po'i bka' bsrungs gter

bdag rnams kyi bskang gso dngos grub 'byung ba'i gter yang thob nas/ de dag gi rgyab yig gi rim pa ni dam tshig rab 'byed slob dpon 'jam dpal bshes gnyen gyis mdzad pa/ 'khrid
kyi rgyab yig gnad 'gag bdun pa bi ma la mi tras mdzad pa/ gsang lam brgyud bu ngos sprod kyi lung yang zer/ chung rtags kyi yi ge gsang ba bi ma las mdzad pa/ rin po
che gser yig can/ po ti smug chung du'ang grags pa g.yu yig can/ de'i bu yig ste/ 'di na 'jam dpal bshes gnyen dang / bi ma la dang / dga' rab rdo rje dang / ye shes mdos
mdzad pa sogs mang du yod/ zangs yig can/ de'i rgyab yig 'phra yig can gyi dum bu gsum pa zhes pa dung yig can/ de'i rgyab yig bi ma las mdzad pa/ bstan pa bu gcig te de
thams cad kyi bla ma brgyud pa sngar bzhin no//! /de nas mkha' 'gro snying tig gi yang dbang rnams dang 'khrid rdzogs par zhus nas/ yig cha'i rim pa ni/ ye shes mtsho rgyal
nyid kyis dkar chag mdzad pa/ yang / gsang khyad 'phags gdams skor dang po la/ btags grol rgyud kyi ma bu brtan pa ni/ btags grol dang ni gcig shes kun grol dang / yang
/ ti'i rgyud dang sangs rgyas sras gcig dang //rang byung rgyud dang yongs rdzogs chen po'i rgyud/ /rgyud drug ma yin bu ni rnam pa drug /btags grol ti ka gsal byed don
snying dang / /kun grol ti ka gsal byed don me long / /yang ti'i ti ka gsal byed shes snying dang / /sras gcig ti ka gsal byed nor bu'i phreng / /rang byung ti ka gsal
byed dung spar khab/ /rtsal dbang ti ka rig pa'i sgron ma dang / /de ltar ma drug bu drug btags grol rgyud 'grel rdzogs/ /de yi phran la lo rgyus rtsal dbang dang / /rgyud

'das rjes gsum dang don khrid bcad pa ste/ /dum bu nyi shu gsum gyis btags grol ma bu tshang / /zhes dang / dbang dang lag len bdag gi ma bu ni/ /rigs lnga phyi nang gnyis
kyi sgrub pa dang / /spros bcas bum dbang gsum pa'i lag len dang / /dbang gsum sa bcad DA ki'i mngon rtogs dang / /dbang gi rgyab yig khyad par dbang lnga dang / /mchod 'bum

dang / /gsang dbang shes rab dbang gi lhan thabs dang / /DA ki'i srog tika spyi gnad bla rdo dang / /nor sgrub gter gyi bum pa bcu gsum ste/ /dum bu nyer gsum dag gis lag
len ma bu grub/ /ces dang / khrid kyi ma bu nyid kyi grangs brtan pa/ thod rgal lam khrid nor bu'i phreng ba dang / /de yi ti ka gsal byed sgron ma dang / /khrid rgyab lung
gi phreng ba ma gsum yin/ /de yi bu ni lag khrid rtags tshad do/ /ma gsum bu gnyis lnga yis khrid kyi lag len grub/ /ces dang / de dag rnams kyi rgyab chos bstan pa ni/

ltas lam khyer gsum/ /ma gnyis bu gsum dag gi bar do grub/ /ces dang / de thams cad kyi mthar/ de bas mang nyung byung na gdams pa 'chal/ /de yi phyir na gsang ba kha byang
gces/ /rgya rgya rgya/ ces dang / de nas yang / 'di'i cha lag gtum mo'i gdams pa dang / /rdo bcud bdud rtsi rdo yi bcud len gnyis/ lto gos zhen pa gcod phyir dgos pa yin/

po/ des bdag la'o//! /mgon po ber nag can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ ye shes mgon po/ slob dpon arNa/ mal gyo blo gros grags/ gnyal pa nyi ma 'bar/ gnyal pa jo sras/ 'gro
mgon ras chen/ spom brag pa/ karma dpag shi/ gnam thog pa/ gnam thog pa gzhon nu 'bum/ rang byung rdo rje/ mgon po rgyal mtshan/ rol pa'i rdo rje phyin chad gong dang
'dra/ ! /tsa ri'i zhing skyong seng gdong can gyi rjes gnang gi brgyud pa ni/ karma dpag shi/ gnyan ras sambha la kSha/ chos rje rang byung rdo rje/ rtogs ldan mgon rgyal
ba/ rol pa'i rdo rje/ mkha' spyod dbang po/ de bzhin gshegs pa/ sog dbon pa bka' bzhi ba rin chen bzang po/ mthong ba don ldan/ gu shrI dpal 'byor don grub/ chos rje nyid/
des bdag la'o// //@/ /bo dong ras chen pa/rje btsun rdo rje rnal 'byor mas/ /rjes bzung rnal 'byor pa yi mchog /dpe bral byin brlabs myur stsol ba/ /dpal 'byor bzang
po'i zhabs la 'dud//de lta bu'i bla ma nges par grub pa'i dbang phyug chen por gyur pa de las shangs pa'i zab chos rnams cha lag dang bcas pa rdzogs par yid ches pa'i gnas
su thob pa las/ dang por ni gu chos drug la yang thog mar smin byed kyi dbang la/ khog 'bubs kyi bka' gnyis dang / gzhung shing gi bka' bdun las/ dang po la rgyud sde lnga'i
dbang ni/ dbus su 'khor lo sdom pa/ shar du kye rdo rje/ lhor gsang ba 'dus pa/ nub tu rdo rje 'jigs byed/ byang du ma hA mA yA ste dkyil 'khor lnga bsdus par dbang
bzhi yongs su rdzogs pa dang / bde mchog gi dbang bzhi lus la bskur ba gnyis/ gzhung shing gi bka'

bdun la spyi'i bka' sgyu lus kyi dbang mo che dang / sgos kyi bka' thabs lam/ sgyu lus/ rmi lam/ 'od gsal/ 'pho ba/ bar do rnams kyi bka' so sor thob cing / so so'i grol lam

pa/ skyer rgang pa/ sangs rgyas gnyan ston pa/ sangs rgyas ston pa/ mkhas grub shangs ston rnams kyi rnam par thar pa ste/ brgyud pa rin chen sna bdun zhes grags pa lta
na/ ne gu ma'i rnam thar khyung po'i rnam thar gyi 'go na yod pa dang bcas pa'o/ /de nas rgyud sde lnga'i dkyil 'khor gyi cho ga de'i lam dus kyi cho ga rgyud sde lnga'i
mngon rtogs bsdus pa/ bde mchog lha lnga'i mchod 'phreng / bde mchog gi dbang bzhi lus la bskur ba'i cho ga ne gu chos drug gi gzhung ngam sgyu lus kyi dbang mo che/ chos
